本章學習目標

  • 理解 Single-Use System (SUS) 供應商、材料與元件確認的風險導向與科學導向方法
  • 掌握 SUS 使用所涉及的病患、製程與操作人員風險分類框架
  • 了解 SUS 組裝環境要求與供應商稽核的關鍵要素
  • 學習替代供應商確認、互換性評估與供應商品質文件的運用
  • 深入理解 Extractables and Leachables (E&L) 的定義、評估方法與對產品品質及病患安全的影響

5.0/5.1 Qualification and Verification — Introduction

原文內容 Original Text

5.0 Qualification and Verification of Suppliers, Materials, Components, and Completed Assemblies

5.1 Introduction

The qualification and verification of suppliers, materials, components, and completed assemblies require attention to several factors. It is important to use a risk-based and science-based approach to qualify both materials and completed assemblies for SUSs in pharmaceutical development and manufacture (18). The assessment of risk must be based on the complexity of the system and its intended use (e.g., product contact versus non-product contact, upstream versus downstream use, short-term contact versus long-term storage). See PDA's Technical Report No. 54 on Quality Risk Management for more information (7). In addition, scientific principles must be applied to 1) identify and monitor extractable materials from films and other components; 2) investigate potential interactions with product CQAs or significant process parameters like cell culture media; and 3) assess the effects of assembly processes such as welding, fusing, mechanical stress, and sterilization (e.g., gamma irradiation) on the materials during manufacturing. In assessing the suitability of the SUS with respect to potential leachables in the final product, extractables may be considered as potential in-process leachables. Finally, the design and functional integrity of the completed SUS must be verified and maintained by appropriately trained end users via suitable processes for construction, packaging, shipping, and deployment.

The supplier of the SUS must provide sufficient data to qualify the materials and components used to assemble the final SUS. In this regard, the end user may use the documents from the supplier to meet most of the verification criteria required to make sure that the SUS is fit for the intended application and purpose. This requires a thorough qualification of the supplier by the end user to ascertain an acceptable supplier quality system, documentation, and an appropriate level of technical capability that extends all the way to the original sources of materials to the supplier. In addition, the suppliers must be able to provide documented evidence of performance claims for off-the-shelf component designs for the SUS. A supplier quality agreement must underpin any custom designs that the end user may need from the supplier.

The first step in a science- and risk-based approach is to identify and assess the risks associated with using an SUS. The end user must identify that the SUS supplier's approach to the design and selection of materials of construction includes components and materials such as:

  • Filters
  • Sensors
  • Polymers
  • Lubricants
  • Slip agents

Supplier quality, manufacturing and analytical capabilities should also be evaluated. The end user must fully qualify and audit a number of potential suppliers before embarking on extensive studies of specific materials because it is preferable to have more than one supplier for the SUS.

It is important for the end user to have access to controlled documentation of the qualification studies conducted on the materials and components of the assembled SUS. Such documentation may include:

  • Batch numbers traceable to the raw materials
  • Product shelf life
  • Certificate of quality
  • Certificate of integrity
  • Endotoxin certification (to required and specific endotoxin level)
  • Animal-free certification
  • Sterilization certification (if sterility is claimed)

A robust change control communication and assessment process between the end user and the supplier (including sub-suppliers) must be established to monitor any changes in processing conditions, equipment, analytical methods, manufacturing site, resins, films, additives, and more. If the supplier does not have an appropriate assessment process in place, the end user may have to perform independent testing. After performing material and component qualification of the assembled products, a functional verification of the SUS should be performed according to the following:

  • Risk assessment — To confirm that the assembled products are fit for purpose
  • Process verification and validation — To confirm that the completed SUS functions within process constraints, including repetitive use or extended storage (if required)
  • Safety — To make sure that the SUS conforms to safety requirements as a pressure vessel (especially for larger volumes) or for containment in the event of rupture or leak

If the SUS assembly includes SU sensors, calibration and additional verification documentation must be supplied.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Risk-based and Science-based Approach (風險導向與科學導向方法)：這是整個 SUS 確認流程的核心原則。不是所有 SUS 都需要相同程度的測試 — 風險越高的應用（例如長期儲存藥物原料藥），確認的深度與廣度就越大。科學導向則強調以數據驅動決策，而非單純依循慣例。

Supplier Quality Agreement (供應商品質協議)：這是終端使用者與 SUS 供應商之間的正式契約，規範品質期望、變更控制通知義務、稽核權利等。對於客製化設計尤其重要。

Change Control (變更管控)：SUS 的供應鏈涉及多層次的供應商（樹脂廠、薄膜廠、組裝廠），任何一層的變更（如更換添加劑或製造廠址）都可能影響最終產品品質。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像你經營一家高級餐廳，決定從陶瓷餐具（傳統不鏽鋼設備）改用高品質免洗餐具（SUS）。你不能隨便在大賣場買塑膠盤子就開始用 — 你需要確認供應商的食品安全認證、材料成分、耐溫性能，還要確保供應商若更換原料配方時會通知你。這就像 SUS 的確認流程：從原料樹脂到最終組裝，每一環都需要被驗證。

重點提示 Key Notes

確認文件清單是稽核的基礎：批號追溯、保質期、品質證書、完整性證書、內毒素認證、無動物源認證、滅菌認證 — 這些文件不僅是合規要求，更是製程出問題時追根溯源的關鍵工具。

功能驗證三要素：風險評估（確認適用性）、製程驗證與確效（確認功能性）、安全性（確認壓力容器合規）。這三層驗證缺一不可。

決策層級 Decision Hierarchy

1. 病患安全 Patient Safety
▼
2. 產品 CQAs
▼
3. 商業與供應鏈彈性

在 SUS 確認中，所有決策都必須以病患安全為最高優先。即使供應鏈成本壓力很大，也不能犧牲確認的完整性。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 TR66 強調必須確認到「原始材料來源」(original sources of materials)？如果只稽核最終組裝商會有什麼風險？
  2. 如果一個 SUS 供應商沒有適當的變更評估流程，終端使用者應該採取什麼措施？這對 CDMO 的營運成本有什麼影響？
  3. 列舉三種情境，說明同一類 SUS 在不同應用中可能需要不同深度的確認測試。

5.2 Risks Associated with Using Single-Use Systems

原文內容 Original Text

The risks associated with the use of SUSs include that to the patient, the process, and operators. The risk to the process may occur as a result of process failure, but it rarely affects patients because of process discontinuation. Normal safety precautions for handling large volumes of liquids, which may also be hazardous, must be maintained. The main focus of this discussion is the risk to the patient. Begin risk assessment by considering the potential for the SUS to interact with product or process fluids. Some of the important parameters are point of use, duration of contact, process conditions (e.g., temperature, presence of solvents, and the ratio of surface area to volume). The greatest risk is associated with long-term (>30 days) storage containers of certain drug products (19). The degree of risk is different for upstream applications because of the ability to use further processing steps to remove modified products or leached compounds and the dilutive effect of multiple filtration and washing steps. Ishikawa (fishbone) diagrams can be used to map the process and then identify and characterize potential areas of concern (Figure 5.2-1).

Figure 5.2-1: Example of an Ishikawa (Fishbone) Diagram for Determining Risk Sources

Table 5.2-1 identifies the risk complexities of SUSs.

Table 5.2-1: Risk Complexities of SUS Items and Applications
System Complexity →
Impact to Process ↓		 Low Moderate High
Low Buffer/Storage UF*/DF†/Concentration Clarification/Recovery
Moderate Transport/Shipping Connectors/Mixing/Medium Storage Cell Culture/Fermentation
High Freeze/Thaw Purification/Product Storage Fill and Finish

*UF – ultrafiltration   †DF – diafiltration

For assembly error or individual component failure, complex systems with multiple valves, manifolds, and sensors may present more risks than simple systems (horizontal axis). Applications that are more demanding or close to the final step may pose higher risks (vertical axis). Condensates may get back to the process if fluid pathways are not designed properly. In order of increasing risk are the following components:

1. Nonfluid contact systems

  • Vent tubing and filter assemblies
  • Samples and sampling systems for repetitive use

Sampling bags are considered a separate category, as the contained product is removed from the process; however, the potential for interactions with bags to interfere with the outcome of assays must be determined.

2. Fluid contact systems

  • Short-term contact, simple components (e.g., bags for cleaning materials, buffer storage and concentrates, antifoam, additives, and media)

Mixing systems have additional requirements for establishing functional performance and are available in a range of designs (refer to Section 4.8.3):

  • Bottom and top mixing
  • Rocking mixing
  • Cleaning, flushing, and draining
  • Long-term storage (storage, holding, and delivery systems with impact on temperature, moisture loss, and gas adsorption)

3. Complex systems

  • Bioreactors, including instrumentation (pH, temperature, pressure, conductivity, gases, nutrients with impact on mixing, cell viability, cell integrity, adhesion, and shear)
  • Predispensed buffer or media additives (concentrates as well as commercial and proprietary blends of media)

4. Product contact and storage systems

  • Tubing, filters, valves, connectors, and manifolds
  • Process intermediate storage containers
  • Bulk drug-substance storage containers
  • Shipping containers
  • Disposable filling needles

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

三類風險對象：SUS 使用的風險可分為對病患（最關鍵）、對製程（導致批次失敗）、對操作人員（安全危害）。TR66 特別聚焦於病患風險。

風險評估的關鍵參數：

  • 使用位置 (Point of use)：上游 vs 下游，離最終產品越近風險越高
  • 接觸時間 (Duration of contact)：>30天的長期儲存風險最大
  • 製程條件：溫度、溶劑存在、表面積/體積比

Ishikawa Diagram (魚骨圖)：一種品質管理工具，用於系統性地識別造成問題的所有可能原因，將原因分類為人、機、料、法、環等大類別。

圖表解讀 Table Analysis

Table 5.2-1 解讀：這是一個 3x3 風險矩陣，橫軸為系統複雜度，縱軸為對製程的影響。右下角的 Fill and Finish（充填與完成）同時具有最高的系統複雜度和最高的製程影響 — 這是風險最高的應用場景。

值得注意的是，Freeze/Thaw（冷凍/解凍）雖然系統複雜度低，但對製程影響高，因為它直接涉及產品品質（蛋白質凝聚、容器完整性等）。

比喻說明 Analogy

風險分級就像建築安全等級：臨時工棚（非接觸系統）的安全要求最低，住宅（流體接觸系統）中等，醫院和核電廠（產品接觸與儲存系統）的安全標準最嚴格。越接近「最終使用者」（病患）的環節，品質要求就越高。

重點提示 Key Notes

上游 vs 下游風險差異：上游應用（如細胞培養）的風險相對較低，因為後續還有多道純化、過濾和清洗步驟可以去除或稀釋 leachables。但下游應用（如藥物原料藥儲存）沒有後續的純化機會，風險最高。

四級風險分類（由低到高）：

  1. 非流體接觸系統 — 排氣管路、取樣系統
  2. 流體接觸系統 — 緩衝液袋、培養基袋
  3. 複雜系統 — 生物反應器、預配培養基
  4. 產品接觸與儲存系統 — 管路、閥門、原料藥儲存容器

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在 Table 5.2-1 中，為什麼 Purification/Product Storage 被歸類為「中等複雜度 + 高影響」而非「高複雜度 + 高影響」？
  2. 一個 CDMO 同時為客戶生產上游細胞培養和下游純化步驟，在 SUS 確認策略上應該如何區分這兩種應用？

5.3 Single-Use System Assembly

原文內容 Original Text

SUSs include fittings, tubing, filters, connectors, bag material (film), and outer packaging. SU components are normally received and stored in areas with minimal environmental control. It is critical for the components to remain in their sealed packaging, and they should be handled with gloves to avoid contamination. Transport into the assembly room must follow standard clean-room practices. All the external packaging of the SU components should be wiped with a suitable antimicrobial or cleansing agent before moving them into the assembly room. The assembly rooms are typically ISO 7 or 8 with a combination of particle and microbial sampling. It is important to design manufacturing suites with HEPA-filtered air, low returns, smooth surfaces, and airlocks for entry and exit. Avoid introducing any sharp edges or corners into the assembly room because they may perforate the SUS bags. Personnel must be trained and wear appropriate clothing for an ISO 7 operation and the assembly room must be cleaned regularly. Where SUSs are preassembled, the supplier takes these steps.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SUS 組裝環境要求：SUS 元件通常在環境控制要求較低的區域接收與存放，但組裝必須在 ISO 7 或 ISO 8 等級的潔淨室中進行。這與傳統不鏽鋼設備的製造環境（通常為一般工廠環境）有顯著不同。

關鍵控制措施：密封包裝保持完整、戴手套操作、外包裝消毒擦拭、HEPA 過濾空氣、人員培訓與著裝、避免尖銳物品。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 組裝就像在手術室中組裝無菌器材 — 你不能在走廊上打開無菌包裝。即使元件本身已經包裝好了，組裝的環境也必須達到一定的潔淨度，因為組裝過程中的任何污染都可能被密封在最終的系統裡。特別提到「避免尖銳邊角」就像手術室不允許有可能刺破手術手套的物品一樣。

重點提示 Key Notes

CDMO 實務考量：如果 CDMO 自行組裝 SUS，就必須維護符合 ISO 7/8 標準的專用組裝室，包括環境監測計畫（粒子計數 + 微生物取樣）。若選擇由供應商預組裝 (preassembled)，則這些責任轉移給供應商 — 但稽核責任仍在 CDMO 身上。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 SUS 元件可以在「最小環境控制」區域存放，但組裝必須在 ISO 7/8 潔淨室？這兩者的風險差異是什麼？
  2. 如果你是 CDMO 的品質主管，你會選擇自行組裝 SUS 還是採購預組裝系統？各有什麼優缺點？

5.4 Supplier Qualification of Single-Use Systems

原文內容 Original Text

Since a typical SUS installation requires the acquisition of several components from various external suppliers, it is important for the end user to qualify suppliers to ensure that they can deliver SU components that meet or exceed regulatory and customer expectations.

5.4.1 Supplier Audits and Technical Diligence

It is important to audit the supplier's quality systems as part of the supplier qualification process to ensure delivery of consistent SU components to the end user. An understanding of the supplier's capabilities may lead to a better understanding of end-user expectations and can help identify any gaps in the capabilities of the supplier. Therefore, the auditing step must encompass manufacturing and technical aspects, and both parties must agree on corrective actions as appropriate. Microbiological control measures for SUSs must be evaluated as part of a supplier audit.

The auditor should review the procedure and records for quarterly dose audits where the SUS is subjected to gamma-irradiation sterilization.

Standard auditing practices, extending to a review of quality systems and complaint handling, should be followed. Unique to SUSs for inclusion in audits would be the supplier's definition of change and how the change-control process functions, including customer notification. The specific particulate control and reduction schemes in place at the supplier should also be evaluated.

Many SUS suppliers may either be ISO 9001 or medical device manufacturers under FDA and ISO registration. ISO 9001 registration means a company operates in a quality management framework that has been audited by a registrar and confirmed as adhering to ISO 9001 guidelines (20). The manufacturing facilities of registered medical devices are subject to inspection and follow 21 CFR Part 820 (cGMPs for Medical Devices) and ISO 13485 (21,22). SUSs, including bulk drug containers, are considered process equipment rather than medical devices; therefore, the manufacturing facilities of SUS suppliers are not subject to regulatory registration or inspection. Although SUS manufacturers tend to design their quality systems along GMP guidelines, the auditor should not expect these systems to adhere strictly to cGMPs for drug or medical device manufacturing (21,23). ISO 9001 is considered a minimum requirement.

Pertinent factors for a technical diligence assessment and an interpretation of its implementation over the clinical development lifecycle are reviewed in greater detail in Section 7.7.3.

5.4.2 Supplier Quality Agreements and Responsibilities

The purpose of a supplier quality agreement is to set quality expectations, identify and develop a mutual understanding of pertinent regulations and guidance documents, and provide advice on managing quality concerns such as audits, complaints, and change control. Change control can be a complex process for an SUS because of the diverse number of suppliers (e.g., compounders, film producers, and bag assemblers) and materials (e.g., resins and additives) involved in the supply chain. The supplier must provide full transparency on the full supply chain of the SUS and guarantee quality oversight of the supply chain. The supplier must have a robust supply chain, which may require improvements, which can be developed with the support of the customer in a partnership mind-set. The extent to which the primary supplier manages the overall supply chain should be assessed, and if necessary, audit and technical diligence activities should be extended to the original supplier of materials and components. It is important to establish a cordial working relationship between the end user and supplier because an SUS supplier will inevitably become an extended part of the end user's manufacturing and quality systems.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Supplier Qualification (供應商確認)：這不只是簡單的「核准供應商清單」管理。對 SUS 供應商的確認需要深入了解其品質體系、製造能力、技術專業度，以及最重要的 — 變更管控流程。

ISO 9001 vs ISO 13485 vs cGMP：

  • ISO 9001：通用品質管理體系標準，是 SUS 供應商的最低要求
  • ISO 13485：醫療器材品質管理體系標準
  • 21 CFR Part 820：FDA 醫療器材 cGMP 法規

重要區分：SUS 被視為製程設備而非醫療器材，因此其製造設施不受法規註冊或查廠的約束。這意味著終端使用者的稽核責任更重。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 供應商的角色就像餐廳的食材供應商 — 他們不受「餐飲業衛生法規」直接管轄（SUS 不是醫療器材），但你的餐廳（藥廠）出了食安問題，最終責任還是在你身上。所以你必須主動去稽核你的食材供應商的衛生管理、冷鏈控制、變更通知機制等，而不能只依賴他們的「自我聲明」。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 稽核的獨特重點：

  • 變更定義與通知：供應商如何定義「變更」？多小的改變需要通知客戶？這在 SUS 中至關重要，因為即使微小的樹脂配方變更也可能改變 E&L profile
  • 微粒控制：SUS 中的微粒是長期以來的產業痛點，必須評估供應商的微粒控制與減少方案
  • 伽馬射線滅菌劑量稽核：季度劑量稽核記錄是確認滅菌有效性的關鍵

合作夥伴心態 (Partnership Mindset)：TR66 特別強調 SUS 供應商將「不可避免地成為終端使用者製造和品質體系的延伸」。這不是一般的買賣關係，而是深度合作關係。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 場景：假設你的 CDMO 同時服務 5 個客戶，每個客戶使用不同的 SUS 配置。你不可能為每個客戶維護完全獨立的供應商確認體系。實務上，你需要建立一個「平台化」的供應商確認框架 — 先確認核心供應商（薄膜、管路、連接器等），再根據個別客戶的產品風險等級決定是否需要額外的專案級確認。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 SUS 被歸類為「製程設備」而非「醫療器材」？這個分類對終端使用者有什麼實際影響？
  2. 在供應商品質協議中，「變更控制」條款應該涵蓋哪些具體項目？請至少列出五項。
  3. 如果一個 SUS 供應商只有 ISO 9001 認證而沒有 ISO 13485，這是否足夠？為什麼 TR66 認為 ISO 9001 是最低要求？

5.5 Qualification of Alternative Suppliers

原文內容 Original Text

The use of SUS permits considerable flexibility in the choice of materials, designs, and suppliers. This flexibility can be used to minimize risk by ensuring that multiple configurations are viable options for any given requirement. There are multiple combinations of films, bag designs, tubing, filters, connectors, and so on, that are capable of delivering or receiving a specified volume of process fluids to the required standard. Therefore, it is advisable for the end user to qualify an alternative supplier as part of the SUS risk management system (7). Risk- and science-based assessment must be used to determine the level of testing and validation required. In a case involving minimal risk, it may be sufficient to treat an SUS from a secondary supplier as representative of the same class of system or material from the primary supplier. The data generated for the original SUS can be used and compared to that from the secondary supplier. With higher-risk cases (e.g., bioreactor bags or product storage), the secondary supplier's component must be subjected to the same comprehensive qualification process as that of the primary supplier. Note that different suppliers may adopt different approaches to tackle a particular issue and still remain within the bounds of an acceptable supplier quality system. For instance, supplier A may test systems for bioburden from every lot whereas supplier B may test representative samples from different lots as proof of an overall bioburden management system. Both approaches may be acceptable and should be reflected in the user specifications (Table 5.5.2-1). An industry effort to standardize SUS testing methods would improve end users' ability to compare alternative SUS suppliers and adequately assess testing differences between suppliers.

5.5.1 Qualification of Alternative Sources

End users typically have two options when it comes to alternative sources: 1) the same SUS supplier with alternative sources of raw materials, or 2) an alternative SUS supplier. Regardless of the choice, the qualification of an alternative source should be part of the drug substance manufacturer's risk-management system. The user should qualify the alternative supplier or raw material source in the same thorough way as the primary supplier or source.

With each option, the risk- and science-based assessment will continue to determine the level of testing and validation required.

The issues under consideration differ somewhat for each option. Suppliers may qualify alternate raw-material sources as part of their risk mitigation strategy at the level of the resins, additives, or the film itself (if sourced separately). For applications with low potential for process or product impact, it might be sufficient to review the data from the supplier's qualification. For applications with high potential for impact, the user may need to consider additional testing (e.g. cytotoxicity, stability). For films sourced separately, differences in formulations and manufacturing processes may occur, and the physiochemical properties and extractable profile of the alternate film can be quite different from the original. Such differences, however, should not be the deciding factor for the suitability of this alternative material for the SUS. The suitability of the alternative material should be determined by the end user depending on the intended use of the SUS.

For an alternative supplier, data generated for the original material can be used and compared to the data of the alternative supplier source. In high-risk cases (e.g., bioreactor bags or storage of bulk drug substance), the second supplier's component has to be treated as a specific instance, and full-scale qualification is required.

5.5.2 Interchangeability

It is important for end users to qualify alternative sources of films to safeguard against supply disruptions and possible shortages. In some situations this may be a minimal risk (e.g., sampling bag used for monitoring cell growth or nutrient conditions), so a comparison of extractables and leachables data from different suppliers may be acceptable; other situations may be more demanding (e.g., storage of bulk drug substance). SUS interchangeability can be considered if functionally equivalent substitution provides a contingency or process alternative while ensuring process performance and product quality. When considering SUS interchangeability, it is important to assess the component's intended function, anticipated processing conditions, and fitness for use (Table 5.5.2-1). In every case, the approach taken should be supported by a sound risk- and science-based assessment with appropriate evaluation and performance verification for the type of substitution desired.

For example, a bag or assembly used simply as a container for process fluids with no product contact has limited critical attributes—the bag should not leak and there should be an acceptable leachables profile. If the assembly has the additional function of acting as a mixer, the design would need to be assessed for functional performance, in this case minimum mixing conditions (time, speed, and so forth, depending on the mechanism) to achieve homogeneity. Once the design is qualified, this would not need to be established for every lot. For an in-process product container potential interaction with the product would need to be examined and deemed appropriate for the conditions (e.g., liquid, frozen, storage time). The presence of particulates may also need to be assessed, depending on where the alternative component is used in the process. For a complex assembly such as a bioreactor, a full-scale assessment should be conducted on the design for performance parameters and attributes (mixing, pH control, sparging, temperature control, cell growth, viability, titer/yield, etc.). The potential impact of differences in growth conditions on product quality should be included.

Table 5.5.2-1: Component Interchangeability Evaluation
Change Description Risk Assessment Focus* Performance Verification
Like-for-like Identical components, dimensions, and materials of construction made by more than one supplier for the same processing conditions 1, 2 Design and user specification monitored through change control
Functionally equivalent Combinations of materials with the same performance but different material suppliers (e.g., bag/filter/tubing) or processing conditions 1, 2, 3, 4, 6 Monitor performance attributes, leachables, and CQAs
Process or functional modification or improvement Similar function or performance with different design and materials of construction and may require some process or equipment modification for operation (e.g., virus filter housing changed) 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6 Monitor performance attributes, leachables, and CQAs in a scaled-down development study

*Risk Assessment Focus Descriptions:

  1. Design, dimension, performance, and materials claims of the proposed substitute (form, fit, and function)
  2. Materials of construction and process contact fluid compatibility, contact area, and time
  3. Availability and extent of supplier biosafety (USP <87> and/or <88>, as appropriate for the application) and extractables data (24,25)
  4. Suitability of supplier extractables data to bracket process fluid and conditions
  5. Application and potential for subsequent leachable removal or dilution
  6. Product impact assessment

When considering interchangeability, in most cases other than like-for-like, the end user will need to do some level of operational or extractable/leachable testing to verify fitness for use. Different dimensions or even top or bottom mixing can have product impact. As discussed in Section 5, Business Drivers for the Adoption of Single-use Systems, the cost of quality can be defined as "any cost that would not have been expended if quality were perfect." The additional end-user operational testing of SUS and related quality control activities to ensure process comparability for SU interchangeability could be included in the cost of quality and should then be considered in the overall SUS implementation costs. After all, if a supplier had perfect interchangeability, this end-user cost would be zero.

5.5.3 Using Supplier Quality Documentation

The end user may employ the supplier documentation as part of the SUS document verification process so long as the end user has audited the supplier and collected the requisite evidence of an acceptable supplier quality system, technical capability, and application of Good Engineering Practices (GEP) guidelines (Table 5.5.3-1) (18). If there is not strict adherence to GEP, then there should be assurance that documentation is accurate and suitable to meet the purpose of verification.

Table 5.5.3-1: Example Supplier Testing and Reference Standards
Vendor A Vendor B Vendor C
Compendial USP <87>, <88> USP <88> USP <87>, <88>
Biocompatibility Testing ISO 10993-4, EP 5.2.8 ISO 10993-4, EP 5.2.8 ISO 10993-4, EP 5.2.8
Extractables Testing USP <661>, 11 solvents, 90 days at 40°C, "Pass" no values EP 3.1.5, USP <661>, "Pass" no values Nothing unless the User Contracts

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Alternative Supplier (替代供應商)：SUS 供應鏈的一大風險是單一來源依賴。TR66 明確建議確認替代供應商作為風險管理的一部分。替代來源有兩種選擇：

  • 同一供應商 + 替代原料來源：風險較低，但仍需評估 E&L profile 差異
  • 完全替代供應商：風險較高，高風險應用需要完整的確認流程

Interchangeability (互換性)：三個層級的替代 —

  • Like-for-like (同等替換)：相同材料、尺寸，不同供應商 → 最簡單的確認
  • Functionally equivalent (功能等效)：不同材料但相同性能 → 需要監測 CQAs
  • Process modification (製程修改)：不同設計和材料 → 需要縮小規模開發研究

比喻說明 Analogy

互換性就像汽車零件的替換策略：

  • Like-for-like：原廠輪胎用另一家同規格原廠輪胎替換 — 只需確認尺寸和性能規格
  • Functionally equivalent：換成不同品牌但同規格的副廠輪胎 — 需要測試抓地力、耐磨性等性能
  • Process modification：從普通輪胎換成雪地輪胎 — 需要重新評估整車操控性能

越往下，需要的測試和驗證越多，成本也越高。

圖表解讀 Table Analysis

Table 5.5.2-1 解讀：這張表是互換性評估的核心框架。注意風險評估焦點的編號：

  • Like-for-like 只需要 1、2（設計規格 + 材料相容性）
  • Functionally equivalent 增加了 3、4、6（生物安全 + E&L + 產品影響）
  • Process modification 再增加 5（後續 leachable 去除可能性）

Table 5.5.3-1 啟示：三家供應商的測試範圍差異很大！Vendor C 甚至「除非客戶要求，否則不做 E&L 測試」。這凸顯了供應商之間缺乏標準化的現實，也說明為什麼終端使用者的稽核如此重要。

重點提示 Key Notes

Cost of Quality (品質成本)：TR66 提出一個重要觀點 — 互換性測試的成本應該納入 SUS 總實施成本中。如果供應商能做到完美的互換性（理想情況），這個成本就是零。現實中，終端使用者必須投入額外的測試資源來驗證替代供應商的適用性。

GEP (Good Engineering Practices)：良好工程實務是利用供應商文件進行驗證的前提條件。如果供應商未嚴格遵循 GEP，終端使用者就需要額外確認文件的準確性和適用性。

實務應用 Practical Application

供應鏈韌性場景：2020 年 COVID-19 疫情期間，許多 CDMO 面臨 SUS 供應短缺。那些事先確認了替代供應商的企業能夠快速切換供應源，維持生產不中斷。沒有替代供應商的企業則面臨數週甚至數月的停產。這個案例生動地說明了為什麼 TR66 如此強調替代供應商確認的重要性。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在 Table 5.5.2-1 中，為什麼 like-for-like 替換不需要風險評估焦點 3（生物安全數據）？
  2. 如果一個 CDMO 需要為生物反應器袋確認替代供應商，應該採用哪個層級的互換性評估？需要做哪些具體測試？
  3. Table 5.5.3-1 顯示供應商之間的測試差異很大。作為終端使用者，你會如何利用這張表來強化你的供應商管理策略？

5.6 Extractables and Leachables (E&L)

原文內容 Original Text

Extractables may be defined as chemical entities that can be extracted from the components of a material by exertion of an exaggerated force (e.g., organic solvent, extreme temperature, ionic strength, pH, contact time). Leachables may be defined as chemical entities that can migrate from product-contact or non-product-contact surfaces into a process stream. Leachables may also include chemical entities that can migrate from contact surfaces into the bulk drug substance or final product under specified conditions of production, storage, and use. While leachables are considered a subset of extractables, they can also be derived from product-contact or non-product-contact materials, under typical process conditions and detected in final dosage. The evaluation of extractables is an essential step in the accurate prediction of leachables and in the selection of a suitable SUS dedicated to the manufacture of a given product. When chemical substances are identified that could be cleared or sufficiently diluted by downstream processes so as to be undetected, these can be termed as in-process leachables for the final dosage and may need to be accounted for during risk assessment. Refer to Table 4.8-1 for a summary of common materials of construction and comments regarding their respective E&L properties.

Drug manufacturers are encouraged to perform a risk-assessment analysis as part of an E&L evaluation within the overall context of enhancing process performance and product safety and efficacy. The accumulation of extractables and leachables in a process fluid is governed by thermodynamic (i.e., the extent to which the materials would migrate) and kinetic (i.e., the rate at which materials would migrate) factors, as well as the amount of time during which such migration would occur. Higher temperatures increase the migration rate of leachables from the bulk of the plastic to the surface in contact with the process stream or formulation. The user can determine the worst-case extent of the extractables by determining the highest temperature at which extractions cease and the entire additive has been removed from the plastic. E&L risk factors can be generally categorized as risk to the patient and risk to the process. In evaluating risks, an extractable or leachable and the level at which it appears will need to be evaluated for impact on process and product quality and for patient safety. The following risk factors may be considered:

  • Proximity of the process steps undergoing a change to the final product
  • Storage and processing conditions (e.g., duration of exposure, temperature, pressure, pH extremes, buffer extraction propensity)
  • The type of process fluid (e.g., purification buffer versus formulated drug substance, presence of solubilizing agents)
  • Construction materials (e.g., PVC containers, bags, and tubing are prone to leaching diethylhexyl phthalate, which has adverse effects on the liver, testis, mammary, nerve, immune system, blood, and fatty tissue) (26,27).
  • Potential adverse effects, including synergistic and additive affects
  • Drug dose, mode, and frequency of administration
  • Therapeutic necessity of the drug (included in drug dose, mode, and frequency)

The presence of leachables during any stage of the production process or storage may pose a safety risk due to their potential to cause toxicity, carcinogenicity, immunogenicity, and/or endocrine dysregulation (28,29). In addition, these substances may adversely impact the physicochemical characteristics (e.g., via aggregation, oxidation, degradation, and formation of particulates) of the final protein product. It has been demonstrated that leachables have adverse effects on cell growth and viability (30). Lastly, the potential for leachables to impact quality control tests should be considered. For these reasons, proper selection and handling of an SUS that supports the production and processing of safe and efficacious therapeutic biologic products is of paramount importance.

Potential sources of extractables and leachables include SU materials used in manufacturing, packaging, storage, filtration, and transfer systems. These include but are not limited to SU bioreactors, bags for intermediate and long-term storage, containers, filters, transfer tubing, valves, fittings, housings, and so on. Extractables and leachables are chemically diverse compounds that may include but are not limited to phthalates (e.g., plasticizers), organic acids, hydrocarbons, cyclic esters derived from urethane adhesives, antioxidants, residual solvents, antistatic and cleaning agents, as well as trace metals and degradation products from irradiation.

5.6.1 Material and Supplier Qualification

It is important for end users to qualify alternative sources of films to safeguard against supply disruptions and possible shortages. There will be situations where this may be a minimal risk (e.g., bags used for sampling), so a comparison of extractables data from different suppliers may be acceptable; other situations may be more demanding (e.g., storage of bulk drug substance). In every case, the approach taken should be supported by a sound risk- and science-based assessment.

Detection, characterization, identification, and quantitation of leachables may present analytical challenges, since these substances represent diverse chemical classes of organic and/or inorganic compounds that coexist in complex mixtures in trace amounts (31). Therefore, well-designed extractables studies are important to provide an analytical road map and to identify early warning signs regarding leachables released during upstream or downstream operations or in storage. Emerging analytical technologies with appropriate sensitivity and specificity may be considered in addition to the currently available methods during the design of such studies. If an extractable may have an adverse effect on the physicochemical or biological properties of a protein, performing characterization studies in which the extractable is spiked into the product may be of value in assessing the potential risk to product quality.

In order to isolate chemicals from plastic components, the study of extractables begins with the selection of a suitable exaggerated condition that is not stipulated for the normal manufacture, storage, or use of the SUS. It is recommended that the extraction studies be performed with material components using the exaggerated conditions with regards to pH, ionic strength, contact time, temperature, surface area–to–volume ratio, and, if applicable, organic solvents of varying polarity and surfactant properties as the extraction media. If the material component in question is not compatible with organic solvents, aqueous media may be used. If a prerinse step is used in routine manufacturing and use of material component, it should be included in the design of the leachables studies but not in the extractables studies because the latter are intended to represent a worst-case situation. Additional pretreatment of plastics such as gamma irradiation and steam treatment can also impact the E&L profile.

A representative sample of process fluid (e.g., cell culture media and buffer) can be used as the extraction media in addition to others listed above for accurate prediction of extractables. If a representative process fluid cannot be obtained (e.g., due to interference with the analytical method), a similar solution to the original may be an acceptable alternative. The extraction study may be performed using a soaking or a recycling method for a specific contact time, under accelerated temperature conditions and preselected surface area–to–volume ratio. USP chapters <661> and <381> contain recommendations for extraction conditions with regards to surface area–to–volume ratio, temperature, and time of extraction (32,33). The USP <661> monograph also includes general analytical testing for the content of nonvolatile residue, residue on ignition, buffering capacity, and heavy metals. However, because such methods are not equipped to identify specific contaminants, their scope and applicability may not be sufficient in every instance. Several industry organizations, such as BioPhorum Operators Group (BPOG) and the Bio-Process Systems Alliance (BPSA), have developed standardized testing approaches. Please see the latest protocols at their websites as they are periodically updated (33-36).

Testing of E&L substances includes the analysis of nonvolatile, semivolatile, and highly volatile organic compounds as well as analysis of trace light and heavy metals. Less specific tests such as pH, conductivity, chemical identity via Fourier transform infrared (FTIR) spectroscopy, and analysis of total organic carbon (TOC) may be performed. TOC analysis cannot be used with extract solvents that contain carbon. Highly selective analytical techniques for the detection, characterization, and quantitation of these chemical entities include high-performance liquid chromatography coupled with mass spectroscopy (HPLC-MS), gas chromatography coupled with mass spectroscopy (GC-MS), inductively coupled plasma with mass spectroscopy (ICP-MS), proton nuclear magnetic resonance (1H-NMR), and atomic spectroscopy (e.g., atomic absorption and atomic emission spectroscopy). For instance, nonvolatile compounds may be analyzed with HPLC-MS, whereas highly volatile and semivolatile organic compounds may be resolved with GC-MS. Other methods such as ICP-MS may be used for the detection of residual metals.

The extractables study must be complemented with an appropriately designed leachables study. In addition to monitoring the substances that are leaching under the recommended conditions of use and storage, leachable studies must be designed to identify any interactions and the resulting effect of such interactions on the in-process material and/or on the product. In many cases, drug substance and drug product stability studies may be used to support conclusions concerning the effects of these substances on product quality over time. This is particularly important where there is no downstream purification process to eliminate impurities (e.g., drug product formulation buffer storage container).

In addition to determining the chemical identity, quantity, and composition of E&L, and the impact on process fluid or product quality, E&L must be assessed for cytotoxicity and toxicity in animals in order to preserve patient safety and clinical efficacy (24,25). This information may be obtained from publicly available literature sources such as ICH Q3C (R3) or Product Quality Research Institute Leachables and Extractables Working Group, which stipulates the safety threshold levels for such impurities (37,38). In the absence of specific toxicity data, the threshold of toxicological concern (TTC) approach may be applied in order to judge the risk associated with a particular leachable.

When an SUS is used to grow cell culture, the end user must determine the effect of cell growth on both individual components and the complete SUS. This is important because a recent study showed that the breakdown products of gamma-irradiated antioxidants can have adverse effects on the viability of the cell culture. Spiking studies showed that the phenomenon can occur at levels well below parts per million in a cell line-specific manner (39).

Cell-based assays can be used to identify the particular combinations of cell lines and plastic extractables that may reduce cell culture viability and growth profiles. End users must evaluate the compatibility of the supplied SUS with their specific application, because certain applications (e.g., media storage, bioreactor bags) have been reported to be sensitive to certain combinations of materials and cell lines (30).

The mechanism of interaction of the SUS and contact solution can include leaching from the plastic into the contact solution or the adsorption of the contained solution or its constituents onto the SUS. These interactions can be modeled through science-based assessments of the physicochemical interactions of the solution and SUS. The use of model solvents for the extractables and leachables is an industry standard that limits the...

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Extractables (可萃取物)：在極端條件下（強溶劑、高溫、極端 pH）從材料中「強制提取」出來的化學物質。這代表了最壞情況的完整化學圖譜。

Leachables (溶出物)：在正常製程或儲存條件下，從材料表面遷移到製程流體或產品中的化學物質。Leachables 是 extractables 的子集，但也可能包含在製程條件下產生的新反應產物。

In-process Leachables (製程中溶出物)：在中間製程步驟中溶出、但可被後續純化步驟清除或稀釋至不可檢測水平的物質。雖然最終不會出現在成品中，但仍需在風險評估中考量。

關鍵區別：Extractables 研究用極端條件建立「化學地圖」，Leachables 研究則用實際條件確認「真實風險」。兩者互補，缺一不可。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像一個新買的水壺：

  • Extractables 研究：就像用沸水、醋、酒精分別浸泡水壺 90 天，看看到底能「逼」出什麼物質 — 這是壓力測試
  • Leachables 研究：就像正常使用水壺泡茶、裝水，看看日常使用下會有什麼物質溶出 — 這是真實情境
  • In-process leachables：就像水壺裝的水還會再經過濾水器 — 即使溶出了東西，後續過濾也能去除

你需要先做壓力測試（extractables）建立完整的風險圖譜，再做日常測試（leachables）確認實際風險。

重點提示 Key Notes

E&L 遷移的科學原理：

  • 熱力學因素：決定物質遷移的程度（平衡狀態下能遷移多少）
  • 動力學因素：決定物質遷移的速率（多快達到平衡）
  • 時間因素：接觸時間越長，遷移量越大
  • 溫度效應：溫度越高，遷移速率越快

Leachables 的危害：毒性、致癌性、免疫原性、內分泌干擾。此外還可能導致蛋白質聚集、氧化、降解和微粒形成 — 直接影響產品 CQAs。

分析方法工具箱 Analytical Methods

E&L 測試需要多種互補的分析技術：

目標化合物類型分析方法
非揮發性有機物HPLC-MS
半揮發性/高揮發性有機物GC-MS
殘留金屬ICP-MS
化學鑑定FTIR
總有機碳TOC（不適用於含碳溶劑）
結構鑑定1H-NMR

參考標準：USP <661>、USP <381>、BPOG 和 BPSA 標準化測試方案。

重點提示 Key Notes

Extractables 研究設計要點：

  • 使用極端條件（非正常製程條件）：極端 pH、高溫、長時間、高表面積/體積比
  • 使用不同極性的有機溶劑作為萃取介質
  • 如果常規製程中有預沖洗步驟 → 應包含在 leachables 研究中，但不應包含在 extractables 研究中（因為 extractables 代表最壞情況）
  • 伽馬射線照射和蒸汽處理等預處理也會影響 E&L 圖譜

毒理學評估：

  • 已知物質：參考 ICH Q3C (R3) 殘留溶劑指南中的安全閾值
  • 未知物質：使用 TTC (Threshold of Toxicological Concern，毒理學關注閾值) 方法評估風險

重點提示 Key Notes

細胞培養的特殊風險：研究已證實伽馬射線照射分解的抗氧化劑可在 sub-ppm（低於百萬分之一）的濃度下，以細胞株特異性的方式影響細胞培養活力。這意味著：

  • 不能僅依賴 chemical E&L 數據 — 必須進行細胞功能性測試
  • 不同細胞株的敏感度不同 — 需要針對特定細胞株測試
  • 培養基儲存袋和生物反應器袋是高風險應用

雙向交互作用：不僅塑膠會向溶液釋放物質（leaching），溶液中的成分也可能被塑膠表面吸附（adsorption）。兩個方向都需要評估。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO E&L 策略：作為 CDMO，你可能同時生產多種生物製劑產品。建議建立一個「平台 E&L 資料庫」：

  • 對所有常用的 SUS 元件（薄膜、管路、連接器、過濾器）進行一次全面的 extractables 研究
  • 建立基準數據庫，新客戶產品導入時只需進行針對性的 leachables 確認
  • 這可以大幅降低每個新專案的 E&L 評估時間和成本

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 extractables 研究不應包含預沖洗步驟，但 leachables 研究應該包含？這反映了兩種研究的根本設計哲學有何不同？
  2. 一個 CDMO 客戶要求將 CHO 細胞培養的生物反應器袋從供應商 A 換成供應商 B。請列出你需要進行的 E&L 相關測試清單。
  3. 為什麼 TOC 分析不能用於含碳溶劑的萃取液？有什麼替代方法？
  4. 解釋 TTC (Threshold of Toxicological Concern) 方法在什麼情況下使用，以及它的局限性是什麼。
PDA Technical Report No. 66 — Single-Use Systems (2014) | p53 - p60

本章學習目標

  • 了解一次性系統（SUS）中 BSE/TSE 風險的來源與評估方法
  • 掌握終端使用者與供應商品質系統的關鍵要素
  • 理解 SUS 的有效期限、微粒管控、生物負荷控制與滅菌方法
  • 認識各種滅菌技術（照射、濕熱、氣體）的優缺點與適用場景
  • 掌握感測器技術在 SUS 中的應用與驗證要點
  • 理解 SUS 完整性測試與洩漏預防的實務策略

5.7 BSE/TSE Concerns 5.8 Quality Systems 5.9 Quality Management 5.10 Sterilization 5.11 Integrity

5.7 Bovine Spongiform Encephalopathy (BSE)/Transmissible Spongiform Encephalopathy (TSE) Concerns

Original Text

SUSs have low-risk BSE/TSE concerns and they do not contain high-risk animal-derived components. Certain mold release and slip agents and plastics resins (e.g., polypropylene or polycarbonate) may contain trace levels of additives (e.g., calcium stearate), which are manufactured from bovine tallow and have low BSE/TSE risk. Tallow is a lubricant sometimes used in pelletizing operations for bulk resin or as a mold release agent for the manufacture of SU components. Tallow is produced by treating beef fat with steam to create a mixture of fats. The fat (e.g., glyceryl tristearate) is then boiled in a sodium hydroxide solution, resulting in a mixture of sodium stearate and glycerin.

Tallow-derived additives are not considered as specified BSE risk materials according to the current revision of the U.S. Code of Federal Regulations, Title 21 Part 189.5 (47). Furthermore, the CPMP's "Note for Minimizing the Risk of Transmitting Animal Spongiform Encephalopathies via Human and Veterinary Medicinal Products" (EMA 410/01 rev 3), gives specific consideration to tallow derivatives (48). It states that they are unlikely to be infectious due to the rigorous processing steps (e.g., transesterification, or hydrolysis, at not less than 200°C under pressure for not less than twenty minutes) used during their manufacture. A BSE/TSE risk assessment should be completed and periodically updated to reflect whether an SUS supplier is using components in the fluid pathway that were fabricated from plastic resins containing bovine-derived additives at trace levels.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

BSE/TSE（牛海綿狀腦病/傳播性海綿狀腦病）：這是一類由 Prion（乃變性蛋白）引起的致命性神經退化疾病。在製藥領域，任何含有動物來源成分的材料都必須評估是否有傳播此類疾病的風險。

Calcium Stearate（硬脂酸鈣）：從牛脂（Tallow）衍生的添加劑，常用作塑膠的脫模劑或滑劑。雖然只有微量存在，但仍需要進行風險評估。

Tallow（牛脂）：將牛脂肪以蒸氣處理後，再經氫氧化鈉皂化反應而成。經過高溫（≥200°C）高壓至少20分鐘的嚴格加工程序，已大幅降低 BSE/TSE 感染風險。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像你在買有機食品。食品本身是有機的（SUS 本身不含高風險成分），但包裝上可能用了微量的膠水，而膠水原料可能來自動物。雖然你實際接觸到這些膠水的機率極低，但作為負責任的製造商，你仍然需要追溯每一層供應鏈，確認風險是否可接受——這就是 BSE/TSE 風險評估的精神。

重點提示 Key Notes

美國 21 CFR 189.5 與 EMA 410/01 rev 3 均認定：經過嚴格加工的牛脂衍生物不屬於高風險 BSE 材料。但這不代表可以忽略——終端使用者仍須完成並定期更新 BSE/TSE 風險評估文件，特別是在更換供應商或材料時。

這也是 GMP 精神的核心：不是「零風險」，而是「已評估、已記錄、已管控的可接受風險」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼即使牛脂衍生物被法規認定為低風險，終端使用者仍須執行 BSE/TSE 風險評估？
  2. 如果 SUS 供應商更換了塑膠樹脂來源，終端使用者應如何更新其 BSE/TSE 風險評估？

5.8 The Quality Systems of the End User and Supplier

Original Text

It is important for the end user to have instituted a robust quality system to receive materials, quarantine unreleased and rejected materials, inspect those materials, and release them to production. Since the testing and release of an SUS can vary widely from end user to end user, a complete and careful documentation in the form of a purchase specification and inspection plan should accompany any off-the-shelf or customized SUS requisition. A supplier quality agreement is another useful way to manage the requirements and expectations of both supplier and end user.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Purchase Specification（採購規格書）：詳細列出終端使用者對 SUS 的品質要求，包括材質、尺寸、微粒限值、滅菌方式等。這是品質管控的第一道防線。

Inspection Plan（進料檢驗計畫）：規定收貨後需執行哪些檢查——外觀、包裝完整性、證書核對等。

Supplier Quality Agreement, SQA（供應商品質協議）：正式合約文件，明確雙方在品質、變更管理、偏差處理等方面的權責。這在 SUS 領域尤其重要，因為供應商的任何材料或製程變更都可能影響到最終藥品。

比喻說明 Analogy

就像開餐廳需要跟食材供應商簽訂合約一樣——你要規定食材的品質標準（採購規格書），到貨時要檢查新鮮度和包裝（檢驗計畫），還要跟供應商約定：如果換了牧場來源必須提前通知（供應商品質協議）。SUS 的品質管控邏輯完全一樣。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 的測試與放行標準因終端使用者而異，這意味著沒有「一體適用」的標準。每家 CDMO 必須根據自身的製程風險，制定專屬的進料管控程序。

特別注意：「現成品」（off-the-shelf）和「客製品」（customized）SUS 都需要有採購規格書和檢驗計畫，不能因為是標準品就省略品質文件。

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 環境中，你可能同時為多個客戶代工不同藥品，每個藥品對 SUS 的品質要求可能不同。因此，建立分級的進料管控體系非常重要——例如：用於最終充填的 SUS 需要最嚴格的檢驗（包括微粒、內毒素等），而用於緩衝液配製的 SUS 可以採用簡化的檢驗流程。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 供應商品質協議中應包含哪些與 SUS 特別相關的條款？
  2. 為什麼即使是「現成品」SUS 也需要制定採購規格書？

5.9 Quality Management for Single-Use System Implementation

5.9.1 Determination of Expiration Date and Shelf Life

Original Text

The SUS supplier is expected to provide estimates for expiration dates and the shelf life of the SUS according to validation of maintenance of sterility tests and key functional properties. The expiration date is normally set post-sterilization. Any extension of the shelf life of the SUS must be supported by pertinent data. Real-time aging studies provide the best data to ensure that both the materials and the functional integrity of a sterile barrier system do not degrade with time. Accelerated studies may be a suitable substitute if real-time aging studies cannot be performed. The ASTM F1980–07(2007) Standard Guide for Accelerated Aging of Sterile Barrier Systems for Medical Devices is a widely used test for accelerated aging of the plastic components of SUSs (49).

The term Ready-To-Use is a marketing term often used to describe the benefits of single-use technology or SUS. This designation has no regulatory or scientific basis supporting suitability for use, and end users are responsible for evaluating and determining whether appropriate quality requirements have been met for their application.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Shelf Life（保存期限）：SUS 滅菌後到失效之間的有效時間。這個期限必須有數據支持，確保材料不會隨時間劣化、無菌屏障不會失效。

Real-time Aging（即時老化試驗）：在實際儲存條件下長期觀察材料性能變化，提供最可靠的保存期限數據。

Accelerated Aging（加速老化試驗）：透過提高溫度等方式加速材料老化，以較短時間預測長期性能。ASTM F1980 是業界廣泛採用的加速老化標準。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Ready-To-Use」只是行銷術語！這個名稱沒有法規或科學依據來證明其適用性。終端使用者必須自行評估 SUS 是否符合其特定應用的品質要求。切勿因供應商標示「即用型」就省略必要的評估與驗證。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像超市裡的「即食沙拉」——包裝上寫著「即食」（Ready-To-Eat），但如果你經營的是醫院餐廳，你仍然需要檢驗食材來源、微生物指標、保存溫度等，不能單純相信包裝上的標示。SUS 的「Ready-To-Use」也是同樣道理。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼即時老化試驗（real-time aging）比加速老化試驗提供更可靠的數據？
  2. 如果一個 SUS 供應商聲稱其產品「Ready-To-Use」，終端使用者還需要執行哪些評估？

5.9.2 Dealing with Particulates

Original Text

The level of particulates found in the SUS depends on the application (fluid path contents) of the system. Particles embedded in the bulk plastic as well as the presence of loose particles or fibers in an SUS are undesirable and their limits should be clearly specified in purchase agreements. If the presence of particulates in the fluid path would not have adverse effects on the product or process, then components used upstream of final filters may not require stipulated particulate levels. However, SUS components employed downstream of final filters or without particulate filtration may require stringent limits for particulates to ensure that the final product meets pharmacopeia standards. An acceptable solution is to qualify fluid path rinse volumes to meet USP <788> and USP <790> or equivalent pharmacopeia standards for large-volume injectables (10,50). In addition, the frequency of sampling and analysis may be extended from lot samples to periodic audits of model SUSs—this would be akin to the bioburden audits that are conducted for the validation of sterilization by irradiation. Applicable SUS model system design and particulate audit practices should be established between the supplier and the end user.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Particulates（微粒）：包括嵌入塑膠本體的顆粒、鬆散的粒子或纖維。在藥品生產中，微粒可能對患者安全構成風險，尤其是注射劑。

USP <788>（注射劑微粒檢測）：美國藥典標準，規定注射劑中不可見微粒的限值。

USP <790>（眼用製劑微粒檢測）：針對眼科藥品的更嚴格微粒標準。

重點提示 Key Notes

微粒管控的嚴格程度取決於 SUS 在製程中的位置：

  • 最終過濾器上游：微粒要求可以較寬鬆，因為下游還有過濾步驟
  • 最終過濾器下游：必須執行嚴格的微粒限值管控，因為已無後續過濾保護

這就是「風險分級管控」的具體體現——在最關鍵的位置投入最多的管控資源。

比喻說明 Analogy

就像家裡的淨水系統：廚房水龍頭前還有濾芯（最終過濾器），所以進水管（上游 SUS）的水質要求可以稍寬；但如果你直接從水龍頭喝水而沒有濾芯（下游 SUS，無後續過濾），那進水管的水質標準就必須達到飲用水等級。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼微粒管控可以從「每批取樣」簡化為「定期稽核模型 SUS」？這樣做需要什麼前提條件？
  2. 如果一個 SUS 用於大量注射劑的最終充填，應符合哪個藥典標準？

5.9.3 Sanitation and Sterilization

Original Text

The use of an SUS in biopharmaceutical manufacturing can vary so widely that in one instance there may be no need for a specific bioburden control (e.g., as in the mixing of nonsterile buffer formulations or other raw materials) whereas in another, stringent restrictions on the incidence of a bioburden are called for (e.g., validated sterility for final formulation and filling of sterile drug product). It is critical for the end user to review processes, fluids, contact, and storage conditions for microbial quality to determine the appropriate measures to be taken.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Bioburden Control（生物負荷控制）：指控制微生物污染的程度。不同應用場景對生物負荷的要求差異極大——從非無菌緩衝液配製（允許一定生物負荷）到最終無菌充填（需經驗證的無菌保證）。

重點提示 Key Notes

決定清潔和滅菌策略的關鍵因素包括：製程類型、接觸流體的性質、接觸時間、以及儲存條件。終端使用者必須根據這些因素的綜合評估來決定適當的微生物品質管控措施——這體現了 GMP 中「基於風險的方法」（Risk-Based Approach）。

5.9.4 Bioburden Control

Original Text

The molding and extrusion of SUS components at high temperatures plus their assembly into a functional SUS in a clean and controlled environment confers advantages such as intrinsically low incidence of bioburden on the fluid paths of the SUS. Although this inherently low degree of bioburden may be adequate for nonsterile processes, many SU components or systems may be autoclaved or subjected to gamma irradiation for additional control of bioburden. Doses of irradiation as low as 8 to 10 kGy are enough to reduce intrinsic bioburden to zero; however, in practice, doses >25 kGy are used to achieve a sterility assurance level (SAL) of 10-6. The increased irradiation dosage has the advantage of attaining a bioburden level comparable to that of validated sterility without conducting the necessary validation protocols or periodic sterilization audits that would otherwise be required for a statistical claim of sterility of 10-6 (51). This may be suitable for bacterial fermentation applications and aseptic processes such as the preparation and storage of downstream chromatography and ultrafiltration buffers and intermediates.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SAL（Sterility Assurance Level, 無菌保證水準）：表示滅菌後存在活微生物的概率。SAL 10-6 表示每一百萬個產品中最多只有一個可能是非無菌的。

Gamma Irradiation（伽瑪射線照射）：利用放射性同位素（通常是鈷-60）發出的伽瑪射線穿透塑膠材料，破壞微生物 DNA 以達到滅菌效果。

劑量與 SAL 的關係

低劑量照射：8-10 kGy → 可將固有生物負荷降至零
                        （但不足以聲稱 SAL 10⁻⁶）

高劑量照射：≥25 kGy  → 可達到 SAL 10⁻⁶
                        （等同於經驗證的無菌水準）
                        （免除定期滅菌稽核的需求）

重點提示 Key Notes

使用 ≥25 kGy 照射劑量的策略優勢在於：不需要執行完整的滅菌驗證方案和定期無菌稽核，就能達到統計上等同於 SAL 10-6 的無菌保證水準。這對下游緩衝液和中間體儲存等應用特別實用。

但要注意：更高的照射劑量也會增加材料劣化和可萃取物（Extractables）生成的風險，這需要在風險評估中一併考量。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼實務上使用 >25 kGy 而不是 8-10 kGy 就足以消除生物負荷的劑量？
  2. 高劑量照射可能帶來哪些「副作用」？如何在風險評估中平衡這些因素？

5.10 Sterilization

5.10.1 Irradiation Sterilization

Original Text

SUSs are especially suitable to sterilization by irradiation because of the relative transparency of plastics to ionizing radiation, which allows complex systems to be sterilized without the risk of spreading the sterilizing agent throughout the fluid path. Irradiation may be used to sterilize plastics or SUS assemblies that may be unsuitable for steam sterilization. The practice of sterilizing via irradiation is well established in the medical device industry with transferable standards that can be applied to SU process equipment (51). Although no specific industry standard has been developed for the sterilization of SUSs, the industry and regulatory communities have adopted the ANSI/AAMI/ISO 11137 standard, Sterilization of Health Care Products—Radiation, and the closely related AAMI Technical Information Report TIR 33:2005, Substantiation of a Selected Sterilization Dose—Method VD max (51,52). Adaptation and implementation of these standards to the implementation of SUS have been discussed in the literature (53). The most common alternative methods mentioned in the standards are the dose substantiation methods (i.e., the verification dose max, or "VD max," methods).

In practice, a typical audit involves the selection of a single-use product (SUP) as representative of the SUS. A supplier quality audit must consider how the product family and the representative product design were derived. In cases where testing the representative product would be impractical (e.g., due to size and complexity), a portion of the sample item may be used with mathematical scaling between the actual product and the sample item. A supplier quality audit must include an understanding of the mathematical scaling technique. Since the standards require that a supplier must perform quarterly dose audits for each product family, the end-user quality audit of the SU supplier must ascertain that there is a procedure in place for the supplier to conduct quarterly dose auditing. Validation normally involves the determination of an average bioburden level in a representative master system, assessment of radiation resistance by sterility testing of the fluid path of the master system after a low "verification" dose (about 8 to 10 kGy), and calculation of a suitable dose to provide a sterility assurance level or a probability of nonsterility of 10-6 for the model product and its variants. The supplier and the end user should review the applicability of validation via master system sterilization to the end user's SUS configuration.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

ISO 11137（醫療產品輻射滅菌標準）：雖然最初是為醫療器材制定的，但已被 SUS 業界廣泛採用。這是目前 SUS 照射滅菌最主要的參考標準。

VD max（驗證劑量最大值法）：一種劑量確認方法。先以低劑量（8-10 kGy）照射代表性產品並進行無菌測試，再根據結果計算達到 SAL 10-6 所需的滅菌劑量。

Quarterly Dose Audit（每季劑量稽核）：供應商必須每季對每個產品家族執行劑量驗證，確保生物負荷水準未發生顯著變化。

比喻說明 Analogy

照射滅菌就像用 X 光機掃描行李：X 光可以穿透行李箱（塑膠外殼），不需要打開箱子就能達到「檢查」效果。同樣地，伽瑪射線可以穿透 SUS 的塑膠材料，在不打開密封系統的情況下完成滅菌——這正是照射滅菌對複雜 SUS 系統最大的優勢。

重點提示 Key Notes

照射滅菌驗證的核心流程：

  1. 選擇代表性產品（或可行的樣品部分）
  2. 測定平均生物負荷水準
  3. 以低驗證劑量（8-10 kGy）照射後進行無菌測試
  4. 計算達到 SAL 10-6 所需的正式滅菌劑量
  5. 每季執行劑量稽核以確認持續合規

終端使用者必須確認供應商的驗證方法適用於其特定的 SUS 配置。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼照射滅菌特別適合複雜的 SUS 組件？相比蒸氣滅菌有何優勢？
  2. 當代表性產品因尺寸過大而無法直接測試時，可以使用什麼替代方法？
  3. 每季劑量稽核的目的是什麼？如果稽核發現生物負荷增加，應採取什麼行動？

5.10.2 Sterilization with Moist Heat

Original Text

Several methods of sterilization are acceptable for use with SUS. Each is appropriate for different applications and should be evaluated for suitability.

  • Autoclaving — This technique is often used to sterilize an SUS or SU components assembled by end users (54). After that, most end users may find it more convenient to source preassembled SUSs that are sterilized by gamma irradiation.
  • Sterilize-in-place (SIP) — Steam-to-connector configuration is one example of SIP. The physical limitations of plastics limit the ability of an SUS to be sterilized by steam pressure in situ. Some SU connectors are designed to be physically attached to a stainless multiple-use port so that the tank connection can be sterilized with steam. Steam-to or steam-through connectors tend to be preconnected to tubing with an SUS at one end and are presterilized by autoclaving or irradiation. A valve or barrier mechanism is used to isolate the sterile system. The steam-to or steam-through connector is then connected to a tank, and the interface is sterilized with steam (55).
  • Gas sterilization — Although it is not a common practice, an SUS may be sterilized using a gas such as ethylene oxide. Gas sterilization is not as popular as other methods of sterilization for two reasons: 1) ethylene chlorohydrin and ethylene glycol reaction by-products can form; and 2) some ethylene oxide may be retained in the filter matrix, when a filter is present. Some of the factors that affect the use of gas sterilization are preconditioning, concentration, relative humidity, temperature, and time. The monitoring and validation of gas sterilization is conducted by destroying a suitable biological indicator such as the spores of Bacillus subtilis. To achieve successful sterilization using ethylene oxide, the SUS should be dry and wrapped in a way that allows for the influx of water vapor and gas into the fluid path. The appropriate concentration of gas and other parameters must be established during development and validation processes. It is important to rid the SUS of residual gas and other undesirable by-products after gas sterilization.
  • Resterilization — SU components are not amenable to multiple autoclave cycles. Gamma irradiation is a cumulative process and most SU components cannot be re-irradiated without causing significant degradation of physical integrity, creation of extractables, and reduction of shelf life. In addition, irradiation may reduce the resistance of the SUS to subsequent steam exposure, which may increase the formation of extractables and leachables. In general, an SUS is not designed to be resterilized.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SIP（就地滅菌）：利用蒸氣對連接介面進行滅菌。由於塑膠材料耐溫有限，SUS 無法像不鏽鋼設備那樣全面進行 SIP，但可透過特殊設計的 Steam-to 或 Steam-through 連接器，對 SUS 與不鏽鋼槽體的接合處進行蒸氣滅菌。

EtO（環氧乙烷）滅菌：較少用於 SUS，主要因為會產生有害副產物（氯乙醇、乙二醇），且氣體可能殘留在過濾器基質中。

Resterilization（再滅菌）：SUS 設計上不支援再滅菌。多次高壓滅菌或照射會導致材料劣化、可萃取物增加、保存期縮短。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 滅菌方法的選擇決策樹：

  • 優先選擇：伽瑪射線照射（最適合預組裝 SUS）
  • 終端使用者自組裝：高壓滅菌（Autoclaving）
  • 不鏽鋼介面連接：SIP（蒸氣到連接器）
  • 不建議：EtO 氣體滅菌（副產物風險）
  • 禁止：再滅菌（材料劣化嚴重）

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 就像免洗餐具——設計上就是一次性使用的。你不會把用過的免洗筷放進洗碗機再用一次，因為材質無法承受反覆清洗和高溫。同理，SUS 不設計為可再滅菌——強行再滅菌就像把紙杯放進烤箱，只會造成材料變質和安全風險。

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 環境中，如果 SUS 在使用前發現滅菌包裝破損或過期，正確的做法是整套報廢而非嘗試再滅菌。這也是為什麼庫存管理（先進先出 FIFO）和保存期限監控在 SUS 管理中如此重要。一套過期的客製化 SUS 可能需要數週才能重新訂購，直接影響生產排程。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 EtO 氣體滅菌不常用於 SUS？列舉至少兩個原因。
  2. Steam-to-connector 的設計如何解決塑膠材料無法耐受高壓蒸氣的限制？
  3. 如果一個 SUS 已經過伽瑪照射滅菌但包裝破損，可以用高壓滅菌重新滅菌嗎？為什麼？

5.10.3 Sensor Technology

Original Text

The pace of technological evolution of SU sensors is so rapid that the end user may decide to use several strategies at the same time. The end user may:

  • Choose a novel method
  • Adapt an existing technology for SU
  • Apply traditional multiple-use sensors in an SUS

The end user must evaluate the technology for suitability according to the accuracy, repeatability, range, and calibration requirements. Other questions to consider are:

  • How compatible is the SU sensor with the sterilization technique?
  • What is the shelf life of the sensor?
  • What is the in-service life of the sensor?
  • How appropriate is the sensor for the SUS in question?

Early examples of SU sensors for pH and dissolved oxygen in an SU bioreactor (SUB) were based on optical differences observed on a chemical patch immersed in the process fluid. Optical sensors are calibrated with a batch-specific calibration standard instead of a zero-and-span calibration technique. The end user must be aware that optical sensors may be sensitive to photo bleaching and drift. In general, steam sterilization cycles may be more damaging to a reusable sensor than a single gamma sterilization cycle. Some SU sensors may be calibrated using a traditional two-point calibration technique prior to use without any adverse effects on sterility. Thus, SU sensors may be inherently more reliable than reusable sensors. The end user must pay attention to the advantages and limitations of a chosen SU sensor, including the specific requirements and circumstances of application.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SU Sensor（一次性感測器）：專為一次性使用設計的製程感測器，常見於 pH 和溶氧（DO）的測量。相比傳統可重複使用的感測器，SU 感測器只經歷一次滅菌循環，可能具有更高的可靠性。

Optical Sensor（光學感測器）：利用浸入製程流體中的化學貼片（Chemical Patch）上的光學變化來測量參數。使用批次專用校準標準品而非傳統的零點/跨距校準。

Photo Bleaching（光漂白）：光學感測器的化學貼片在長時間光照下可能失去螢光強度，導致測量漂移。

比喻說明 Analogy

傳統可重複使用的感測器就像一把反覆經過高溫洗碗機清洗的菜刀——每次清洗都會造成些許磨損。而 SU 感測器就像一把全新的手術刀——只用一次，所以性能最佳。這也是為什麼 SU 感測器在某些方面可能比可重複使用的感測器更可靠。

重點提示 Key Notes

選擇 SU 感測器時必須評估的四大面向：

  • 準確度與重複性：是否符合製程要求？
  • 滅菌相容性：與 SUS 的滅菌方法是否相容？
  • 保存期限：感測器本身（尤其是化學貼片）的有效期是多久？
  • 使用壽命：在製程條件下能穩定運作多長時間？

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 SU 感測器可能比傳統可重複使用的感測器更可靠？
  2. 光學式 pH 感測器的校準方式與傳統電極式有何不同？各有什麼優缺點？

5.10.4 Qualification and Validation

Original Text

The end user is responsible for process validation, and the method for validating an SUS must be determined using a risk-based approach, which considers the effective integration of the SUS design into the end user's quality systems (8). Although purchasing a preassembled, sterilized SUS allows the end user to take advantage of the qualification data generated by the SUS supplier, it is incumbent on the end user to understand the supplier's qualification approach and how it applies to the end user's specific application. The scope of process validation at the manufacturing site must encompass the materials for construction, relevant testing procedures (e.g., for heavy metals, particulates, pyrogenicity, cytotoxicity, leachables, and extractables), and information on any sterilization method used. Any deficiencies discovered during the validation process may be mitigated by applying additional targeted checks or other controls. Additional information may include pressure limitations, correct procedures for using aseptic connectors and tubing fusers, and how many times pump tubing can be reused. The validation study should ensure and document process-specific fitness for use of the SUS.

Pertinent validation concerns for an SUS include the following:

  • SU products, and qualified alternative designs, used in bulk drug substance and sterile filling should be incorporated into the media fill program.
  • SU filtration systems may need to be designed with alternative receiving containers to accommodate pre-use wetting and integrity testing.
  • Since it may not be feasible to test the SUS for leaks, the manufacturing, shipping, handling, and operation procedures should be assessed for their assurance of avoiding issues (punctures, tears, stresses) that may lead to leaks.
  • While extractables data may be suitable for predicting worst-case in-process leachables, actual testing of leachables may be necessary for final drug formulation in bulk storage containers.
  • When proprietary sterile connections are incorporated into the SUS, the end user must review supplier validation data to determine whether any additional process-specific validation may be required.
  • Proper handling and manipulation of the SUS by trained operators should be qualified.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Process Validation（製程驗證）：終端使用者的責任，必須證明 SUS 在其特定製程中能持續且可靠地運作。供應商的確認數據是起點，但不是終點。

Risk-Based Approach（基於風險的方法）：驗證的深度和廣度應與風險成正比——高風險應用（如最終充填）需要最全面的驗證。

Media Fill（培養基充填模擬）：使用培養基代替藥品進行模擬充填，以驗證無菌製程的有效性。SUS 組件必須納入培養基充填計畫中。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 驗證的六大關注重點：

  1. 培養基充填：SUS 和替代設計須納入 Media Fill 計畫
  2. 過濾系統設計：需考慮使用前潤濕和完整性測試的需求
  3. 洩漏風險：因無法直接測試，需從製造、運輸、操作流程保證
  4. 浸出物測試：最終藥品配方可能需要實際浸出物測試
  5. 專利連接：需審查供應商驗證數據的適用性
  6. 操作人員培訓：SUS 的正確處理和操作須經確認

比喻說明 Analogy

買一台預組裝的烤箱（預組裝 SUS），廠商會提供性能測試報告（供應商確認數據）。但這不代表你不需要在自己的廚房試烤——你仍然要確認在你的電壓、你的擺放位置、你的食譜下，這台烤箱能正常運作（製程驗證）。供應商的數據是起點，而非終點。

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 環境中，驗證 SUS 的成本和時間投入不容忽視。建議建立「SUS 驗證平台」——將常用的 SUS 配置進行一次性全面驗證（包括 E&L、微粒、無菌性、培養基充填），之後新專案如使用相同配置，可引用平台驗證數據，大幅縮短專案啟動時間。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼終端使用者不能完全依賴供應商的確認數據？
  2. SUS 為什麼必須納入培養基充填計畫？如果不納入會有什麼風險？
  3. 「驗證過程中發現的缺陷可透過額外的針對性檢查來緩解」——請舉一個具體例子。

5.11 Integrity

5.11.1 Testing an SUS for Leaks

Original Text

The requirements for testing an SUS will depend on its intended use. The retention of structural integrity (i.e., containers do not leak) is the main concern and is a key concern in process-contact applications. For low-risk applications (e.g., sample and buffer bags), an understanding of supplier testing, performance, and training in appropriate handling procedures may be sufficient.

SUSs are increasingly used for the production of vaccines, and the egress of a live virus could have serious consequences; therefore, specific testing of individual systems is recommended.

When an SUS is used for holding media, the potential for microbial ingress that may compromise sterility becomes a significant concern. Attempts have been made to assess the maximum size of a defect that will compromise the effectiveness of a flexible bag (56). This is a complex undertaking because it depends on factors such as the surface tension of the liquid in the bag, time, temperature, and the method of measurement. In addition, the permeability of individual components (e.g., tubing and films) may differ according to the test agent (e.g., gas or dye) used.

The structural integrity of the SUS should be carefully evaluated in a collaborative manner by the end user and the supplier. Post-shipment/transport testing to evaluate the method of packaging the SUS will need to be incorporated. To test for the integrity of the fluid path during qualification—including tubing manifolds and connectors—a suggested method is to internally pressurize tubing with air and hold it under water. Provided that testing will not compromise the sterility or cleanliness of the equipment, manifolds can be inspected by manipulation to check for air bubbles at both tubing connector engagements and along the entire length of tubing. For upstream applications, the user should confirm the supplier's claims during verification and accept materials based on their documentation thereafter. A special case may need to be made for customized SUS. Demands are generally stricter for product containers; therefore, end users may wish to ask the suppliers what testing is feasible for larger containers at their sites versus the end user's site (after installation).

To test a bag container or a SUS for leakage, a suggested method (depending on the size of the SUS) is to fill the plastic bag or SUS with water inside the bin, drum, or tank and check for leaks at maximum volume. If the location of the leak is not apparent, fill the plastic container with water outside of the bin, drum, or tank on a flat, absorbent surface such as cardboard or paper. Locate the leak by identifying wet spots on the absorbent surface corresponding to a position on the container. Using the mapped location of the leak on the bag, examine the bin, drum, or tank for sharp points that may have caused the leak. Examine the leak under magnification to determine whether the leakage was caused by puncture, tear, creasing, pinhole, or another means. Track leak locations to help with root cause analysis of failure modes (e.g. handling, structural/design considerations, and material failure).

If the end user determines that a leak was caused by a manufacturing defect, the failed sample should be returned to the supplier for quality investigation and corrective action. The returned sample should include full information regarding the conditions of use and location of the leak. Suppliers should maintain records of system failures and their root causes for further analysis.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Structural Integrity（結構完整性）：SUS 的容器不會洩漏——這是最基本的品質要求。完整性測試的嚴格程度取決於應用風險。

Microbial Ingress（微生物侵入）：當 SUS 用於儲存培養基或無菌製品時，任何缺陷都可能導致微生物進入，破壞無菌性。

重點提示 Key Notes

完整性測試的風險分級策略：

  • 低風險（樣品袋、緩衝液袋）：依賴供應商測試數據和適當的操作訓練即可
  • 中風險（上游製程）：驗證時確認供應商聲明，後續依據文件接受
  • 高風險（疫苗生產、活病毒）：建議對每個系統進行個別測試
  • 最高風險（最終藥品容器）：最嚴格的測試要求

比喻說明 Analogy

洩漏偵測就像偵探辦案：先在容器中注水（犯罪現場保全），然後在吸水性表面上找到濕點（找到證據），再對照袋子上的位置找到漏點（鎖定嫌疑人），最後用放大鏡檢查是穿刺、撕裂還是材料缺陷（確認動機和手法）。追蹤每次洩漏的位置，就像建立犯罪熱點地圖——幫助你找出系統性的根本原因。

實務應用 Practical Application

洩漏測試的實務流程：

  1. 在容器/桶內以水填滿 SUS 袋至最大容量
  2. 如漏點不明顯，將裝水的袋子移到吸水表面（紙板或紙張）上
  3. 辨識吸水表面上的濕點位置，對照袋子上的相應位置
  4. 檢查容器/桶內是否有尖銳物可能刺穿袋子
  5. 用放大鏡檢查漏點類型（穿刺、撕裂、折痕、針孔）
  6. 記錄並追蹤所有洩漏位置，進行失效模式分析

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼疫苗生產中活病毒的 SUS 完整性要求特別嚴格？
  2. 運輸後測試（Post-shipment testing）為什麼需要納入完整性評估？
  3. 如果發現洩漏是由製造缺陷造成的，終端使用者應該採取哪些步驟？

5.11.2 Leak Prevention in an SUS

Original Text

Leaks in fluid management systems can lead to contamination, personnel safety risk, and product loss. A thorough investigation must be conducted to determine the cause, identify the source of the leak, and monitor corrective and preventive actions. The investigation strategy should include a leak-investigation procedure for generating standard reports. Such a report must include the location of the leak on the assembly, the surrounding temperature conditions, composition of the fluids, any adverse mechanical events, and an analysis of the failure mode. This information is particularly useful for trend analysis. Consider the example depicted in Figure 5.11.2-1 in which a bioprocess container (BC) was investigated for leaks. Individual reports for each leak were analyzed and the location of each leak was mapped and identified according to type and cause (57).

Figure 5.11.2-1: Investigation of a Bioprocess Container for Leaks

The leaks were mapped onto a deconstructed view of the BC (Figure 5.11.2-2). The map indicated the leaks were more likely to occur at the bottom and top of the bag (i.e., where the BC was handled by operators). Subsequently, the operators were trained to avoid damage due to mishandling, and this led to a significant decline in leak rates (57).

Distribution of Bioprocess Container Leak Locations: Bag Chamber, Tubing, Connector, Sampling Manifold

Figure 5.11.2-2: Identifying the Location of Leaks on a Bioprocessing Container

This, in turn, led to the following recommendations.

For end users:

  • Train operators to be aware of the root causes of leaks.
  • Remove sharp objects from the vicinity of a BC.
  • Improve lifting equipment for handling the BC.
  • Make sure that the BC fits properly into the container in order to minimize handling.

Partnering with suppliers:

  • Share leak investigation reports when returning defective products.
  • Use supplier-developed methods to improve reliability.
  • Identify and implement a more robust BC.

The summation of activities involving the hands-on steps required to successfully assemble and make a system ready for use for a specific SUS application is called deployment. This includes a defined setup and deployment stage, with standardized activities for each part, and is a recognized success factor for SUS implementation. Deployment should be a routine part of the workflow and planning for each SUS application.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Leak-Investigation Procedure（洩漏調查程序）：標準化的報告程序，記錄洩漏位置、環境條件、流體組成、機械事件和失效模式。這些數據是趨勢分析的基礎。

Trend Analysis（趨勢分析）：透過系統性收集和分析洩漏數據，找出重複出現的模式和根本原因——例如案例中發現洩漏多發生在袋子頂部和底部（操作人員拿取的位置）。

Deployment（部署）：指將 SUS 組裝並準備就緒以供特定應用使用的所有動手操作步驟的總和。標準化的部署流程是 SUS 實施成功的關鍵因素。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像你經營一家物流公司，運送液體產品。如果某條路線的包裹經常破損，你不會只是每次賠償了事——你會建立破損報告系統，追蹤每個破損的位置、原因和時間，最終發現是搬運工在卸貨時總是抓同一個角落導致破損。解決方案：培訓搬運工正確的搬運方式 + 改善包裝設計。SUS 洩漏預防的邏輯完全一樣。

重點提示 Key Notes

案例研究的關鍵發現：將洩漏位置「地圖化」後，發現洩漏集中在袋子頂部和底部——正是操作人員拿取的地方。這個發現直接指向根本原因（操作不當）而非材料缺陷。

改善措施雙管齊下：

  • 終端使用者端：操作人員培訓、移除尖銳物、改善搬運設備、確保袋子正確放入容器
  • 供應商合作端：分享洩漏調查報告、採用供應商改善方法、導入更耐用的設計

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 環境中，建立 SUS 洩漏追蹤系統的具體做法：

  1. 建立標準化的洩漏調查表單（含位置圖示、照片、環境數據）
  2. 每月彙整洩漏數據進行趨勢分析
  3. 設定洩漏率 KPI 和告警閾值
  4. 定期與供應商召開品質改善會議，分享洩漏分析結果
  5. 將洩漏預防納入操作人員的年度複訓計畫

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼洩漏調查報告需要包含「周圍溫度條件」和「流體組成」？這些資訊如何幫助找到根本原因？
  2. 案例中發現洩漏多發生在袋子頂部和底部，這指向什麼根本原因？你會建議什麼改善措施？
  3. 什麼是「Deployment」？為什麼它被認為是 SUS 實施的成功關鍵因素？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • BSE/TSE 風險：SUS 整體屬於低風險，但含牛脂衍生添加劑（如硬脂酸鈣）的塑膠樹脂仍需完成風險評估。美國 21 CFR 189.5 和 EMA 410/01 均認定經嚴格加工的牛脂衍生物不屬於高風險 BSE 材料。
  • 品質系統：終端使用者須建立完整的進料管控體系，包括採購規格書、檢驗計畫和供應商品質協議（SQA）。不同 SUS 的測試與放行標準因應用而異。
  • 有效期限與保存期限：須有即時或加速老化試驗數據支持。「Ready-To-Use」僅為行銷術語，不具法規或科學效力。
  • 微粒管控：依據 SUS 在製程中的位置（最終過濾器上游 vs 下游）實施風險分級管控，下游組件須符合 USP <788>/<790> 標準。
  • 生物負荷控制：低劑量照射（8-10 kGy）可消除固有生物負荷，但 ≥25 kGy 才能達到 SAL 10-6 的無菌保證水準。
  • 滅菌方法：伽瑪照射是 SUS 首選滅菌方式；SIP 適用於不鏽鋼介面連接；EtO 因副產物風險不建議使用；SUS 不設計為可再滅菌。
  • 感測器技術：SU 感測器只經歷一次滅菌循環，可能比可重複使用的感測器更可靠，但須注意光漂白和漂移等限制。
  • 確認與驗證：終端使用者負責製程驗證，須涵蓋材料建構、測試程序、滅菌方法，且 SUS 須納入培養基充填計畫。
  • 完整性與洩漏：完整性測試需依風險分級——從低風險（依賴供應商數據）到高風險（個別系統測試）。建立標準化洩漏調查程序和趨勢分析是預防洩漏的關鍵。
  • 洩漏預防：案例研究顯示操作不當是洩漏的主要根本原因。標準化的部署（Deployment）流程和操作人員培訓是 SUS 實施成功的關鍵因素。

PDA Technical Report No. 66 (2014): Single-Use Systems for Pharmaceutical and Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing

Section 3b: Quality Considerations Part 2 (5.7–5.11) | Pages 53–60

Educational Material for CDMO Professionals

Section 4: Business Drivers

商業驅動因素 | p61-p69

PDA Technical Report No. 66 (2014) — Single-Use Systems | p61 - p69

本章學習目標

  • 理解驅動企業採用 Single-Use Systems (SUS) 的關鍵商業因素與評估框架
  • 掌握 Lifecycle Approach (生命週期方法) 與 Opportunity Cost (機會成本) 在 SUS 決策中的應用
  • 學習 Cost of Goods Manufactured (COGM) 模型的結構，包含 Process Model、Operational Model、Variable Cost 及 Fixed Cost 子模型
  • 理解 Investment Costs (投資成本) 的組成因素，包括設備、設施、公用設施及間接成本
  • 認識 SUS 實施對 QC/QA 品質成本及固定營運成本的影響
