Complementary documents

The PEP, sometimes called a project implementation plan (PIP), provides a thorough and detailed description of the project. It complements other project documents such as the VMP, user requirements, and other non-GxP documentation, including environmental safety, waste-handling requirements, and inspections and building permits. Since not all projects involve the same level of complexity, the PEP may need to be modified accordingly. Therefore, this table is for illustrative purposes. The final content of the PEP will depend on the approach to the project, risk-management level, and business drivers such as the nature of the product, lifecycle requirements, engineering policies, and project scale.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PEP (Project Execution Plan，專案執行計畫)— 這是 SUS 實施的「總綱文件」。它涵蓋 12 大主題，從專案簡介、範圍界定、合約文件、品質策略、風險管理，一路延伸到 HSE（健康安全環境）、採購安裝、教育訓練和移交支援。

VMP (Validation Master Plan，確效主計畫)— 與 PEP 並行的確效規劃文件，定義整個 SUS 的確效策略、範圍和時程。

重點提示 Key Notes

Table 7.4.1-1 的 12 個章節結構提供了 PEP 的完整藍圖。注意幾個容易被忽略的重點：

  • 第 6 章 Organization：包含衝突解決機制 — 這對多部門協作的 SUS 專案至關重要
  • 第 8 章 Risk Management：不只是風險評估，還要有具體的緩解策略和計畫
  • 第 11 章 Handover：包含 Materials Management（物料管理），這是 SUS 持續運作的關鍵

PEP 的內容深度應依據專案複雜度調整 — 小型 SUS 專案可以精簡，大型設施建置專案則需要完整展開。

比喻說明 Analogy

PEP 的 12 個章節就像蓋房子時的「建築設計說明書」。第 1-4 章是「我們要蓋什麼」；第 5-6 章是「誰來蓋、怎麼蓋」；第 7-8 章是「品質和風險怎麼管」；第 9 章是「安全和環保」；第 10-11 章是「實際施工到驗收移交」；第 12 章是「附件和參考資料」。少了任何一個部分，房子都可能出問題。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你的 CDMO 同時為三個不同客戶的生物藥品建置 SUS 產線，PEP 中的哪些章節最需要客製化？
  2. 為什麼 PEP 需要包含「衝突解決」(Conflict Resolution) 機制？請舉一個 SUS 實施中可能發生的跨部門衝突情境。
7.4.2 Process and Facility Requirements: Basis of Approach

Original Text

Process and facility requirements are key business drivers, and their consideration forms an important part of the PEP preparation. SUSs can be integrated and deployed within existing processes and manufacturing facilities. However, when a high level of SUS integration is necessary, new facilities may be required because of the radical structural differences between SU and MU systems. For PEP preparation, SUS integration must be considered from the point of view of the engineering service, suppliers, and the end user. The outputs are three relatively simple documents which outline the implementation strategy: facility-, implementation-, and operational-level plans.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SUS 整合需要從三個不同的視角來規劃，產出三份文件：

  • Facility-Level Plan（設施層級計畫）— SUS 如何融入設施設計空間
  • Implementation-Level Plan（實施層級計畫）— 供應商和終端使用者在生產、行銷和供應 SUS 時的參數
  • Operational-Level Plan（營運層級計畫）— SUS 組裝、連接和部署的參數

重點提示 Key Notes

當 SUS 整合程度很高時，可能需要全新的設施設計。這是因為 SU 和 MU 系統在結構上有根本差異：SU 不需要 CIP/SIP 管路、不需要大量公用設施連接，但需要更多的倉儲空間、廢棄物處理區域和人員操作動線。這個決策點對 CDMO 的資本支出影響巨大。

7.4.3-7.4.5 Three-Level Integration Plans

Original Text

7.4.3 Facility-Level Plan

This plan shows how the SUS fits into the facility design space together with other process equipment, and it summarizes different functional situations.

7.4.4 Implementation-Level Plan

This contains the parameters that affect the supplier during the production, marketing, and supply of SUS for off-the-shelf or customized systems. In addition, it describes the parameters that influence the end user during the creation of self-made or in-house SUSs.

7.4.5 Operational-Level Plan

This describes the parameters for SUS integration (i.e., assembly, connection, and deployment) in readiness for manufacturing. It is essential to review each of these factors thoroughly because they provide the necessary content to complete the PEP and subsequent documents. The operational-level plan contains elements from manufacturing and SUS strategies. The input and output documents for SUS integration are illustrated in Figure 7.4.5-1.

[Figure 7.4.5-1: SUS Process and Facility Integration]

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

三個層級的整合計畫形成一個從宏觀到微觀的規劃架構：

  • Facility-Level（設施層級）— 回答「SUS 在廠房中的位置在哪裡？」
  • Implementation-Level（實施層級）— 回答「SUS 設備從哪裡來？是外購還是自製？」
  • Operational-Level（營運層級）— 回答「SUS 怎麼組裝、連接、部署到可以開始生產？」

比喻說明 Analogy

三個層級計畫就像規劃一場大型宴會：Facility-Level 是選擇場地和空間配置（宴會廳的桌椅怎麼擺放）；Implementation-Level 是決定食材和餐具的來源（自己煮還是外燴？餐具買現成的還是訂製？）；Operational-Level 是當天的準備流程（菜色如何上桌、餐具如何擺設、服務人員如何走動）。

重點提示 Key Notes

Implementation-Level Plan 中提到兩種 SUS 來源：off-the-shelf（現成品）和 self-made（自製品）。這個選擇對風險管理有重大影響 — 自製 SUS 雖然靈活度高，但需要自行承擔規格制定、批次紀錄、適格性確認和穩定性研究等所有品質責任。

7.4.6 Facility-Level Integration Plan

Original Text

This is normally a concise document that describes the integration of the SUS into the facility design space (87). Robust process knowledge is a prerequisite for defining the various operational situations of the facility. It is critical to adopt a holistic approach because several factors (e.g., compliance, environment, operational requirements, and the compatibility of processes and equipment) may affect the successful operation of the SUS. These factors depend on the nature and properties of the product (e.g., biological or chemical entity) and the requirements for containment. Figure 7.4.6-1 provides a conceptual representation of how the successive steps in facility-level integration may be achieved. Some of the most relevant parameters to consider include:

  • Product type
  • Sterile or nonsterile processing
  • Product volume
  • Lifecycle
  • Available surface footprint
  • Dependence on utilities
  • Flexibility of facility design
  • Avoiding cross-contamination
  • Level of segregation and dedication
  • Environment (e.g., room air grade, containment)
  • Personnel interactions
  • Process validation (may be necessary when the equipment used in scale-up changes in terms of volume, aspect ratio, or between MUS and SUS)

[Figure 7.4.6-1: Process and Facility Considerations for SUS Implementation]

The chart on the left side of the figure depicts a holistic vision of a facility from the top-level processes that created it (outside rings) to the process design space (inside ring). The key points to address during implementation are illustrated as a stakeholder pathway. The triangle and the down-facing arrow on the right show how the risk from biological or chemical potency may affect the amount of dedication/segregation and containment necessary at all levels within the manufacturing site.

A structured risk-based approach should be used to prepare the facility plan, starting with the manufacturing strategy prepared in S1 and S2, and the SUS implementation strategy prepared in S3.

Process mapping and regulatory assessment tables (RATs) are additional tools for defining facility requirements. Process mapping identifies operating scenarios and potential CQAs, while a RAT enables cross-referencing to key GMP factors and other regulatory requirements where it is appropriate for the user to document their policy regarding those regulations (i.e., how they intend to practically address those requirements) (87). The use of good engineering practice (GEP) also complements this strategy by providing a framework for the application of key concepts (e.g., project engineering, common practices, and operations and maintenance) (90). Examples include non-GxP compliance, design reviews, change management, equipment maintenance, and lifecycle management.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Facility Design Space（設施設計空間）— 指設施中可供 SUS 整合的物理和功能空間。這不僅是地板面積的問題，還包括潔淨度等級、公用設施配置、人員動線和物流動線的整體規劃。

RAT (Regulatory Assessment Table，法規評估表)— 一種實用工具，用於將法規要求與使用者的具體應對策略進行交叉對照。例如，針對 ICH Q7A 的某一條款，RAT 會記錄該條款的原文以及使用者計畫如何滿足該要求。

GEP (Good Engineering Practice，良好工程實務)— 為工程專案提供系統性框架的方法論，涵蓋專案工程、共通實務、營運和維護等面向。

重點提示 Key Notes

設施層級整合的 12 個參數清單非常重要，特別注意以下幾點：

  • Cross-contamination avoidance（避免交叉污染）— SUS 本身就是降低交叉污染風險的有效手段，但設施設計仍需考慮人員流動和物料流動的隔離
  • Process validation — 從 MUS 轉換到 SUS 時，即使製程相同，因設備型態改變（如體積比、攪拌方式）可能需要重新進行製程確效
  • Dependence on utilities — SUS 設施通常較不依賴 WFI、純蒸汽等公用設施，但對倉儲和廢棄物處理的需求增加

比喻說明 Analogy

設施層級整合就像在既有的社區中規劃一棟新建築。你不能只看建築本身的設計（SUS 設備），還必須考慮周圍的道路（物流動線）、供水電力（公用設施）、停車位（倉儲空間）、消防通道（安全規範）、鄰居的影響（交叉污染風險）以及市政法規（GMP 要求）。RAT 就是你用來逐條檢查建築法規是否符合的核對表。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 TR66 強調設施整合需要「holistic approach」（整體性方法）？如果只關注單一因素（如設備尺寸），可能會遺漏哪些風險？
  2. 請解釋 RAT 如何幫助 CDMO 在面對法規查核時快速展示合規策略。
7.4.6 Regulatory Assessment Table (RAT) Example

Table 7.4.6-1: Example of a Regulatory Assessment Table

ICH Q7A - Basic Requirements for Active Substances Used as Starting Materials: Specific Guidance for APIs Manufactured by Cell Culture/Fermentation

Section Excerpt from ICH Q7A User Policy for Meeting Each Requirement
18.30 "Where aseptic addition of cell substrates, media, buffers, and gases is needed; closed or contained systems should be used where possible. If the inoculation of the initial vessel or subsequent transfers or additions (media, buffers) are performed in open vessels, there should be controls and procedures in place to minimize the risk of contamination." All aseptic additions will be performed as closed processes within closed systems. SUS must be presterilized; MUS must have received a SIP treatment.
18.31 "Where the quality of the API can be affected by microbial contamination, manipulations using open vessels should be performed in a bio-safety cabinet or similarly controlled environment." A risk-based approach will be used to determine whether a particular manipulation might be affected by microbial contamination. If a process step is considered to be at particular risk, for example, where an open connection should be made, these open steps will always take place in a microbiological safety cabinet under EU-GMP Grade A with background Grade B conditions.
18.34 "Cell culture equipment should be cleaned and sterilized after use. As appropriate, fermentation equipment should be cleaned and sanitized or sterilized." Process equipment used for upstream production runs will be sourced as an SUS and, as such, will be used only once.
18.38 "Shared (multiproduct) equipment may warrant additional testing after cleaning between product campaigns, as appropriate, to minimize the risk of cross-contamination." Some equipment used in the production process may be an SUS-MUS hybrid. The CIP procedures for the MUS components (e.g., steel sampling valves) will consist of a decontamination step by SIP or autoclaving followed by a defined and controlled cleaning procedure. These processes will be validated.

This table is an example based on Chapter 18 of ICH Q7A (EU-GMP Part II) (2). Other regulatory texts can also be exploited in this manner. A RAT is used to cull the sections of a regulatory text that are most applicable to the project and to document the company's position with regard to each chosen paragraph. This helps to identify the key strategies or policies that may be required. A RAT can be a useful supplement as part of a risk-management-based approach to developing situations for facility-operating scenarios.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

RAT（法規評估表）的實際運作方式：

  • 左欄：列出法規原文的相關條款編號和內容
  • 右欄：記錄使用者（公司）針對每一條款的具體因應政策

這種「法規原文 vs 公司政策」的對照格式，讓查核員和內部團隊都能清楚看到每一項法規要求是如何被滿足的。

重點提示 Key Notes

注意 Table 7.4.6-1 中幾個重要的政策聲明：

  • 18.30 對應政策：所有無菌添加都在封閉系統中進行 — 這正是 SUS 的核心優勢
  • 18.31 對應政策：開放式連接必須在 EU-GMP Grade A + 背景 Grade B 環境下進行 — 這是典型的 SUS-MUS 混合操作的風險控制
  • 18.34 對應政策：上游製程設備使用 SUS，只使用一次 — 直接消除清潔確效的需求
  • 18.38 對應政策：混合系統中的 MUS 部件（如鋼製取樣閥）需要經過確效的 CIP 程序

實務應用 Practical Application

建議 CDMO 為每個新的 SUS 實施專案建立自己的 RAT。除了 ICH Q7A 之外，也可以針對以下法規建立 RAT：

  • EU GMP Annex 1（無菌藥品製造）
  • FDA 21 CFR 211（cGMP）
  • PIC/S GMP Guidelines
  • ICH Q8-Q12（品質設計與生命週期管理）

RAT 可以作為法規查核的「預防性準備工具」，也是跨部門溝通法規要求的統一語言。

7.4.7 Equipment-Level Integration Plan

Original Text

This brief document describes factors influencing the supplier or end user during the construction, marketing, and supply of the SUS as an off-the-shelf, customized, or self-made system. Some of the parameters for verification are:

  • Position in the product lifecycle and making sure that it is compatible with future GMP and quality systems
  • Working volumes
  • Transport conditions
  • Handling or moving the system, and protecting it during this process
  • Physical support (e.g., whether the system can support itself or requires a supporting structure)
  • Physical parameters
  • Flow rates for gases and liquids
  • Temperature range (e.g., cold storage to process conditions)
  • Heating and cooling requirements
  • Agitation and mixing
  • Pressure
  • Sterilization or chemical sanitation cycles
  • Chemical compatibilities (e.g., organic solvents, gas permeability)
  • Direct-impact phenomena (e.g., cellular growth kinetics)
  • Biocontainment capabilities
  • Standardization
  • Control systems and their validation
  • Autonomy [i.e., does the system require an uninterrupted power supply (UPS) in case of power failure?]

At S4, it is generally assumed that 1) sufficient process knowledge exists to enable a coherent review of the design factors that must be built into the SU, and 2) this would be performed from a risk-based perspective. Some of the most relevant design factors are:

  • Construction materials
  • Physical properties
  • Microbial control methods
  • Size and volume
  • Physical parameters
  • Direct-impact phenomena (e.g., contact time, E&L, biocompatibility)

For many end users, establishing a close partnership with major SUS suppliers allows them to leverage their extensive experience in the process field. Adopting customized SUS or using inexperienced suppliers would increase risk, although this may be mitigated by on-site SUS testing. The onus is on the end user to ascertain the compatibility of process, equipment, and facility design space from a risk-based perspective (Sections 7.4.10 and 7.7).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Equipment-Level Integration Plan（設備層級整合計畫）涵蓋 18 個驗證參數，這些參數可以分為幾大類：

  • 物理與機械：工作體積、壓力、溫度範圍、攪拌混合、物理支撐
  • 化學相容性：有機溶劑、氣體滲透性、化學消毒循環
  • 生物學影響：細胞生長動力學、生物圍阻能力
  • 物流與後勤：運輸條件、搬運保護
  • 系統整合：控制系統確效、不斷電系統 (UPS)、標準化

重點提示 Key Notes

S4 階段有兩個關鍵假設：(1) 已有足夠的製程知識，(2) 設計審查基於風險方法。這意味著如果製程知識不足就貿然進入 S4，可能導致設備規格不正確，後續的修改代價極高。

另一個重要觀點：與大型 SUS 供應商建立夥伴關係可以降低風險，因為他們有豐富的應用經驗。使用客製化 SUS 或經驗不足的供應商會增加風險，但可以透過現場測試來緩解。這對 CDMO 的供應商管理策略有直接影響。

比喻說明 Analogy

設備層級整合就像選購汽車引擎。你不能只看馬力（工作體積）這一個指標，還要考慮油耗（公用設施依賴）、排氣量（廢棄物產生）、散熱效率（加熱/冷卻需求）、耐用性（化學相容性）、安全氣囊（生物圍阻）、自動駕駛功能（控制系統）以及備用電池（UPS）。任何一個參數的疏忽都可能導致整台車無法正常運行。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在設備層級的 18 個驗證參數中，哪些參數對生物製劑的 SUS 特別關鍵？哪些對化學藥品的 SUS 更為重要？
  2. 為什麼 TR66 建議與「major SUS suppliers」建立夥伴關係，而非使用多家小型供應商？請從風險管理角度分析。
7.4.8 Operational-Level Integration Plan

Original Text

This describes the parameters for SUS integration (i.e., assembly, connection, and deployment) in readiness for manufacturing. A risk-based approach should be used because of the structural and functional diversity of SUSs (91). Some of the important parameters to consider during deployment include:

  • Packaging and container integrity — It must be determined whether preuse leak testing of SUS is feasible. Manufacturing, shipping, handling, and operational procedures should be qualified to maintain SUS integrity. This can be achieved by implementing control strategies within the end user's organization and between supplier and end user.
  • SUS testing and release — Testing and release vary with use. The same off-the-shelf system may have different test and release criteria depending on process-, product-, regulatory-, and user-imposed requirements.
  • Reuse of components — In general, reuse of SUSs is not recommended. The policy for this should have been established in the SUS strategy (Section 7.2.1.7). However, there are circumstances in which the reuse of SUS may be acceptable (e.g., use of a container as a mixing vessel or reservoir for buffer concentrates in which there are no broken connections). A risk analysis should be performed to determine if the risks are acceptable.
  • Training — Appropriate personnel training is essential because the collapse of a bag may lead to stress cracks that could result in a loss of structural and functional integrity. Training topics might include the use of different sterile connection and disconnection devices or techniques for avoiding bag creases or holes during deployment.
  • Shelf life — A coherent expiration and shelf-life policy should be implemented, especially in situations in which the end user has a large number of different SUSs from multiple suppliers or local, self-made assemblies.
  • Quality assurance — Ensuring quality during deployment should be addressed at an early stage of implementation. Technical diligence may enhance this goal (Section 7.4.10 and 7.7.3).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Operational-Level Integration（營運層級整合）是 SUS 從「靜態設備」變成「可用系統」的關鍵轉換點。六個重點參數涵蓋了 SUS 從到貨到上線使用的完整流程：

  • Preuse leak testing（使用前洩漏測試）— 確認 SUS 在運輸和儲存過程中未受損
  • Reuse policy（重複使用政策）— 原則上不建議重複使用，但在特定條件下（如未斷開連接的緩衝液容器）可接受
  • Technical diligence（技術盡職調查）— 對 SUS 產品、供應商和製程相容性的深入了解

重點提示 Key Notes

營運層級最容易被忽略但影響最大的是人員訓練。袋體的塌陷可能導致應力裂紋，進而破壞結構和功能完整性 — 這是一個非常實際的操作風險。培訓主題應包括：

  • 不同類型的無菌連接和斷開裝置的使用
  • 部署過程中避免袋體褶皺或孔洞的技巧
  • 正確的搬運姿勢和方法

對 CDMO 而言，操作人員的 SUS 專業訓練品質直接決定了產品品質和批次成功率。

比喻說明 Analogy

營運層級整合就像飛行員的起飛前檢查清單。不管飛機設計得多好（設備層級）、機場跑道多完美（設施層級），如果起飛前的儀器檢查（洩漏測試）、機組人員訓練（Training）、油料有效期（Shelf life）沒有到位，飛行安全就無法保障。每一項看似瑣碎的檢查項目，都可能是決定任務成敗的關鍵。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在什麼情況下，SUS 的重複使用可能是可接受的？使用者需要進行哪些風險分析？
  2. 為什麼同一款 off-the-shelf SUS 在不同應用中可能有不同的測試和放行標準？請舉例說明。
7.4.9 Technological Survey

Original Text

The aim of this document is to complement the information gathered as part of the manufacturing strategy (Sections 3.0, 7.0, and 7.1). Depending on when the manufacturing strategy is written, an update to the document may be necessary. However, if a greater level of information is obtained in S1 and entry into the full implementation process takes place at G4, then this survey can be omitted. Adaptations of the implementation road map are addressed in Section 7.1. However, if the organization of the road map is changed, care should be exercised that the implementation process does not lose structure and that the comprehensive treatment of all of the elements necessary remains in place.

The components for SUS implementation often come from a range of suppliers, and a SWOT-type assessment (i.e., strengths, weaknesses, opportunities, and threats) may be used to evaluate and compare solutions. The aim is to make sure that the best available technology is selected while also obtaining pertinent information for including any further requirements in the specification process. Sources of information may include:

  • Suppliers
  • In-house know-how
  • Industry networks and associations
  • Journals
  • Conferences
  • Industry guidelines

Suppliers may be considered as stakeholders.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Technological Survey（技術調查）是對市場上可用的 SUS 技術解決方案進行系統性調研。其目的是確保選擇最佳可用技術 (Best Available Technology, BAT)。

SWOT Assessment（SWOT 分析）在此用於評估和比較不同的 SUS 解決方案：

  • S (Strengths)：供應商的技術能力、產品成熟度
  • W (Weaknesses)：產品限制、化學相容性問題
  • O (Opportunities)：新技術、成本節省潛力
  • T (Threats)：供應鏈風險、專利限制

重點提示 Key Notes

技術調查可以在某些條件下省略 — 如果在 S1 階段已取得足夠的技術資訊。但如果實施路線圖的組織架構有所改變，必須確保實施流程不會失去結構性，所有必要元素的完整處理仍然到位。這個警告在 TR66 中多次出現，顯示實務中組織架構調整導致品質遺漏是常見問題。

比喻說明 Analogy

技術調查就像買房前的市場調研。你會查看不同建商的口碑（Suppliers）、問住過的朋友的經驗（In-house know-how）、參加房展會（Conferences）、閱讀建築雜誌（Journals）、加入購屋社群（Industry networks）。SWOT 分析則是你在幾個候選物件之間做比較時的決策工具。

7.4.10 Supplier Selection and Supply-Chain Review

Original Text

The aim of this review is to determine a policy for the identification and selection of suppliers in order to complete the PEP and project planning.

The selection of appropriate SUS suppliers can often be an arduous task that can be made less cumbersome with a risk-management approach. For a successful SUS implementation, it is essential to have a detailed and transparent relationship between suppliers, vendors, and the end user. This requires good communication and understanding of stakeholder management in order to garner the expectations of both the suppliers and the end users. Being able to share pertinent information with suppliers at the early stages of the project may speed up the design process. Note that in order to obtain full benefits from this approach, the exchange of uni- or bilateral confidential disclosure agreements (CDA) may be required. The implementation and management of an end user–supplier relationship via technical diligence is described in Section 7.7.3. Suppliers provide material data, advice on applying typical designs, and the following documents:

  • Process flow diagrams (PFDs)
  • Piping and Instrumentation Diagrams (P&IDs)
  • Component lists
  • Physical layout proposals
  • Operation manuals
  • Pricing
  • Qualification packages, including guidelines on E&L, for example

For both large companies and SMEs, it is critical to prevent the selection of equipment and suppliers from becoming an ad hoc process because that can lead to unnecessary and costly redundancies. In addition, working with too many suppliers may divert limited resources that could otherwise be gainfully employed in other parts of the SUS implementation process. Since the degree of business integration of a particular SUS supplier may depend on the size, location, and SUS assembly concerned, it is important to adopt a risk-mitigation approach to SUS supplier qualification and validation (Section 7.7.3).

Starting materials such as resins and films should be treated as critical raw materials as part of the verification process due to the complexity of SUS implementation (18). It is important to begin the supplier technical diligence (i.e., obtaining a thorough understanding of the SUS product, supplier, and compatibility of the SUS with the end user's process and facility) at this stage. These principles are based on established procedures for critical raw materials as recommended by the Association for Professionals in Infection Control and Epidemiology (APIC) due diligence process, ASTM E2500-07 vendor technical capability as part of the PVV process (Figure 7.2.7.1-1), and quality by design (QbD)-inspired raw materials qualification processes (18,92–94). Full details on how to implement the technical diligence process are described in Section 7.7.3. Note that this task may require the exchange of uni- or bilateral CDAs or nondisclosure agreements (NDA).

The quality of the entire supply chain should be assessed, qualified, and implemented via a structured risk-management process (72). All parties in the supply chain should make sure that their activities maintain business continuity and support the health of patients. SUS equipment that is purchased occasionally may be done on a contractual basis, but a quality and supply agreement must be used to buy routine SUS equipment (Sections 7.5.7 and 7.7.12).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Technical Diligence（技術盡職調查）— 這是 TR66 中的核心概念之一。它不僅僅是供應商稽核，而是對 SUS 產品本身、供應商的技術能力以及 SUS 與使用者製程和設施的相容性進行全面深入的了解。基礎概念源自 APIC 盡職調查流程和 ASTM E2500-07。

CDA/NDA（保密協議）— 為了實現供應商與使用者之間的資訊透明交流，可能需要簽署單向或雙向保密協議。這在早期專案階段特別重要，可以加速設計流程。

Quality and Supply Agreement（品質與供應協議）— 用於常規 SUS 設備採購的正式合約，涵蓋品質標準、供應條款和變更通知等。臨時性採購可以用一般合約，但常規採購必須有品質供應協議。

重點提示 Key Notes

供應商選擇的兩個核心風險：

  • Ad hoc selection（隨意選擇）— 設備和供應商的選擇不能是臨時起意的過程。這會導致不必要的重複採購和成本浪費，不論公司規模大小都可能發生。
  • Too many suppliers（過多供應商）— 與太多供應商合作會分散有限的資源。供應商管理本身就需要投入大量時間和人力，過多的供應商會壓縮用於 SUS 實施其他環節的資源。

TR66 強調「起始物料（如樹脂和薄膜）應被視為關鍵原材料」— 這意味著它們需要與 API 起始物料同等級的管控和審查。

比喻說明 Analogy

供應商選擇與管理就像組建一支 F1 賽車團隊。你需要精心挑選引擎供應商（核心 SUS 供應商）、輪胎供應商（薄膜和配件供應商）和燃料供應商（樹脂等原材料）。與太多供應商合作就像賽車有太多不同品牌的零件 — 整合成本暴增、故障排除困難。而 Technical Diligence 就是你在簽約前對每個供應商進行的徹底試車和技術評估。CDA 則是賽車隊之間保護技術機密的協議。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 TR66 將 SUS 的樹脂和薄膜歸類為「critical raw materials」？這對供應商管理策略有什麼影響？
  2. 臨時性 SUS 採購和常規 SUS 採購在合約要求上有什麼不同？為什麼常規採購必須有 Quality and Supply Agreement？
  3. 在 CDMO 環境中，如何平衡「減少供應商數量」與「維持供應鏈韌性」之間的矛盾？
7.4.11 Extractables and Leachables Database

Original Text

It may be convenient for the end user to begin collecting E&L guidance and testing data. Note that this can also be implemented in the next stage, Implementation S5: Development. At a minimum, however, the end user should collect extractables data at this stage.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

E&L Database（萃取物與溶出物資料庫）— E&L 是 SUS 實施中最重要的安全性考量之一：

  • Extractables（萃取物）— 在加嚴條件下從 SUS 材料中萃取出的化合物
  • Leachables（溶出物）— 在正常製程條件下從 SUS 材料遷移到產品中的化合物

TR66 建議最遲在 S4 階段開始收集 Extractables 資料，Leachables 資料可以延後到 S5 階段收集。

重點提示 Key Notes

雖然這一小節篇幅簡短，但 E&L 的重要性不容小覷。及早建立 E&L 資料庫有以下好處：(1) 在供應商選擇階段就能排除不適合的材料；(2) 為後續的規格制定和確效提供基礎數據；(3) 法規申報時需要完整的 E&L 數據。對 CDMO 而言，系統化的 E&L 資料庫是跨客戶專案的重要資產。

7.5 Implementation S5: Development

Original Text

During this stage, the SUS user requirements are developed, including layout and design, specifications, and standardization. Complete user requirements should precede the procurement process (e.g., commercial negotiations between strategic project partners or raising a purchase order).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Implementation S5: Development（開發階段）— 在 S4 的商業案例建立之後，S5 聚焦於將策略轉化為具體的使用者需求文件。此階段的關鍵輸出包括：使用者需求 (User Requirements)、佈局與設計、規格書 (Specifications) 和標準化政策。重要的是，完整的使用者需求必須在採購流程之前完成。

重點提示 Key Notes

S5 的核心原則：先定義需求，再開始採購。在實務中，很多組織因為時程壓力而跳過完整的需求定義直接進入採購，結果往往導致規格不匹配、變更訂單增加和專案延誤。這個順序不可顛倒。

7.5.1 User Requirements for Implementation

Original Text

User requirements should be prepared at the start of the development process. The principal user and stakeholders must be identified and their requirements obtained. The user requirements are based on product and process knowledge, critical quality attributes, and any relevant regulatory requirements. The principal user should also provide the justifications for the resources required to design, purchase, qualify, and implement any new process, system, or equipment. These justifications can be developed prior to selecting an SUS or supplier, or they may be developed for a particular system. Some or all of the requirements can be based on a QbD approach. In this case, the product and process-control strategy performed earlier in the QbD process will become a prerequisite for defining the SUS requirements.

User requirements and functional specifications may be recorded together in a single document for low-risk, small-scale SUS. However, multiple user requirements may be needed for complex systems or processes. In this case, it would be critical to avoid conflicts across multiple documents. Any necessary conflicts must be identified and documented. The user requirements are created by the end user or on the end user's behalf; however, some supplier documentation may be necessary to supplement this. Supplier documentation is acceptable if the supplier follows GEP (90), has an appropriate quality system, and is technically capable according to ASTM E2500-07 and PDA Technical Report No. 60: Process Validation — A Lifecycle Approach (8,18). In some cases, the supplier documentation could replace the company document. The user requirements are kept current throughout the system's lifecycle and should be reevaluated after any change in intended use, user needs, or altered materials specifications (e.g., the films used, functional specifications, regulatory assessments or supplier quality audits, technical diligence). An example of a user requirements document is included in Section 8, Appendix 1.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

User Requirements（使用者需求）— SUS 實施的基礎文件，基於三大支柱：

  • 產品與製程知識— 了解產品特性和製程參數
  • CQA（關鍵品質屬性）— 影響產品安全性和有效性的品質特性
  • 法規要求— 適用的 GMP 和法規規範

使用者需求可以採用 QbD（品質源於設計）方法，將產品和製程控制策略作為定義 SUS 需求的前提條件。

重點提示 Key Notes

使用者需求文件的管理有幾個重要原則：

  • 文件複雜度應匹配風險等級：低風險小規模 SUS 可以將需求和功能規格合併在一份文件中；複雜系統則需要多份文件，但必須避免文件之間的衝突
  • 供應商文件可以補充甚至替代公司文件：前提是供應商遵循 GEP、有適當的品質系統、並符合 ASTM E2500-07 的技術能力要求
  • 使用者需求是活文件：必須在系統生命週期中保持更新，任何用途變更、使用者需求變更或材料規格變更都需要重新評估

比喻說明 Analogy

使用者需求文件就像訂製西裝前的量身記錄。你必須先測量身材數據（產品和製程知識）、了解穿著場合（CQA）、確認禮儀規範（法規要求），然後才能讓裁縫（供應商）開始製作。如果你讓三個裁縫分別做上衣、褲子和背心，必須確保尺寸規格不會互相矛盾（避免多文件衝突）。而且，如果你增重或減重了（製程變更），量身數據就需要更新。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在什麼條件下，供應商的文件可以替代終端使用者自己編寫的使用者需求文件？
  2. 如果 CDMO 的客戶變更了產品配方（例如更換緩衝液組成），使用者需求文件中哪些部分需要重新評估？
7.5.2 Preparing User Requirements

Original Text

Brainstorming sessions, workshops, interviews, assessments, and ad hoc discussions may be used to gather pertinent information about the needs of the end user. Other useful information may be obtained from suppliers, case histories, and workflow analyses. These requirements may not be fully defined initially but may be developed further during subsequent phases of the project. It is crucial to determine the level of interest of each stakeholder has in the project and ensure that stakeholders receive adequate and regular communications throughout the SUS process lifecycle. User requirements statements must be written to a level of specificity that:

  • Describes the SUS function
  • Allows end users to verify that the system meets their functional requirements
  • Addresses the compatibility of processes and materials (e.g., polymer films)

However, they must be general enough to avoid constraining the system design. If a supplier will provide specific functionality, then the user requirements must be specific enough to determine that functionality.

Any particular safety concerns and training needs resulting from the requirements should be noted for later implementation. Finally, make sure that a change-control process is in place for this process.

A functional risk-assessment approach may be used for further evaluation of critical requirements for the quality and function of the SUS. For instance, if an integrated SUS is composed of components from multiple sources, it may be necessary to identify the CQA of each component. An example would be a bioreactor system in which the hardware and SUS bags are sourced from different suppliers. Requirements that are not deemed to satisfy CQA may be further evaluated to determine whether they express a regulatory requirement or not. The project team may apply other criteria such as priority, clinical development stage, importance to the business, and other factors that may influence company decisions.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

使用者需求的撰寫是一門平衡的藝術，需要在兩個極端之間取得平衡：

  • 足夠具體：能描述 SUS 功能、可驗證是否滿足需求、涵蓋製程與材料相容性
  • 足夠概括：不會限制系統設計的彈性空間

Functional Risk Assessment（功能性風險評估）可用於進一步評估關鍵需求。例如，一個整合型 SUS 由多個來源的組件組成時（如生物反應器硬體和 SUS 袋來自不同供應商），需要識別每個組件的 CQA。

重點提示 Key Notes

需求收集的方法多元：腦力激盪、工作坊、訪談、評估和非正式討論。TR66 特別指出需求可能「最初並非完全定義」而在後續階段進一步開發 — 這反映了 SUS 實施的迭代本質。

同時注意兩個關鍵提醒：

  • 必須有變更管控流程來管理使用者需求的變更
  • 必須確保利害關係人在整個 SUS 生命週期中獲得充分且定期的溝通

比喻說明 Analogy

撰寫使用者需求就像訂披薩：你需要說「我要一個 12 吋的瑪格麗特披薩，不要洋蔥」（具體到可以驗證），但不需要說「麵團必須用 00 號義大利麵粉，水溫 38 度，發酵時間 24 小時」（太具體會限制廚師的專業發揮）。如果你對特定供應商有特殊的功能需求（例如無麩質），那就必須明確寫出來。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 使用者需求如何在「足夠具體」和「足夠概括」之間取得平衡？請以 SUS 混合袋為例說明。
  2. 當一個整合型 SUS 由多個供應商提供組件時，功能性風險評估應如何進行？
7.5.3 Layout and Design

Original Text

The layout and design of the SUS can often be achieved using a standard design format; however, in certain cases, process-specific requirements may result in the need for a unique design process (refer to Section 4). A structured approach like the one from the S88 batch-automation standard may be used to attain completeness of design and control over interfaces because it focuses on the actual batch operations (95). This approach examines three key elements:

  • Operations
  • Equipment (reusable parts)
  • Consumable materials (SU parts)

Start the design process with the functional requirements of the SUS in mind. Figure 7.5.3-1 provides an example of a scope drawing, and the accompanying listing below shows typical considerations for designing a generic SUS within this context.

[Figure 7.5.3-1: Example of SUS Installation Scope Drawing]

This schematic representation of the flow path of an SUS facility shows that design meets both spatial requirements and container staging.

Typical Considerations:

Operations

  • Transportation, delivery, and installation
  • Process operations
  • Ergonomics
  • Sufficient space for operations
  • Manufacturing operations, including the following staging processes: Setting up, Charging, Processing, Feeding, Discharging, Storing, Dismantling

Equipment (Reusable Parts)

  • Bag support
  • Control system
  • Heating/cooling device
  • Pumps
  • Scales
  • Tables
  • Layout (i.e., the physical arrangement)

Materials (SU Parts)

  • Process-containing part (e.g., bag, cartridge, capsule, membrane)
  • Volume
  • Agitation
  • Footprint
  • Sampling
  • Sensors
  • Inlets and outlets
  • Films
  • Tubing
  • Connectors

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

S88 Batch-Automation Standard（S88 批次自動化標準）— 這是 ISA（國際自動化學會）的標準，提供了一個結構化的方法來設計和控制批次製造流程。TR66 借用這個標準的框架來確保 SUS 設計的完整性，將設計拆分為三個關鍵元素：

  • Operations（操作）— 從運輸安裝到製造操作的完整流程
  • Equipment（設備 - 可重複使用部件）— 袋體支架、控制系統、泵浦等
  • Materials（材料 - 一次性部件）— 袋體、管路、連接器等

重點提示 Key Notes

Layout and Design 的「Typical Considerations」清單是 SUS 設計的實用檢查表。特別注意：

  • Ergonomics（人因工程）— SUS 操作通常比 MUS 需要更多的手動操作（如袋體安裝、管路連接），人因工程設計直接影響操作效率和錯誤率
  • Staging processes（分階段流程）— 從 Setting up 到 Dismantling 的七個步驟定義了 SUS 的完整使用週期
  • SU parts 中的 Sensors（感測器）— 一次性感測器（如 pH、DO 探頭）是 SUS 中技術挑戰較大的部分

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 的佈局設計就像設計一個組合式行動廚房（用於大型戶外宴會）。Operations 是整個烹飪流程（從食材搬運到上菜撤盤）；Equipment 是可以反覆使用的設備（瓦斯爐、工作台、冰箱）；Materials 是每次使用後丟棄的物品（鋁箔紙、保鮮膜、烘焙紙）。S88 標準的方法論確保你不會只設計了廚房但忘了規劃從停車場到廚房的搬運動線。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 TR66 建議使用 S88 批次自動化標準的框架來進行 SUS 設計？這個標準如何確保「設計完整性」？
  2. 在 SUS 的 Layout and Design 中，人因工程 (Ergonomics) 為什麼特別重要？請舉一個因為人因設計不佳導致操作失敗的潛在情境。
7.5.4 Specification

Original Text

The design process produces a series of specifications for the proposed SUS. The user requirements cover both MU and SU parts and can be communicated through the following means:

  • Descriptive text
  • Calculation
  • Diagrams, drawings, and PFDs
  • Reference to existing equipment

Implementation of a periodic design review procedure is critical for success. The delivery and installation process must be examined carefully to ensure that the SUS will be delivered in a form that will integrate into the facility.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Specifications（規格書）是設計流程的具體產出，將使用者需求轉化為可測量、可驗證的技術要求。規格的表達方式包括：描述性文字、計算結果、圖表和流程圖、以及與現有設備的參照比較。

Periodic Design Review（定期設計審查）是確保設計持續符合需求的關鍵機制。特別要注意 SUS 的交付和安裝過程 — 必須確保 SUS 以能整合進設施的形式交付。

重點提示 Key Notes

規格書涵蓋 MU 和 SU 兩個部分 — 這很重要，因為 SUS 系統通常是混合系統（MU 硬體 + SU 組件），規格必須同時考慮兩者。定期設計審查的目的是在發現問題時能及早糾正，避免在製造完成後才發現設計不符合需求，導致昂貴的返工。

7.5.5 Standardization Policy

Original Text

Although the inherent flexibility at the core of SUS design is an advantage, it could degenerate into a disadvantage by introducing unwelcome variations in the supply chain if left unchecked. Therefore, introducing a standard design policy across the project may reduce the incidence of variations, especially as the scale of operations becomes more complex. Implement a standardization policy as part of the user requirements according to the following guidelines:

  • Working volumes may be chosen so that bag ranges cover a series of application ranges.
  • Connections and material on bags and tubing may be chosen so that several possibilities for connecting are maintained (e.g., providing weldable tubing and a typical connector together).
  • Setting up an SU toolbox consisting of Y pieces, sample manifolds, and lengths of tubing for special or infrequent applications will allow a more specific design element to be attached to a more standardized bag design.
  • An active standardization policy may have been defined as part of the SUS strategy (Section 7.2.1). If so, it may not be necessary to implement it at this stage.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Standardization Policy（標準化政策）是控制 SUS 設計彈性所帶來的供應鏈變異的關鍵策略。TR66 提出三種實用的標準化方法：

  • Bag ranges（袋體範圍系列化）— 選擇標準化的工作體積，讓一系列的袋體規格能涵蓋多種應用需求
  • Connection standardization（連接標準化）— 統一袋體和管路的連接方式，同時保留多種連接可能性
  • SU Toolbox（一次性工具箱）— 建立標準化的附件庫（Y 型接頭、取樣歧管、管路段），讓特殊需求可以透過附件附加到標準化袋體設計上

比喻說明 Analogy

標準化政策就像 LEGO 積木的設計理念。LEGO 的偉大之處在於用有限數量的標準化零件（標準的凸點間距和尺寸）來實現無限的組合可能。SU Toolbox 就是你的「特殊零件盒」— 當標準零件無法滿足需求時，你可以從中取出 Y 型接頭或取樣歧管來擴展功能。這比為每個應用訂製全新的設計要高效得多。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 的靈活性是雙面刃：優點是可以快速客製化，缺點是如果不加控制，每個操作者或每個專案都可能創建不同的設計，導致供應鏈變異激增、庫存管理困難、人員訓練成本上升。標準化政策的核心目標是「在保持必要彈性的同時，最大化可重複性和可預測性」。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果一家 CDMO 在不同客戶專案中使用了 15 種不同的 SUS 袋體設計，這會帶來哪些管理挑戰？標準化政策如何幫助解決？
  2. 「SU Toolbox」的概念如何在保持標準化的同時滿足特殊應用需求？
7.5.6 Extractables and Leachables

Original Text

In some cases, an E&L database collection may have begun in S4 (Sections 5.6 and 7.4.11). If not, E&L data should be compiled now. Although there is no specific regulatory guidance document for E&L in SU systems, the USP, FDA, and EMA have extensive E&L guidance documents for SU technology (96–100). In addition, a number of cross-industry initiatives are in place to standardize the approach for SUS and achieve industry and regulatory consensus or provide a cross-industry database of current knowledge (100–102).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

E&L 的法規環境在 2014 年（TR66 出版時）尚無 SUS 專屬的法規指引文件，但 USP、FDA 和 EMA 有針對一次性技術的廣泛 E&L 指引。業界也有多項跨產業標準化倡議，致力於：

  • 統一 SUS 的 E&L 評估方法
  • 達成產業和法規共識
  • 建立跨產業的知識資料庫

重點提示 Key Notes

如果 E&L 資料庫在 S4 尚未開始建立，S5 是最後的建立時機。E&L 數據的收集需要時間，且可能影響材料選擇和設計決策。越早開始收集，越能減少後期發現材料不適用而需要重新設計的風險。

7.5.7 Procurement

Original Text

Although procurement procedures will differ from company to company, it is critical to make sure that the end user requirements and other relevant specifications are correctly used and that the SUS-based equipment adheres to those specifications. It is important to maintain a close partnership between suppliers and end users in order to facilitate the procurement process. Some of the key points to consider are as follows:

  • The main procurement process will be outlined and planned in the PEP.
  • Key stakeholders must be identified and their roles and responsibilities must be clearly defined. This is extremely important in cases where procurement precedes the implementation of a quality and supply agreement.
  • Contractual issues must be clearly defined. The end user's legal team should have reviewed and, if necessary, negotiated any modification(s) to the supplier's general terms and conditions of sale to ensure that the user's business, financial, and operational expectations are met (e.g., compliance with Incoterms 2011) (103).
  • Good project planning and management principles must be carefully followed so that the project remains on track throughout its life.
  • A change-notification process should be in place between the equipment supplier and the end user in order to monitor any design changes that take place at this point.
  • Appropriate verifications must be conducted and the acceptance criteria met on a timely basis in order to avoid unnecessary delays.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Procurement（採購）是將使用者需求和規格書轉化為實際訂單的關鍵步驟。TR66 列出六個關鍵考量：

  • PEP 中的採購規劃— 採購流程應在 PEP 中預先規劃
  • 利害關係人的角色與責任— 特別是在品質供應協議尚未建立時
  • 合約條款— 包括 Incoterms（國際貿易條件）的遵守
  • 專案管理— 確保專案時程不脫軌
  • Change-Notification Process（變更通知流程）— 監控供應商端的設計變更
  • 驗收標準的及時驗證— 避免不必要的延誤

重點提示 Key Notes

採購流程中最關鍵的風險控制點是變更通知流程。SUS 供應商可能在採購期間變更材料、設計或製程，如果沒有正式的變更通知機制，終端使用者可能在不知情的情況下收到與原始規格不同的產品。這對產品品質和法規合規性有重大影響。

另一個容易被忽視的重點：合約條款中的 Incoterms（國際貿易條件）定義了運輸過程中風險和費用的分擔方式。SUS 在運輸過程中特別脆弱（薄膜材料容易受損），選擇正確的 Incoterms 條款可以明確責任歸屬。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 採購就像訂製精密的醫療器材。你不能只簽一張訂單然後等貨到 — 你需要持續監控製造商是否按照你的規格生產（驗收驗證）、是否偷偷換了原材料（變更通知流程）、運輸過程中是否妥善保護（Incoterms）、以及如果有爭議該怎麼處理（合約條款）。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 的採購部門應建立 SUS 專屬的採購 SOP，涵蓋：

  • 採購前的需求確認和規格審查流程
  • 與供應商的變更通知協議模板
  • 到貨驗收的標準檢查清單
  • 不符合規格時的處理程序（退貨、讓步接受等）
  • 緊急採購的授權和簡化流程

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果 SUS 供應商在製造過程中變更了薄膜材料但未通知終端使用者，可能造成哪些後果？
  2. 為什麼 TR66 強調在品質供應協議建立之前，利害關係人的角色與責任定義「extremely important」？

章節銜接說明

  • 本節（Section 5b）涵蓋 Implementation S4（商業案例）和 S5（開發）的完整內容（7.4-7.5, p88-p99）
  • 本節將與 Section 5c 合併，後者將接續涵蓋 Implementation S6-S7 等後續實施階段
  • PEP、使用者需求和採購流程的概念將在後續章節中被持續引用和深化
PDA Technical Report No. 66 — Single-Use Systems (2014) | p100 - p107

本章學習目標

  • 理解 SUS 實施階段 S6（測試與驗證）中交付、安裝、確效、訓練與安全的完整流程
  • 掌握 S7（啟動上線）中供應商管理、常規採購與技術盡職調查 (Technical Diligence) 的關鍵要素
  • 學習 HSE（健康、安全與環境）計畫在 SUS 專案中的制定與執行
  • 了解品質與技術協議、物流倉儲策略在維持 SUS 持續營運中的角色
  • 區分品質稽核 (Quality Audit) 與技術盡職調查 (Technical Diligence) 的目的與範疇差異

7.6 Implementation S6: Testing and Validation

Original Text

During this stage, methods and documentation must be developed for equipment SOPs, maintenance, qualification and process validation, HSE processes, and personnel training. Some documents (e.g., the validation master plan) may require updates at this stage to maintain compliance.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Implementation S6 (實施階段 S6)：這是 SUS 專案從設計走向實際運作的關鍵轉折點。此階段需要完成所有設備 SOP、維護計畫、確效與驗證文件、HSE（健康安全環境）流程以及人員訓練的建立。

Validation Master Plan (驗證主計畫)：此文件統領整個驗證活動，在 S6 階段可能需要因應新的 SUS 設備資訊進行更新，以確保法規合規性。

比喻說明 Analogy

S6 階段就像新餐廳開幕前的「試營運」期。菜單（SOP）已擬定、廚房設備（SUS 硬體）已到位，現在要實際測試每道菜的流程是否順暢、廚師是否熟悉操作、消防設備是否合格。所有細節必須在正式開幕（S7 啟動）前確認完畢。

7.6.1 Delivery (交付)

Original Text

The PEP must cover the delivery process, including responsibilities of the supplier and the end user. Transport logistics are sometimes complex, and the procedure by which the equipment will be safely shipped (transported) and unloaded from its delivery vehicle must be considered. Some suppliers do not take unloading into account, and the end user may need to take particular precautions here or ensure that the supplier contractually takes responsibility. There may be specific non-GxP issues to resolve such as documentation (delivery notes), inspection for inventory or damage, and insurance or the removal and appropriate disposal of crates and other packaging materials.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PEP (Process Engineering Plan，製程工程計畫)：PEP 是貫穿 SUS 實施全過程的主文件，必須涵蓋交付流程中供應商與最終使用者各自的責任。

交付階段看似簡單，實則暗藏許多風險：運輸損壞、卸貨責任歸屬不明、包裝廢棄物處理等。這些雖屬 non-GxP 範疇，但若處理不當，會延誤整個專案時程。

重點提示 Key Notes

許多供應商的基本報價不包含卸貨服務！最終使用者必須在合約中明確約定卸貨責任歸屬，否則可能面臨額外成本與延誤。務必在 PEP 中加入交付驗收檢查清單：交貨單核對、外觀損壞檢查、庫存登記與保險索賠程序。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果供應商的報價不含卸貨服務，你會如何在合約中保護最終使用者的權益？
  2. 大型 SUS 設備運輸時，可能遇到哪些物流挑戰？你會如何提前規劃？

7.6.2 Installation (安裝)

Original Text

The PEP will also cover all aspects of the startup process, including post-delivery storage, handling prior to installation unpacking, and the responsibilities of the supplier and the end user in a more general manner. Transferring the equipment to its place of use can be problematic if equipment dimensions or facility access has not been reviewed in advance. Preparing the area, particularly in cases where the SUS equipment will be used in manufacturing operations, may require specific training. The overall strategy and approach will depend on the nature of the SUS and the level of risk associated with this process (Section 7.4.1). In some cases, non-GxP documentation may be generated or supplied and work permits (e.g., fire safety) secured during the installation processes (e.g., removals).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Installation (安裝)：安裝不只是把設備放到定位。從交付後的暫存、拆箱前的處理、到搬運至使用地點，每一步都需要計畫。特別是設備尺寸與設施通道的預先評估，若忽略此步驟，可能會發生設備無法進入廠房的窘境。

比喻說明 Analogy

這就像買了一台大型冰箱送到新家，結果發現電梯太小、門框太窄，根本無法搬進廚房。在製藥廠房中，這種情況造成的延誤和成本遠比家用設備嚴重。提前量測設備尺寸與所有通道寬度，是最基本卻最常被忽略的步驟。

重點提示 Key Notes

在 GMP 製造區域進行安裝時，可能需要：(1) 特定的人員訓練；(2) 動火許可等工作許可證；(3) 拆除舊設備的 non-GxP 文件記錄。安裝策略應依據風險評估結果（Section 7.4.1）來制定。

7.6.3 Qualification (確效)

Original Text

Qualification of an SUS should include lifecycle testing that reproduces the most impactful steps of the system's lifecycle (e.g., sterilization, transport, freezing/thawing) followed by a verification of the key functionalities and performance attributes (e.g., integrity testing). The lifecycle testing must be designed to cover the intended working space. Please refer to Sections 5 and 7.7 for a discussion of the SUS qualification process and supplier qualification, respectively.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Lifecycle Testing (生命週期測試)：不是只測試 SUS 在「完美狀態」下的表現，而是模擬其整個使用生命週期中最具衝擊性的步驟——例如滅菌、運輸震盪、凍融循環——然後再驗證關鍵功能（如完整性測試）是否仍然合格。

Integrity Testing (完整性測試)：確認 SUS 在經歷生命週期壓力後，系統的密封性與屏障功能仍然完好。這是確保產品無菌保證的關鍵步驟。

重點提示 Key Notes

確效測試必須涵蓋「預期工作空間 (intended working space)」，意即不能只在最佳條件下測試，還必須涵蓋邊界條件與最壞情境。這與 ICH Q8 中 Design Space 的概念相呼應。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 SUS 確效必須包含生命週期測試，而不只是靜態的功能測試？
  2. 請列舉三個 SUS 生命週期中「最具衝擊性」的步驟，並說明它們可能造成的風險。

7.6.4 Training (訓練)

Original Text

Training is a GMP requirement and an integral part of SUS technical implementation. The goal of any training program should be to provide specific knowledge and understanding that will support successful operations. Although, the specific training needs are normally described in the user requirements, other training requirements (e.g., for project management and risk assessment) may be critical for the successful implementation of the project. Training programs for SUS should include concepts and principles of operation that might be unique to SUS and unfamiliar to MUS operators.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Training (訓練)：訓練是 GMP 的硬性要求，也是 SUS 技術實施不可或缺的環節。重點不只是「怎麼操作」，更包括專案管理與風險評估等軟技能。

MUS (Multi-Use System，多次使用系統)：傳統不鏽鋼設備。SUS 的操作概念與 MUS 有根本差異，習慣 MUS 的操作人員需要「重新學習」SUS 的獨特原理。

比喻說明 Analogy

從 MUS 轉換到 SUS，就像從手排車換到電動車。雖然都是「開車」，但煞車回饋、加速特性、充電（而非加油）等概念完全不同。如果只告訴電動車駕駛「跟以前一樣開就好」，一定會出問題。同理，MUS 操作員必須接受 SUS 專屬訓練。

7.6.5 Training Workflow (訓練工作流程)

Original Text

Guidelines for a training workflow are as follows:

  • Examine each part of the entire SUS PEP individually and identify the functional areas concerned.
  • Identify the training needs in each functional area and assign stakeholders.
  • Assemble training requirements in a training matrix (example in Section 10, Appendix 3).
  • Determine the scope of each training module. Some subjects may require more than one level of presentation and may require periodic retraining.
  • Make sure that a trainee assessment or evaluation process is included at the end of the training module; this is a GMP requirement.
  • Take the resources as well as the subject and complexity of the training requirement into account when planning training procedures.
  • Some training modules may be delivered by competent team members or operators who are familiar with SUS implementation. Other training modules may be delivered by suppliers.
  • Add completed training modules to the individual training records of each stakeholder.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Training Matrix (訓練矩陣)：將每個功能領域的訓練需求與相關利害關係人對應起來的表格工具。確保沒有人被遺漏、沒有主題被忽略。

重點提示 Key Notes

訓練工作流程的核心原則：

  • 完整性：逐一檢視 PEP 的每個部分，辨識所有需要訓練的功能領域
  • 分級制：某些主題需要多層次的訓練，且需要定期複訓
  • 評估機制：每個訓練模組結束後必須有考核評估——這是 GMP 的強制要求
  • 記錄追蹤：完成的訓練必須記錄在個人訓練檔案中

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 環境中，操作人員可能同時處理多個客戶的不同 SUS 平台。訓練矩陣的設計必須考慮到：(1) 通用 SUS 基礎知識；(2) 特定客戶/產品的操作程序；(3) 跨平台差異的認知訓練。供應商提供的訓練模組可以節省內部資源，但必須確保其內容符合公司的 GMP 標準。

7.6.6 An Example of SUS Training (SUS 訓練範例)

Original Text

Factors that may contribute to the leakage of bags are:

  • Poor handling during deployment
  • Mechanical stress on films or welds
  • Accidental puncture or stressing of the SUS during handling and setup

Incidences of bag leakage may be reduced through the following interventions:

  • Changing storage bin and bag design, if appropriate
  • Optimizing the method of deployment (i.e., installation)
  • Providing operational training
  • Providing bag-handling awareness training
  • Implementing a control strategy (e.g., remedial procedures by the supplier)
  • Monitoring location and type of bag damage for trending

The in-house training program should be based on operational parameters and operator feedback. Operators should be educated and engaged about:

  • Working areas and surfaces
  • Bag installation and filling
  • Prior root causes for failure
  • Leakage history and trends
  • Root-cause analyses

Additional details on training are provided in Section 6.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Bag Leakage (袋體洩漏)：SUS 最常見也最令人頭痛的問題之一。洩漏不僅造成產品損失，更可能危及無菌保證。本節從「原因分析」到「預防介入」提供了完整的訓練框架。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 袋體就像手術室中的無菌手套——材質本身很耐用，但若拿取方式不當（指甲刮到、拉扯過猛），就會破損。訓練操作人員正確的「袋體處理意識」，就像訓練外科醫師正確穿戴手套一樣重要。

重點提示 Key Notes

防止袋體洩漏的六大介入措施中，「操作訓練」和「袋體處理意識訓練」是最具成本效益的。根據產業經驗，大部分的袋體損壞都是人為操作不當造成的，而非材料缺陷。因此，建立「操作人員回饋→根因分析→趨勢監控」的持續改善迴路至關重要。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你的工廠在過去三個月內發生了五次袋體洩漏事件，你會如何設計一個訓練改善方案？
  2. 為什麼操作人員的「意識訓練」比單純的「操作步驟訓練」更加重要？

7.6.7 Safety (安全)

Original Text

Health and safety issues involving the control of both recognized and unidentified hazards in order to achieve an acceptable level of risk in the workplace are the responsibility of all stakeholders. Ensuring safety in the workplace as required by local laws can be best addressed by preparing an HSE plan.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

HSE Plan (健康、安全與環境計畫)：一份系統性的文件，涵蓋專案全程的健康、安全與環境關注事項。HSE 計畫是所有利害關係人的共同責任，不僅要管理「已知風險」，更要考慮「未辨識的風險」。

重點提示 Key Notes

安全不是某個部門的責任——「the responsibility of all stakeholders」（所有利害關係人的責任）。在 SUS 專案中，由於涉及大量手動操作（搬運、安裝、拆卸），安全風險可能比傳統 MUS 更為複雜多變。

7.6.8 Preparation of a Health, Safety, and Environment Plan (HSE 計畫的制定)

Original Text

The HSE plan addresses health, safety, and environmental concerns throughout the SUS project. It should be prepared at an early stage and incorporated into the user requirements. Published examples of an HSE plan (although not related to SU technology) can be found in the literature. The HSE plan lists stakeholders and those responsible for performing specific HSE activities. These activities may range from mapping and analyzing the impact of HSE to developing and implementing process improvements. A workflow for developing an HSE plan may consist of the following steps:

  • Screen — Quick clarification of any HSE aspects related to the project
  • Define — Overall evaluation of significant HSE concerns during the project lifecycle
  • Plan — Final HSE plan with stakeholders, activities, responsibilities, and deadlines

The screening and defining activities involve the complete evaluation of the project from an HSE point of view in order to determine HSE concerns that require immediate action. Some of the HSE concerns for a typical SUS project are presented here.

Health Safety Environment
  • Ergonomics
  • Manual operations
  • Flammables
  • Equipment malfunction
  • Improper operation of equipment
  • Emissions
  • Waste
  • Energy
  • Water
  • Chemicals
  • Fossil fuels and raw materials
  • Consumption of raw materials
  • Wrappings and other support materials
  • Transport

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

HSE 三步驟工作流程：

  • Screen (篩選)：快速盤點專案中與 HSE 相關的面向
  • Define (定義)：全面評估專案生命週期中的重大 HSE 關注事項
  • Plan (計畫)：制定最終 HSE 計畫，明確列出利害關係人、活動、責任與時程

比喻說明 Analogy

HSE 計畫就像醫院的感染管控計畫 (Infection Control Plan)——不是出了問題才寫，而是在專案早期就納入使用者需求規格中。三步驟流程就像醫院的「風險篩檢→詳細評估→制定方案」，從宏觀到微觀逐步聚焦。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 專案的環境面向特別值得關注：一次性使用意味著大量的塑膠廢棄物、包裝材料和運輸碳足跡。這與傳統 MUS（使用 CIP/SIP 但產生較少固體廢棄物）形成鮮明對比。企業的永續製造政策必須納入 SUS 的 HSE 評估中。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. SUS 與 MUS 在環境影響面向上有哪些根本性差異？
  2. 為什麼 HSE 計畫應該在專案早期就制定，而不是等到安裝階段？

7.6.9 Health and Safety Issues Related to SUS (SUS 相關 HSE 議題)

Original Text

SUSs often consist of plastic components that have low resistance to physical stress, pressure, and temperature extremes. A typical setup includes a range of support equipment (e.g., pumps, agitators, scales) that requires manual transportation, installation, and dismantling. This generates a unique set of HSE concerns, as presented in the following lists.

Safety

  • Tubing ruptures at eye level
  • Bag ruptures at eye level
  • Spills and slippage
  • Emergency stops for moving parts
  • Automatic restarts after power cuts
  • Tubing on floor that may result in tripping
  • Loose parts (e.g., media containers, peristaltic pumps) that can fall
  • Mobile containers over feet or hands, mobile containers squeezed in doorways
  • Mobile containers' finish, corners, and handles
  • Connections failing for compressed air and other gases (e.g., CO2 and nitrogen)
  • Retention of infectious material
  • Failure in connecting to CIP/SIP equipment
  • Position of emergency stop during filling operations may be out of sight from dispensing vessel

Health

  • Ergonomics for installation and removal of SUS components (e.g., installing bags, filters)
  • Ergonomics for handling bags that contain liquid
  • Stress of communicating during filling operations that may be out of sight from dispensing vessel
  • Lifting heavy or cumbersome objects
  • Insufficient work space and surfaces

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SUS 的安全風險與 MUS 截然不同。MUS 是固定的不鏽鋼設備，一旦安裝就很少移動；SUS 則由塑膠組件構成，耐壓性和耐溫性較低，且需要頻繁的手動搬運、安裝與拆卸。這產生了一組獨特的安全隱患。

重點提示 Key Notes

特別需要注意的高風險情境：

  • 眼部高度的管路/袋體破裂：如果處理的是生物製劑或有害物質，後果可能非常嚴重
  • 停電後自動重啟：未受控的設備重啟可能導致嚴重的安全事故
  • 地面管路絆倒風險：SUS 的臨時管路布線經常造成地面障礙
  • 緊急停機按鈕位置：充填操作時，緊急停機按鈕可能不在操作人員視線範圍內

比喻說明 Analogy

想像一下廚房的安全差異：一間是配備固定式不鏽鋼爐灶的專業廚房（MUS），另一間是使用臨時瓦斯管線和移動式設備的流動廚房（SUS）。後者的安全風險更為複雜——管線可能絆倒人、設備可能滑動、連接處可能鬆脫。需要完全不同的安全思維。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 針對「管路在眼部高度破裂」的風險，你會制定哪些預防措施？
  2. SUS 操作中，人因工程 (Ergonomics) 問題為什麼比 MUS 更加嚴重？請舉例說明。

7.7 Implementation S7: Launch (啟動上線)

Original Text

The PEP leads to an initial procurement of equipment for the SUS project in addition to setting out a secure supply chain for continuous operation of the SUS. Initial supplier evaluations are part of the PEP preparation in S4 (Section 7.4.10). In the following paragraphs, these first steps are consolidated with a detailed evaluation of the appropriate tools for the routine management of suppliers.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Implementation S7 - Launch (啟動上線)：S7 標誌著 SUS 從「專案模式」轉入「營運模式」的關鍵時刻。PEP 不僅引導初始設備採購，更要建立一條安全可靠的供應鏈，以支持 SUS 的持續運作。此階段的核心任務是將 S4 階段的初步供應商評估，深化為常規化的供應商管理體系。

比喻說明 Analogy

S7 就像餐廳從「試營運」轉為「正式營業」——試營運時可以用少量食材測試，但正式營業後必須建立穩定的食材供應鏈：固定的供應商、品質協議、備用供應商、庫存管理策略等。沒有穩定的供應鏈，再好的廚藝也無法持續出餐。

7.7.1 Management of Materials (物料管理)

Original Text

Since continuous sourcing of supplies is critical to keeping the SUS in a productive state, it is important to maintain an efficient routine supplier management (e.g., technical diligence, quality audits, quality and supply agreements, and purchasing, logistical, and waste-handling strategies) to create a robust support for SUS manufacturing operations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Routine Supplier Management (常規供應商管理)：涵蓋技術盡職調查、品質稽核、品質與供應協議、採購策略、物流策略和廢棄物處理策略等多個面向。SUS 與 MUS 的根本差異在於：SUS 是「消耗品模式」，持續供應的中斷直接等於生產停擺。

重點提示 Key Notes

對於 CDMO 而言，物料管理的重要性不言而喻。由於 SUS 組件無法重複使用，任何供應中斷都會直接影響客戶的產品交付時程。建立「穩健的供應商管理體系」是 SUS 營運成功的基石。

7.7.2 Routine or Operational Procurement (常規採購)

Original Text

Routine procurement for SUS (e.g., single-use bioreactors or chromatography systems) requires a supplier qualification program for each of the SUS suppliers included in the PEP. Whenever the risk and complexity of the component in question is considered significant, the qualification program should be implemented using a risk-management approach. Some of the factors to consider are as follows:

  • The end user may have to adopt a different approach to the procurement of integrated SUS equipment versus routine SUS components (Sections 5.2, 5.4, 5.5, 6.12.1, 6.14, 7.5.7, and 7.6.2).
  • A backup policy of sourcing the same component from at least two different vendors should be adopted, and the suitability for the backup to be interchangeable with the original must be defined.
  • The end user must evaluate and audit the supplier's manufacturing capabilities and supply chain to determine the supplier's ability to increase output on demand.
  • The relationship between the end user and the supplier should be as transparent as possible in order to enhance the unimpeded operation of the SUS.
  • The quality systems of the supplier should be examined as part of a quality audit process, and quality and supply agreements should be implemented (Section 7.7.4).
  • The supplier should be provided with a detailed description of the manufacturing process of the SUS, film quality, biocompatibility, and testing (e.g., bioburden monitoring of the SUS), particulates, extractables and leachables, and testing of leakages.
  • A contract (supply or manufacturing agreement) describing the commercial conditions that relate to the supply chain, guarantee of delivery, and transport quality should be implemented.
  • Both the supplier and the end user must institute robust change-control processes in order to prevent ad hoc modifications to the SUS.
  • Time lines from the design to arrival of both MUS and SUS parts should be monitored.
  • Evaluation models (preferably at the end user's site) that use mock-ups of preliminary SUS designs (available for training and simulations) should be tested. Testing is an important risk-mitigating procedure. This process may have been started as part of the SUS strategy (Section 7.2.3).
  • The end user should adhere to green and sustainable manufacturing policies throughout the entire supply chain and evaluate waste disposal for carbon footprint reduction.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Supplier Qualification Program (供應商確認計畫)：針對 PEP 中的每個 SUS 供應商實施的系統性評估計畫。當組件的風險和複雜度較高時，應採用風險管理方法來實施。

Dual Sourcing (雙重供應策略)：同一組件至少從兩家不同供應商採購的備份策略，並須定義備用供應商的產品是否可與原廠互換。

Change Control (變更管控)：供應商和最終使用者雙方都必須建立嚴格的變更管控流程，以防止對 SUS 的臨時性修改。

重點提示 Key Notes

常規採購的十一項考量因素中，最關鍵的三點：

  • 雙重供應商策略：避免單一供應商風險，但「互換性」的定義和驗證是巨大的技術挑戰
  • 雙向變更管控：不僅使用者不能隨意更改，供應商的任何製程變更也必須通知使用者並經過評估
  • 永續製造：SUS 的環境影響（大量塑膠廢棄物）正受到越來越多的監管關注

實務應用 Practical Application

作為 CDMO，你的客戶可能指定使用特定供應商的 SUS 組件。但如果該供應商發生產能不足或品質問題怎麼辦？建議在客戶的技術轉移過程中，就主動協商備用供應商方案，並在品質協議中明確「供應商變更」的程序和責任歸屬。模型評估（使用 mock-up 進行模擬測試）是降低風險的有效手段。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 SUS 的供應商管理比 MUS 更加複雜？請從「消耗品」的本質來分析。
  2. 如果供應商單方面變更了薄膜配方，可能對你的製程產生哪些影響？你會如何通過變更管控來防範？
  3. 「綠色永續製造」在 SUS 供應鏈中面臨哪些特殊挑戰？

7.7.3 Technical Diligence (技術盡職調查)

Original Text

A QbD approach is the best way to qualify suppliers for SUSs. It is based on ICH principles (ICH Q8) and it embraces the complementary concepts of quality-risk management and pharmaceutical quality-system management (as detailed in ICH Q9 and Q10), process validation and verification, and stakeholder management (Sections 7.2.1, 7.2.2 and 7.2.3). These approaches lay the foundation for quality-driven processes built on a science- and risk-based approach and understanding. This is the case not just for the process for which the SUS will be used but also for the SU technology that will be deployed, thus supporting patient safety and product availability. The QbD approach allows for the identification and management of critical sources of variability in which control strategies can be used to maintain a state of control and facilitate the application of continuous improvement throughout the SUS product lifecycle.

Technical diligence can be started at S4 (Section 7.4). Based on established principles, it involves a carefully documented visit to the supplier's site. The outcome should be an appropriate and measured understanding of all the technical issues pertaining to the SUS manufacturing process, readiness for installation, and operation at the end user's facility. Technical diligence should be considered an important step in the supplier qualification process and a complement to the quality audit process. The principal differences between technical diligence and a quality audit are summarized in Table 7.7.3-1.

Table 7.7.3-1: Principal Differences Between a Quality Audit and a Technical Diligence Assessment

Description Quality Audit Technical Diligence
Purpose Compliance, quality systems Extensive technical understanding of design, manufacture, fitness for purpose, and control strategy
Personnel involved Quality team(s) Scientists, engineers, SMEs, and the supplier's technical and manufacturing staff
Scope Focused, supplier's quality systems Open-ended scope will vary depending on project, supply-chain transparency, subsuppliers back to source

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Technical Diligence (技術盡職調查)：不同於品質稽核只關注「合規性」，技術盡職調查的目的是深入理解供應商的設計、製造、適用性和控制策略。這是一種基於 QbD（Quality by Design，品質源於設計）原則的供應商評估方法。

QbD Approach (品質源於設計方法)：基於 ICH Q8/Q9/Q10 原則，通過科學和風險導向的方法來辨識和管理關鍵變異來源，建立控制策略以維持受控狀態。

比喻說明 Analogy

品質稽核就像檢查一間餐廳是否有營業執照、衛生許可和食安制度（合規性）；技術盡職調查則像是派一位主廚去實地考察食材供應商的農場——了解土壤品質、灌溉方式、施肥策略、收割流程，判斷食材是否真正適合自己的料理風格。兩者互補，缺一不可。

圖表解讀 Table Analysis

Table 7.7.3-1 清楚呈現了品質稽核與技術盡職調查的三大差異：

  • 目的不同：稽核聚焦「合規」；技術盡職調查聚焦「技術理解」
  • 參與人員不同：稽核由品質團隊主導；技術盡職調查需要科學家、工程師和 SME 的深度參與
  • 範疇不同：稽核範圍明確且聚焦；技術盡職調查是開放式的，可能需要追溯到次級供應商

Table 7.7.3-2: Some Pertinent Factors for a Technical Diligence Assessment Checklist

Supplier Information Supplier Technical Capability End-User Product Suitability and Compatibility
CDA implemented Design: engineering drawings and specifications Fit with the end user's process
Company and stakeholders Risk to the end user Fit with the end user's facility and warehousing
Level of supplier integration Resins, films, and other components Prototype testing procedure
Sourcing and supply chain Manufacturing process overview Qualification
Contingency planning Irradiation or other form of sterilization Deployment method
Plant tour SUS shelf life Training and HSE

Determine the supplier's degree of integration:

  • Vertical: The supplier manufactures practically everything on-site, from the film to the finished and packaged SUS
  • Horizontal: These activities are spread over more than one site
  • Mixed model: A combination of vertical and horizontal integration

The mixed model has become increasingly common. Resin is nearly always sourced as a bulk from larger industrial companies, and the SUS supplier company may be specialized in the production of SUS for pharmaceutical operations and have facilities on more than one continent. In some cases, it may require more than one technical diligence visit to the supplier's sites to address all the relevant technical concerns (e.g., the film's blow-extrusion may be performed at a different site than that used for SUS assembly and testing). The end user should pay careful attention to supply chain issues in this context. Depending on sourcing from another continent or from multiple continents could easily be disrupted by many factors beyond the end user's control and should be assessed from a risk-based approach.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Supplier Integration Models (供應商整合模式)：

  • Vertical (垂直整合)：從薄膜到成品全部在同一站點製造——供應鏈最簡單，但供應商選擇有限
  • Horizontal (水平整合)：活動分布在多個站點——需要多次技術盡職調查拜訪
  • Mixed (混合模式)：最常見的形態，樹脂通常從大型工業公司大量採購，SUS 組裝和測試可能在不同地點

重點提示 Key Notes

Table 7.7.3-2 提供了技術盡職調查的檢查清單框架，涵蓋三大面向：供應商資訊、技術能力、與最終使用者的適用性。特別注意：

  • CDA (保密協議)：技術盡職調查涉及深層技術資訊交換，保密協議是前提
  • 應急計畫 (Contingency Planning)：供應商是否有備援方案至關重要
  • 跨洲供應鏈風險：依賴不同大洲的供應可能因地緣政治、天災、物流中斷等因素而輕易斷裂

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你的 SUS 供應商採用混合整合模式，薄膜吹塑在歐洲、組裝在亞洲、測試在北美，你會如何規劃技術盡職調查的行程和重點？
  2. 為什麼 CDA 必須在技術盡職調查之前就簽署？不簽 CDA 會有什麼風險？

Table 7.7.3-3: An Interpretation of the SUS Implementation Process

Clinical Status of Product SUS Implementation Stage FDA PV Stage Supplier Qualification Activity Quality Agreement Risk & Complexity
Preclinical material Technical assessment (1), detailed investigation (2), and scoping (3) PV S1 Collect supplier and SUS product information Optional High
IMPs for toxicology and phase I Business case (4), development (5), and testing and validation (6) PV S1-2 Perform technical diligence Yes High
IMPs for phases II and III / PPQ conformance batches Launch (7) PV S2 Perform technical diligence and an audit Yes Moderate
Licensed product SUS exploitation stage PV S3 Continue supplier verification Yes Low

A quality audit may be executed either following or in parallel with the technical diligence process (e.g., an audit questionnaire can be part of the technical diligence process for phase I IMPs). A practical example of the technical diligence process can be found in Brown's presentation on Implementation and Technical Diligence.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

生命週期方法的實施對照表：Table 7.7.3-3 是本節最重要的表格之一，它將產品的臨床開發階段、SUS 實施階段、FDA 製程驗證 (PV) 階段、供應商確認活動和品質協議需求全部對齊。

圖表解讀 Table Analysis

這張表格揭示了一個重要的趨勢：

  • 風險隨時間降低：從臨床前的「高風險」逐步降至上市產品的「低風險」
  • 供應商管理深度遞增：從「蒐集資訊」→「技術盡職調查」→「技術盡職調查+稽核」→「持續驗證」
  • 品質協議從選配到必配：臨床前階段品質協議為選項，但進入臨床後就是必要的
  • Phase-appropriate approach（階段適切方法）：不同開發階段對供應商管理的要求不同，體現了 ICH 的階段適切原則

比喻說明 Analogy

這就像學生到職場的成長過程：實習期（臨床前）只需了解公司基本資訊；試用期（Phase I）需要展示實際能力；正式聘用（Phase II/III）要通過績效考核和背景調查；長期員工（上市產品）則進入持續監督與年度考評模式。每個階段的管理深度和正式程度逐漸提高。

7.7.4 Quality and Technical Agreements (品質與技術協議)

Original Text

Quality and technical agreements clarify the functional aspects of a business relationship by delineating the responsibilities of quality, regulatory, and production personnel within each company in order to enhance communication and prevent ambiguity as referred to in Section 6. A quality agreement should not be confused with a business, supply, or manufacturing agreement. Several templates for APIs are available for chemical and biological products, and the end user may adapt them to an SUS from the Bulk Pharmaceuticals Task Force (Society of Chemical Manufacturers and Affiliates or SOCMA) or the International Pharmaceutical Excipients Council (IPEC).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Quality Agreement (品質協議)：明確界定雙方品質、法規和生產人員責任的文件。注意：品質協議不等於商業協議或供應協議——它專注於品質相關的責任劃分。

SOCMA / IPEC 範本：現有的 API（原料藥）品質協議範本可以改編為 SUS 用途，但需要根據 SUS 的特殊性質（如 extractables/leachables、薄膜品質、生物相容性等）進行調整。

重點提示 Key Notes

品質協議的核心功能是「防止模糊性 (prevent ambiguity)」。在 SUS 供應鏈中，供應商和使用者之間的責任界線往往比 API 供應更加模糊——例如：薄膜的 extractables 測試是誰的責任？生物相容性數據由誰提供？變更通知的時限是多久？這些問題都必須在品質協議中明確回答。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼品質協議不應與商業/供應協議混為一談？兩者的核心目的有何不同？
  2. 將 API 品質協議範本改編為 SUS 品質協議時，你認為需要增加哪些特定條款？

7.7.5 Logistics and Storage (物流與倉儲)

Original Text

The storage and warehouse facilities required for the efficient operation of the SUS should be defined in the PEP. In general, the amount of pallet space required may be calculated as a function of consumption and the dimensions of the shipping container. A risk-based approach may be used to allocate storage space for critical consumables with limited or no alternative suppliers, while standard consumables can be sourced as and when they are needed. Value-stream mapping (a lean manufacturing technique used to analyze the flow of materials and information required to bring a product or service to the user) can be used to identify improvements in lead time or to identify inefficient operations. For example, a value-stream map can show where excess materials are accumulating. Some of the factors to consider are:

  • High-risk consumables
  • Standard consumables
  • Storage policy
  • Pallet space
  • Frequency of delivery to consumers
  • Environmental storage conditions monitoring and control (a GMP requirement)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Value-Stream Mapping (價值流圖，VSM)：精實製造的核心工具之一，用於分析從原材料到最終使用者的物料和資訊流動。在 SUS 倉儲管理中，VSM 可以幫助辨識前置時間的改善空間和效率低落的環節。

Risk-Based Storage (風險導向倉儲)：關鍵消耗品（特別是沒有替代供應商的）應配置較多的安全庫存空間；一般性消耗品則可以按需採購。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 的倉儲策略就像超市的庫存管理：暢銷且獨家代理的商品（高風險消耗品）需要較大的儲架空間和安全庫存；而容易從多家供應商取得的日用品（標準消耗品）則採用即時補貨模式。價值流圖就是超市的「動線分析」，找出哪裡在排隊（瓶頸）、哪裡在囤積（浪費）。

公式與計算 Formula

棧板空間需求 = f (消耗速率, 貨櫃尺寸)

安全庫存策略：
  高風險消耗品 → 較高安全庫存 (2-4 週)
  標準消耗品   → 按需採購 (JIT)

GMP 要求：
  環境儲存條件 → 必須監控與管控
  (溫度、濕度等)

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 相比 MUS 在倉儲上有一個獨特的挑戰：SUS 是消耗品，每批生產都需要全新的組件，因此所需的倉儲空間遠大於 MUS。環境儲存條件的監控與管控是 GMP 的強制要求——某些 SUS 組件（如薄膜袋）對溫度和濕度敏感，不當儲存可能導致保質期縮短或材料劣化。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你的 SUS 使用量突然因為新客戶訂單而增加 50%，你的倉儲策略需要做哪些調整？
  2. 價值流圖如何幫助你發現 SUS 供應鏈中的「隱藏浪費」？請舉一個具體例子。
  3. 為什麼 SUS 的倉儲管理比 MUS 更加複雜且佔用更多空間？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • S6 測試與驗證階段涵蓋交付、安裝、確效、訓練和安全五大領域。每個環節都需要在 PEP 中詳細規劃，並明確供應商與最終使用者的責任劃分。
  • SUS 確效必須包含生命週期測試（Lifecycle Testing），模擬滅菌、運輸、凍融等最具衝擊性的步驟，確保在預期工作空間內的功能表現。
  • 訓練是 GMP 的硬性要求。SUS 操作人員需要接受專屬訓練，因為 SUS 的操作原理與 MUS 有根本性差異。袋體處理意識訓練是減少洩漏的最有效手段。
  • HSE 計畫應在專案早期制定。SUS 因大量手動操作而產生獨特的安全風險（眼部高度破裂、地面管路絆倒、人因工程挑戰等），同時其一次性使用的特性帶來顯著的環境影響。
  • S7 啟動上線的核心是建立從專案採購轉向常規營運採購的供應商管理體系，包括雙重供應策略、變更管控和品質協議。
  • 技術盡職調查與品質稽核互補：前者聚焦技術理解（由科學家和工程師主導），後者聚焦合規性（由品質團隊主導）。供應商的整合模式（垂直/水平/混合）決定了調查的複雜度。
  • 品質協議是防止責任模糊的關鍵文件，必須與商業協議分開管理。SOCMA 和 IPEC 提供了可改編的範本。
  • 倉儲策略應採用風險導向方法：高風險消耗品配置安全庫存，標準品按需採購。價值流圖 (VSM) 是優化物流效率的精實工具。環境監控是 GMP 的強制要求。

PDA Technical Report No. 66 (2014): Single-Use Systems

Section 5c: Implementation Framework S6-S7 (Sections 7.6-7.7, p100-p107)

Educational Material for CDMO Professionals

A1

Section A1: Appendix: URS Example

附錄：URS範例 | p108-p120

PDA Technical Report No. 66 (2014) Single-Use Systems | p108 - p120

本章學習目標

  • 理解 User Requirement Specification (URS) 文件在 SUS 設施專案中的角色與結構
  • 掌握 URS 範例中涵蓋的主要領域：設施描述、製程、物料流、人員流、法規、公用設施、潔淨室、控制系統
  • 學習如何為基因治療病毒載體的 SUS 生產設施撰寫使用者需求
  • 認識 BSL2 生物安全要求如何影響設施設計與 HVAC 系統規劃
  • 了解 URS 如何為後續設計確認 (DQ) 及驗證活動奠定基礎

8.0 / 8.1 Description of Document

Original Text

8.0 Appendix I: Overall User Requirement Specification Example

8.1 Description of Document

This appendix contains an example of user requirements (UR) written for an SUS facility. This material is referenced in Section 7.5.1, User Requirements, and should be used as an example for how this type of document is structured. The complexity and size of the document will change according to the type of SUS and complexity of the project. These types of documents should be considered as living (i.e., they can be updated as appropriate should the project or UR change). The document can be prepared by the end user or a sponsor of the end user such as an engineering company or supplier.

This document describes the UR concerning the new production suite, GMP, SUS (shown in figure below). This is an overall UR specification and detailed UR will be written. The requirements stated in this document may not be qualified but will form the basis for design.

8.1.1 Abbreviations

AbbreviationFull Term
