Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

User Requirement Specification, URS (使用者需求規格書): URS 是製藥工程專案中最重要的基礎文件之一。它由使用者（製藥公司）撰寫，明確定義「我需要什麼」，而非「如何做到」。URS 是後續所有設計（概念設計、基本設計、細節設計）的起點，也是 Design Qualification (DQ) 的驗證依據。

Living Document (活文件): URS 不是一次定稿就永不更改的文件。隨著專案進展、法規變化或製程需求調整，URS 可以且應該被更新——但必須透過正式的變更管控 (Change Control) 程序。

比喻說明 Analogy

URS 就像蓋房子時的「需求清單」：你告訴建築師「我需要三間臥室、兩間浴室、一個開放式廚房」，但不會告訴他用什麼品牌的水泥或什麼尺寸的鋼筋。URS 描述的是「What」（需要什麼），而非「How」（如何實現）。建築師根據你的需求出設計圖，就像工程公司根據 URS 產出設計規格 (Design Specification)。

重點提示 Key Notes

本附錄提供的是一個整體性 (Overall) 的 URS 範例，實際專案中還需要針對個別系統（如 HVAC 系統、WFI 系統、自動化系統等）撰寫更詳細的 URS。整體 URS 定義大框架，細節 URS 則深入每個子系統。

注意：本 URS 範例中的需求「may not be qualified」——意思是這些需求不一定全部需要正式確認 (Qualification)，但它們構成設計的基礎。哪些需求需要確認，會在後續風險評估中決定。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 URS 被稱為「活文件」？在什麼情況下需要更新 URS？
  2. URS 可以由「end user 的 sponsor（如工程公司或供應商）」撰寫，這在 CDMO 情境中意味著什麼？
  3. 「Overall URS」與「Detailed URS」之間有何差異？請舉例說明。

8.2 Introduction

8.2.1 Description of Facility

Original Text

Company X needs to equip a new facility GMP, SUS for the manufacture of injectable products for viral particle gene therapy. This document outlines the user requirements of the facility. In this project and UR document, abbreviation T4 stands for the main building site and GMP, SUS for the cleanroom area. The new production suite should be designed for biosafety level 2 (BSL2) and comply with EU GMP and FDA cGMP.

The products of this facility shall be based on modified live viral particle technologies (gene therapy). The manufacturing process shall cover production of biological bulk and final filled products for sterile, as parenteral applications. The initial adenovirus production portfolio covers in the first instance two bulk and two final products, which are known as Product 1 and Product 2.

Product 1 is a novel gene-based product that is given as a suicide therapy for tumors. Product 2 is a novel product being developed to deliver a growth factor for use in surgery.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

BSL2 (生物安全等級 2): BSL2 適用於處理對人員有中等潛在危害的微生物。此案例使用活病毒載體（腺病毒），因此需要 BSL2 等級的生物安全防護。這直接影響設施的 HVAC 設計（需要負壓或定向氣流）、廢棄物處理（需要滅活）、及人員防護。

Gene Therapy (基因治療): 利用病毒載體將治療性基因送入患者細胞。此處使用腺病毒 (Adenovirus) 作為載體，是一種常見的基因治療技術平台。

雙重法規合規: 設施需同時符合 EU GMP 和 FDA cGMP，這表明產品將在歐盟和美國市場上市。雙重合規會增加設計複雜度，因為兩套法規在潔淨室分級、環境監控等方面有些許差異。

比喻說明 Analogy

BSL2 設施就像一個「有門禁的實驗室」——與一般辦公室相比，它有嚴格的出入管控、特殊的通風系統（確保空氣只往內流，不往外洩）、以及專用的廢棄物處理通道。想像一個處理感染性物質的醫院病房：空氣是負壓控制的，廢棄物要先滅菌才能丟棄，人員進出要換裝。SUS 設施在此基礎上，再加上 GMP 的潔淨度要求。

重點提示 Key Notes

這個 URS 範例特別有價值，因為它展示了 SUS 技術在基因治療這類先進治療藥品 (ATMP) 生產中的應用。由於基因治療產品批量通常較小、產品種類變化快，SUS 的靈活性和免清洗特性特別適合此類應用。

注意 URS 中使用的語言：「shall」表示強制性需求；「should」表示建議性需求。在 URS 撰寫中，用詞的選擇直接影響後續驗證的範圍。

8.2.2 Environment / 8.2.3 Capacity

Original Text

8.2.2 Environment

As a design basis for the HVAC in Company X, an upper limit of +30°C at 50% RH (63 kJ/kg) in summertime and lower limit of −37°C in wintertime for the outside climate will be used.

8.2.3 Capacity

The target capacities to fulfill the expected need of the market for the facility are summarized in the following list. Total number of vials will be about 130,000.

The process capabilities are limited by the drug substance manufacture. The drug substance manufacture will need 24-hour, 7-day-week control. However, the filling operation will be run on an 8-hour, 5-day-week basis.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

HVAC 設計基準 (Design Basis): HVAC 系統的設計需考慮當地最極端的氣候條件。此案例設定夏季最高 +30°C/50% RH、冬季最低 −37°C，暗示設施可能位於北歐（如芬蘭）。這些數據決定了 HVAC 系統的冷卻和加熱能力設計。

產能規劃: 年產約 130,000 瓶——在基因治療領域屬於中等規模。藥物原料 (Drug Substance) 製造需要 24/7 監控（因為細胞培養不能中斷），但充填 (Filling) 只需 8 小時/天、5 天/週，反映了兩個工段不同的運營節奏。

重點提示 Key Notes

在 URS 中明確定義環境設計基準至關重要——如果 HVAC 設計基準設定錯誤（例如低估了夏季最高溫度），可能導致潔淨室在極端天氣下無法維持所需的溫濕度條件，進而影響產品品質和 GMP 合規性。

8.2.4 Process

Original Text

8.2.4.1 Production Process

The planned process for large-scale manufacturing of Product 1 and Product 2 vectors for the commercial scale process is shown below.

Thawing and expansion of master cell banks (API clean process)

  • T-flask, roller bottles, and rocker bags

Infection of expanded cells with working virus seed stock (WVSS) (API clean process)

  • Infection of the cell suspension with WVSS
  • Full CPE monitored with analytical and process tools

Cell lysis and clarification of crude viral lysate (cCVL) (API clean process)

  • Benzonase® and surfactant treatments to lyse the cells
  • Depth filtration to remove cell debris

Buffer conditioning by crossflow ultrafiltration (API clean process)

  • Diafiltration to reduce the amount of host cell– and growth medium–originated impurities
  • Buffer conditioning suitable for chromatography

Chromatography (API clean process)

  • Capture and polishing of recombinant adenoviruses

Crossflow ultrafiltration (API clean process)

  • Concentration
  • Diafiltration to remove the chromatography elution components (salts)
  • Change to final formulation buffer standardization of concentration
  • Freezing and holding in −70°C

Fill and finish (aseptic process)

  • Thawing final sterilization filtration prior to filling
  • Washing and sterilization of vials
  • Filling, stoppering, and crimping

Inspection, packaging, and storage

  • Checking of container seals and visual inspection
  • Labeling of primary containers and packaging
  • Freezing and storage of the drug product

8.2.4.2 Assumptions for planning

  • Disposable equipment is used during processing of the product.
  • The production suite should be equipped with its own WFI facility and solution manufacture.
  • Glass vials for sterile filling are brought into the facility ready to be washed and depyrogenated. Stoppers and aluminum crimps for filling are bought from suppliers presterilized.

8.2.4.3 Storage in GMP, SUS

There shall be storage areas for incoming raw materials and packaging material within T4. The GMP, SUS area shall provide storage of a batch material between process steps in the production.

8.2.4.4 Inactivation

All floor and process drains, such as product-containing waste waters, elution buffers, and so on, from the manufacturing areas shall be led to the collection tanks in the inactivation system. The connection to the collection tank shall be a closed system. Inactivation shall be carried out chemically or thermally in the balance tanks. After inactivation and neutralization, the drain liquid is transferred to the common drainage for transportation to the municipal wastewater treatment plant.

Floor and process drains from other areas shall be led directly to the common drainage or, when appropriate, to existing T4 balancing tank.

8.2.4.5 Waste Handling

Used equipment from the aseptic area and reusable equipment from the API areas are placed and sealed into plastic bags and decontaminated in a decontamination area (BSL2). The risk assessment will show the need for decontamination in the autoclave.

8.2.4.6 CIP

No CIP station is necessary due to the use of disposables. Elution solutions are used in order to clean columns and filter systems. A washing machine is used for washing filling-machine parts and filter holders.

8.2.4.7 Washing and Sterilization

Sterilization of reusable equipment shall be performed in an autoclave. Stoppers and aluminum crimps are bought from suppliers presterilized. Vials are to be washed and depyrogenized locally on entering the filling area.

8.2.4.8 SIP

No sterilization-in-place (SIP) is necessary due to the use of disposables and the supply of media, buffer, and elution solutions.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

製程流程概觀: 這是一個典型的腺病毒載體生產製程，包含以下關鍵階段：

  • 上游 (Upstream): 細胞解凍 → 細胞擴增 → 病毒感染 → 細胞裂解
  • 下游 (Downstream): 深層過濾 → 超過濾/透析過濾 → 層析純化 → 濃縮/換液
  • 充填 (Fill & Finish): 無菌過濾 → 充填 → 加塞 → 壓蓋

注意所有上游和下游步驟都標註為「API clean process」（原料藥潔淨製程），而充填則標註為「aseptic process」（無菌製程），反映不同工段的無菌要求等級。

比喻說明 Analogy

SUS 在這個製程中的角色就像「免洗餐具」用於外燴活動——每次使用全新的拋棄式設備（搖擺袋、管路、過濾器、層析管柱等），用完即丟，不需要清洗和滅菌。這不僅省去了 CIP/SIP 系統的建置成本，更重要的是消除了交叉污染的風險——就像用免洗餐具永遠不會有前一位客人的殘留。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 對設施設計的簡化效果:

  • 無需 CIP 站 — 大幅減少公用設施需求和設備佔地面積
  • 無需 SIP 系統 — 不需要潔淨蒸氣系統的複雜管線配置
  • 但仍需高壓滅菌釜 (Autoclave) — 用於可重複使用設備的滅菌和 BSL2 廢棄物的滅活

這是 SUS 的核心價值主張：簡化設施、加速建設、降低資本支出，但不是完全消除所有傳統設備。

生物安全滅活要求 Biosafety Inactivation

由於使用活病毒載體 (BSL2)，所有接觸過製程物料的廢水和排放物必須經過化學或熱滅活才能排入公共下水道。這是生物安全法規的硬性要求，在 URS 中必須明確定義滅活系統的規格。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼即使採用全拋棄式設備，仍然需要高壓滅菌釜？
  2. 如果把此設施從 BSL2 降為 BSL1，URS 中哪些需求可以簡化或省略？
  3. 「API clean process」與「aseptic process」在潔淨室等級要求上有何差異？

8.2.5 Material Flows

Original Text

The risk of cross-contamination shall be minimized in the layout of the plant area and in the manufacturing areas. Special attention shall be put on straight flows so that possibility for mix-ups between products from different process phases or different products is minimized. Line clearance shall be performed between production runs of different products. The facility shall be designed for sequential batches of cells to be expanded in cell culture at the same time. Attention shall also be put on keeping the BSL2 requirements in the layout.

8.2.5.1 Traffic to and from T4

The incoming raw materials shall be transported to the goods-receiving area of T4. In the same way, the final products are removed for transportation from the same T4 building. Rejected material is transported to incineration.

The following shall be delivered to or brought out of T4:

Incoming:

  • Raw material for the process
  • Utensils, disposables, and components for production
  • Clothing for cleanrooms
  • Packaging materials
  • Material for cleaning of cleanrooms

Outgoing:

  • Final products in cardboard boxes
  • Clothing from cleanrooms
  • Production waste
  • Additional waste

Material flows for the production shall be separated from the other material flows.

8.2.5.2 Storage areas in GMP, SUS and T4

The main function of the storage areas in T4 is to receive and store the raw material needed in production and daily work and, when approved, to distribute it for use. Released final products shall be stored and dispatched to the customer in pallets or smaller packages. The storage areas also work as storage for hazardous and medical material and collection points for waste. The storage areas shall be designed for storage of at least two months' needs in production and consumption. The storage for finished products shall be dimensioned for six months' production.

There shall be storage areas for the following materials and products:

  • Incoming raw material, packaging material, and pallets (existing)
  • Raw material in cold storages (MCB in liquid nitrogen and MVSS in freezer)
  • Intermediates during process (cold storages)
  • Quarantined material and packaging material (existing)
  • Approved bulk material and packaging material (existing)
  • Rejected raw material and packaging material (existing)
  • Finished products (freezers)
  • Quarantined finished products (existing freezers)
  • Approved finished products (existing freezers)
  • Rejected finished products
  • Reference samples (existing)
  • Spare parts (existing)
  • Samples for stability studies (existing)
  • Lining materials and used boxes (existing)

8.2.5.3 Material Airlocks

Transport of material or products between unclassified and classified rooms and rooms with different classifications shall be done through extracted airlocks or pass-throughs. The airlocks shall be of the one-way type because personnel and the material flow shall be unidirectional. The material or product shall be unpacked and sprayed with ethanol inside the airlock when transporting to a room with class C classification. Filling components passed into the class B area shall be washed and depyrogenated, or packages of presterilized components shall be subject to a vaporized hydrogen peroxide (VHP) cycle.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Unidirectional Flow (單向流動): 物料和人員只能沿一個方向移動，避免乾淨物料與廢棄物料交叉。這是 GMP 設施設計的基本原則之一，也是防止交叉污染 (Cross-Contamination) 的關鍵。

Line Clearance (生產線清場): 在不同產品批次之間進行的清潔和檢查程序，確保上一批次的物料不會殘留在生產線上。在 SUS 設施中，由於使用拋棄式設備，line clearance 的範圍和複雜度會大幅降低。

Material Airlock (物料氣鎖): 連接不同潔淨等級區域的過渡空間，用於物料傳遞。氣鎖內維持壓差，防止低潔淨區的空氣進入高潔淨區。

比喻說明 Analogy

物料流管理就像機場的行李處理系統——出境行李和入境行李走不同的通道，不會交叉。「Airlock」就像機場的安檢區——所有進入管制區的物品必須經過檢查和處理（拆包、噴酒精消毒或 VHP 滅菌），才能進入更乾淨的區域。

重點提示 Key Notes

儲存需求設計: URS 要求原物料儲存量為至少兩個月的生產需求，成品儲存為六個月的產量。成品儲存需求較大，因為基因治療產品需要在 −70°C 冷凍儲存，且放行檢測需要較長時間。這些數字直接決定了冷凍櫃和液態氮儲存設施的規模。

SUS 對儲存的特殊影響: 使用拋棄式設備意味著需要大量儲存空間來存放一次性耗材（袋子、管路、過濾器等），這是傳統不鏽鋼設施不需要考慮的。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 URS 要求物料氣鎖必須是「one-way type」？如果允許雙向通行會有什麼風險？
  2. 進入 C 級區域的物料需要「噴灑酒精」，而進入 B 級區域的充填組件需要「清洗除熱源」或「VHP 循環」——為什麼要求不同？

8.2.6 Personnel Flows / 8.2.7 Training

Original Text

8.2.6 Personnel Flows

The risk of cross-contamination shall also be minimized in the personnel flows. The main office building area has existing entrance, lunchroom, offices, and other social rooms.

There shall be emergency exits from the T4 and GMP, SUS buildings. If possible, the use of emergency exits should not compromise contained operation.

Personnel lockers and changing rooms for factory suit shall also be situated in T4. There shall be authorization control at the entrance to the manufacturing area, allowing only authorized personnel to enter. The working areas should be visible by inspectors and QA personnel for observation of the activities.

8.2.6.1 Gowning

Personnel working in the production areas and in laboratories shall wear suitable protective clothes for classified rooms and working in a BSL2 containment area. Personnel working in office areas, such as the central facility control room, may wear common clothes.

8.2.6.2 Personnel Airlocks

The first main objective with airlocks is to maintain a positive pressure in the classified area and, by that, ensure a proper separation of the individual rooms or areas when only cleanliness grades are to be considered. The second main objective with airlocks is to prevent contaminants from BSL2 active rooms from spreading to nonactive cleaner areas. The personnel entering or leaving the cleanrooms shall go through airlocks where gowning is performed to suit the classified area gowns. The airlocks can be of the one-way type. There should be unidirectional personnel flow in the active areas.

8.2.6.3 Estimated Number of Personnel

About 8–11: cell culture rooms, 2–3 persons; downstream, 3–4 persons; filling, 3–4.

8.2.7 Training

In order to assure that the personnel have updated information of their working area, all personnel shall be trained in GMP procedures and in using SOPs and instructions concerning them.

Sufficient training for the personnel shall be provided by the supplier of every process equipment and utility and automation system. The education level shall be maintained with additional training during the whole lifecycle of the plant.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Personnel Airlock 的雙重目的:

  • GMP 目的: 維持潔淨區的正壓差，防止外界空氣中的微粒和微生物進入
  • BSL2 目的: 防止活性區 (Active Areas，即處理活病毒的區域) 的生物性污染物擴散到非活性區

這兩個目的有時會產生衝突——GMP 要求潔淨區正壓（空氣從乾淨區往髒區流），而 BSL2 要求活性區負壓（空氣從外往內流，防止生物危害物外洩）。設施設計必須巧妙平衡這兩個需求。

比喻說明 Analogy

人員氣鎖就像「太空站的氣密艙」——太空人從外太空（非管控區）進入太空站（潔淨區）前，必須在氣密艙中換裝、加壓。同樣，操作人員從辦公區進入潔淨室前，必須在更衣區逐層穿上無塵衣。差別在於，這裡還要考慮 BSL2 的反向需求——有些區域的空氣流向要「向內」而非「向外」。

重點提示 Key Notes

緊急出口與生物安全的平衡: URS 中特別提到「emergency exits should not compromise contained operation」——這意味著即使在緊急疏散時，也要盡可能維持生物安全的圍阻。這在實務設計中是一個挑戰，需要特殊的氣鎖設計或連鎖控制系統。

人力規劃: 僅需 8-11 人即可運行整個設施，反映了 SUS 設施的人力效率優勢——不需要大量人力進行設備清洗、組裝和滅菌驗證等工作。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. GMP 正壓需求和 BSL2 負壓需求如何在同一設施中共存？請思考可能的設計方案。
  2. 為什麼 URS 要求「工作區域應該讓檢查員和 QA 人員可以觀察」？這對設施設計有何影響？

8.3 Regulatory Requirements

Original Text

The production facilities shall be designed to meet applicable requirements in the US CFR, EU GMP, PIC/S, and applicable EU directives and Finnish legislation. All components and systems shall be designed and commissioned according to GEP, GAMP, and ASME standards and shall have a CE mark and a declaration of conformity.

The substances used and produced at the site shall meet the effective versions of monographs in the Ph. Eur., USP, or registered specifications. The compressed air and gases shall meet the demands in ISO 8573-1.

The cleanrooms shall be designed, constructed, and commissioned according to ISO 14644 and 14698, to meet cGMPs above.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

多重法規合規框架:

  • US CFR: 美國聯邦法規，特別是 21 CFR Part 211 (藥品 cGMP) 和 Part 600 (生物製品)
  • EU GMP: 歐盟 GMP 指南，包括 Annex 1 (無菌藥品製造)
  • PIC/S: 藥品稽查合作計畫，提供全球一致的 GMP 稽查標準
  • Finnish Legislation: 確認設施位於芬蘭，需遵守當地法規

關鍵標準:

  • ISO 14644: 潔淨室和相關控制環境的分級與測試標準
  • ISO 14698: 潔淨室的生物污染控制標準
  • ISO 8573-1: 壓縮空氣品質標準
  • GAMP: 良好自動化製造實務，用於電腦化系統驗證

重點提示 Key Notes

在 URS 中列出所有適用的法規和標準非常重要——這些構成了設計的法規邊界條件。如果遺漏了某個適用法規，可能導致設施建成後無法通過監管機構的查廠檢查 (Regulatory Inspection)。

CE 標誌 (CE Mark) 的要求確認設備須符合歐盟安全指令，是在歐盟境內使用設備的法律要求。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果此設施的產品也要銷往日本市場，URS 的法規需求章節需要增加哪些內容？
  2. ISO 14644 和 EU GMP 在潔淨室分級上有何差異？為什麼 URS 中要同時引用兩者？

8.4 User Requirements

8.4.1 Functional Area Requirements

Original Text

The following areas shall be available in the manufacturing suite:

  1. Material receipt and product dispatch
  2. Storage for incoming materials (room temp and cold)
  3. Quarantine area
  4. QC laboratory control area
  5. Released and rejected material storages
  6. Weighing room (optional)
  7. Master cell bank storage
  8. Master virus seed stock storage
  9. Airlocks for personnel and materials going between areas of different classification
  10. Personnel locker room/changing room
  11. Column packing room
  12. Cell culture room, clean
  13. Cell culture room, infected (upstream)/harvest
  14. Purification room (downstream)
  15. Filter integrity testing
  16. Filling
  17. Visual inspection, labeling, and packaging
  18. Washing area
  19. Decontamination
  20. Clean area
  21. Intermediate storage
  22. Media/buffer preparation area
  23. Storage for the final drug product (−70°C)
  24. Area for production utilities
  25. Area for waste inactivation
  26. Technical space for building HVAC and cleanroom HVAC
  27. Area for cleanroom clothes
  28. Area for maintenance equipment
  29. Storage for cleanroom cleaning equipment
  30. Control room/IT (CNC—external to change room routine)

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

功能區域清單 (Functional Area List): 這是 URS 的核心內容之一——列出設施中必須包含的所有功能區域。這份清單直接驅動設施的平面佈局 (Layout) 設計。

值得注意的幾個特殊區域：

  • #12 vs #13: 細胞培養分為「clean」和「infected」兩個房間——這是 BSL2 和病毒生產的特殊需求，感染前和感染後的操作必須在不同房間進行
  • #19 Decontamination: BSL2 設施必備，用於活病毒廢棄物的滅活處理
  • #25 Waste Inactivation: 與 #19 配合，處理液態生物性廢棄物
  • #30 Control Room (CNC): 控制室設在更衣流程之外，操作人員不需穿潔淨衣即可監控生產

重點提示 Key Notes

此清單共列出30 個功能區域，足見即使是採用 SUS 的設施，空間規劃仍然相當複雜。SUS 雖然省去了 CIP/SIP 設備房，但增加了拋棄式耗材的儲存空間和廢棄物處理區域。

注意 #6「Weighing room (optional)」——在 SUS 設施中，許多溶液由供應商預先配製好直接以袋裝供應，因此秤量室可能不是必需的。

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 情境中，如果要在同一設施中生產多個客戶的基因治療產品，功能區域清單需要額外考慮：專用 vs 共用區域的劃分、不同客戶產品的儲存隔離、以及更靈活的 changeover 策略。SUS 的優勢在此更加明顯——換產品時只需更換一次性耗材，而非清洗整套不鏽鋼系統。

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

公用設施分類:

  • 製程氣體: CO2、O2、製程空氣——用於搖擺袋 (Rocker) 細胞培養系統
  • 水系統: WFI（注射用水）、純水 (PW)、自來水、冷凍水——各有不同用途和品質等級
  • 蒸氣: 工廠蒸氣（加熱用）和潔淨蒸氣（滅菌用）——SUS 設施仍需潔淨蒸氣用於高壓滅菌釜
  • 廢水: 分為「活性廢水」(Waste active) 和「非活性廢水」(Waste inactive)——BSL2 設施的關鍵區分

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 並未完全消除公用設施需求: 從表中可以看到，雖然省去了 CIP 系統，但仍需要 WFI（清洗用）、潔淨蒸氣（高壓滅菌釜用）、液態氮（冷凍儲存用）等。這提醒我們：SUS 簡化了製程接觸面的清潔和滅菌，但設施的基礎公用設施仍然是必需的。

VHP「Has to be considered」: 氣化過氧化氫 (VHP) 用於表面除污和氣鎖消毒，此處標註為「需考慮」而非確定需要，表示在後續詳細設計階段才會決定是否採用。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 SUS 設施仍需要潔淨蒸氣 (Clean Steam)？它用在哪些地方？
  2. 「Waste active」和「Waste inactive」的分流管理為什麼重要？如果混合處理會有什麼後果？

8.4.3 Cleanroom and HVAC

Original Text

8.4.3.1 Room Classification

The rooms are classified according to the needs of the process and BSL2 containment requirements. The cleanrooms are designed according to ISO 14644-1 but validated, operated, and monitored according to EU GMP and PIC/S. The protection classes of electrical equipment in the cleanrooms shall be IP54 and in other areas according to room activity.

Table 8.4.3.1-1 Sample Room Classifications

ActivityClass (ISO 14644-1)Grade (EU GMP)
UDAF-hood and aseptic fillingCore area 5A
Aseptic filling room7B
Aseptic formulation rooms, chromatography and filter stations, cell growth, buffer preparation8C
Sampling and weighing of raw material, clean corridors, and washing rooms8 (at rest)D
Visitors corridors, clean utility production, utility production, packaging hall, and all other controlled production areasUnclassifiedUnclassified
HVAC, utility production, social areasUnclassifiedUnclassified

ISO classes are, unless separately mentioned, defined as during operation.

Airlocks shall be clean-room classified according to cleaner classification when at rest.

8.4.3.2 Ventilation Equipment

The ventilation system is divided into separate systems, according to use (one for cleanrooms and one for technical basement). Space will be reserved for future expansion of ventilation systems, which will serve cleanrooms on the first floor.

The cleanroom ventilation systems consist of fresh-air-handling units to obtain the air changes specified for each room or classified area. The ventilation system shall be designed as a "full fresh air" system in order to ensure the BSL2 and prevent cross-contamination in the production suite. The cleanrooms and technical spaces with high heat generation shall be equipped with separate circulation air-handling units to maintain room temperature within acceptable limits. Fan filter units shall be used in nonactive (BSL2) cleanrooms. There shall be a redundancy in the HVAC for the primary fan motors at a minimum. Due to the fact that operators will be in the cleanroom only eight hours a day, there shall be a possibility to have a lower airflow at night.

8.4.3.3 Air Filtration

The air for basement ventilation is filtered in three steps: G4, F7, and F9 filter, according to EN 779, within the air-handling unit.

Cleanroom air is prefiltered in four steps: G4, F7, F9, and H12, according to EN 779 and EN 1822, within the air-handling units. The terminal filter is minimum H13.

Exhaust air from the area where live virus is processed is filtered in two steps: F7 and H14 filter. Exhaust air from the basement is F7 filtered.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

ISO vs EU GMP 潔淨室分級對照:

  • ISO 5 / Grade A: 無菌操作核心區（UDAF 層流罩下），微粒數最嚴格
  • ISO 7 / Grade B: 無菌操作背景環境
  • ISO 8 / Grade C: 無菌製造的一般操作區
  • ISO 8 at rest / Grade D: 較低風險操作區（靜態時達到 ISO 8）

Full Fresh Air System (全新風系統): 所有送入潔淨室的空氣都是經過過濾的新鮮空氣，不回收再利用。這是 BSL2 設施的要求——如果回收空氣，可能將活病毒從一個房間帶到另一個房間，造成交叉污染。

H14 排氣過濾: 處理活病毒區域的排氣必須經過 HEPA H14 過濾（效率 ≥ 99.995%），防止活病毒顆粒排入大氣。

比喻說明 Analogy

HVAC 的「全新風系統」就像醫院負壓隔離病房的通風——每一口送進去的空氣都是新鮮的，每一口排出來的空氣都經過 HEPA 過濾。不像一般辦公室的空調會回收室內空氣。這確保了「進去的空氣是乾淨的，出來的空氣也是安全的」。

重點提示 Key Notes

夜間降低風量: URS 允許在非操作時段降低送風量——這是一個重要的節能設計考量。全新風系統的能耗極高（因為所有空氣都需要加熱/冷卻和過濾），夜間降低風量可以顯著降低運營成本。但必須確保降低風量後仍能維持必要的壓差和潔淨度（at rest 狀態）。

風機冗餘 (Redundancy): 主風機必須有備用——如果潔淨室 HVAC 風機故障，將導致壓差喪失，可能危及產品品質和 BSL2 安全性。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼活病毒處理區的排氣需要 H14 (99.995%) 而非 H13 (99.95%)？效率差異 0.045% 在實際意義上代表什麼？
  2. 「Full fresh air system」相比「回風系統」的主要缺點是什麼？在哪些情況下可以考慮部分回風？

8.4.4 Control and Automation System

Original Text

8.4.4.1 Process Control System

The process equipment is of the stand-alone type, which means that every unit has its own control system. The system shall consist of a local PLC/PC and an HMI and it shall be possible to handle at least three user levels. Every user shall have an individualized user name and password to restrict the access and maintain the audit trail. The ability of a control system to communicate with a SCADA system shall be stated in the UR. There shall be electronic records from the process but no electronic batch records.

All utility systems and appropriate equipment shall have separate control systems, which control production, distribution, and quality of the utility. It shall be possible to connect critical parameters to a SCADA system.

There should be an overall data collection and viewing system for the entire production plant.

8.4.4.2 Facility Monitoring System

The cleanrooms shall have a facility monitoring system (FMS) consisting of a PLC and an HMI. The FMS shall monitor the critical parameters for room conditions [e.g. temperature, pressure, viable and nonviable particles, microbial presence, and moisture (some areas)] in every classified room. The critical refrigeration devices also have to be connected to the FMS. The whole GMP, SUS suite is controlled by the building monitoring system (BMS). Cleanrooms in grades A and B will be equipped with a continuous online particle monitoring system. The operational C grade areas are also equipped with online particle monitoring (e.g., manifold system).

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Stand-alone Control (獨立控制): 每台設備有自己的 PLC/PC 和 HMI，而非由中央系統統一控制。這在 SUS 設施中很常見，因為拋棄式設備供應商通常提供整合好的設備控制系統。

三級使用者權限: 通常為 Operator（操作員）、Supervisor（主管）、Administrator（管理員），每級有不同的操作權限。這是 21 CFR Part 11 / EU GMP Annex 11 對電子記錄的基本要求。

Audit Trail (稽核追蹤): 系統必須記錄所有操作、修改、和數據存取的時間戳和操作者身份。這是數據完整性 (Data Integrity) 的核心要素。

FMS vs BMS: FMS 專注於 GMP 關鍵參數（潔淨室壓差、微粒、溫度等），BMS 負責整體建築的設施控制（照明、電力、一般 HVAC 等）。兩者通常是獨立系統，但可以交換數據。

重點提示 Key Notes

連續線上粒子監控: A 級和 B 級區域必須配備連續線上粒子監控——這是 EU GMP Annex 1 的要求。C 級區域使用多歧管系統 (Manifold System)，由一台粒子計數器輪流採樣多個採樣點，是一種成本效益較高的方案。

URS 中指出「electronic records but no electronic batch records」——表示雖然有電子數據記錄，但批次記錄仍以紙本為主。這在 2014 年是常見做法，但現今趨勢已朝向電子批次記錄 (EBR) 發展。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 URS 要求設備控制系統具備與 SCADA 通訊的能力，即使目前不使用 SCADA？
  2. 「Stand-alone」設備控制與「集中式」控制各有何優缺點？在 SUS 設施中為何偏好前者？

8.4.5 Health, Safety, and Environmental Requirements

Original Text

8.4.5.1 General

An HSE risk analysis shall be performed for the plant. Special attention shall be put on taking care of the environment. Contribution to the sustainable development shall be made by using natural resources rationally and by preventing health and environmental damage caused by waste. The generated waste shall primarily be reused, secondarily used as energy, and only as a final solution be transported to the dump. Special attention shall also be put on biosafety containment.

8.4.5.2 Air

Air from the production areas shall be filtered before leaving the building.

8.4.5.3 Drain

After inactivation, the drain liquid is processed further and neutralized in the municipal effluent plant together with all other drain systems.

8.4.5.4 Material

Waste material (e.g., biowaste, cardboard, plastics, paper, glass, and other waste) shall be sorted and reused if possible. If not, the material shall be transported to a dump or burned.

Hazardous and dangerous waste shall be gathered separately and moved to a storage area for hazardous waste. The waste shall be transported to incineration. Hazardous waste can be, for example, medical waste from production and equipment or returned medicines.

8.4.5.5 Emergency Systems

TypePurposeAreaRequired
Fire alarmPersonnel safetyAllYes
Intruder alarm systemSecurity / BiosecurityOuter wallsYes
SprinklerFire control—No
Cell phonesPersonnel safetyAllYes
Oxygen sensorsPersonnel safetyIn liquid N2, CO2 presence, excess O2Yes
UPS (uninterrupted power supply)Business contingency, Maintenance of bio-containment, Personnel safetyUDAF-hood, HVAC FMS including PMS, control systemsYes
Diesel generatorBusiness contingency, Maintenance of bio-containment, Personnel safetyUDAF-hood, HVAC FMS including PMS, refrigerators, and freezersYes
Waste active failure alarmBusiness contingency, Maintenance of bio-containment, Personnel safety, Pollution controlBasementYes
Leak and other appropriate detectorsTo avoid damage to equipment, HSE issuesBasementYes

8.4.5.6 Noise

A risk assessment regarding noise levels shall be performed. Both internal and external noise shall be analyzed.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

HSE (健康、安全、環境) 風險分析: 這是設施設計中與 GMP 同等重要但常被忽視的面向。URS 要求進行系統性的 HSE 風險評估，涵蓋：

  • 健康 (Health): 人員暴露於生物危害物質的風險
  • 安全 (Safety): 液態氮窒息風險、高壓蒸氣燙傷風險等
  • 環境 (Environment): 排氣過濾、廢水滅活、廢棄物分類處理

廢棄物處理優先順序: 再利用 → 能源回收 → 最後才是掩埋。這反映了歐盟的永續發展法規要求，對 SUS 設施尤為重要，因為拋棄式設備會產生大量塑膠廢棄物。

重點提示 Key Notes

緊急系統的層次化設計:

  • UPS (不斷電系統): 提供短時間（通常 15-30 分鐘）的備用電力，讓關鍵設備（UDAF 罩、HVAC、監控系統）有序關機或切換到柴油發電機
  • 柴油發電機: 提供長時間備用電力，覆蓋範圍更廣（包括冷凍櫃和冷藏庫）
  • 兩者配合形成「無縫供電」：UPS 負責瞬間切換，柴油發電機負責長期供電

注意：不需要灑水系統 (Sprinkler = No)——這可能是因為潔淨室中灑水會造成嚴重的微粒和微生物污染，以及 BSL2 區域的水可能被生物污染。替代方案可能是惰性氣體滅火系統。

比喻說明 Analogy

緊急供電系統就像醫院的電力備援——手術室的電力不能中斷，即使外面停電了，UPS 立刻接手供電，同時柴油發電機在幾十秒內啟動提供長期電力。SUS 設施的 UDAF 罩和 HVAC 就像手術室的無影燈和層流系統——一旦斷電，無菌環境就會被破壞。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. SUS 設施產生的大量塑膠廢棄物如何與「永續發展」目標平衡？有哪些可行的解決方案？
  2. 為什麼需要「氧氣感測器」？液態氮在什麼情況下會對人員造成危險？
  3. 如果潔淨室不使用灑水系統，應該採用什麼替代消防方案？

8.4.6 Maintenance and Service

Original Text

A maintenance program for the whole suite shall be developed before start of production. The program shall include the facility and technical equipment within, the ventilation system and equipment, the production equipment, and all laboratory equipment. The maintenance system shall produce, in advance, weekly reports of equipment that needs service.

All equipment in the area shall be assigned an item number, which shall be fed to the maintenance system. The maintenance personnel are responsible for service of all equipment. Two times a year (summer and winter) there shall be production stops for maintenance of the production equipment.

Spare parts for process equipment for two years of continuous production shall be stored.

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

預防性維護 (Preventive Maintenance): URS 要求在生產開始前就建立完整的維護計畫。每件設備都有唯一的項目編號 (Item Number)，確保可追溯性。系統能自動產生週報，提前通知需要維護的設備。

計畫性停機 (Planned Shutdown): 每年夏季和冬季各一次停機維護——選擇夏季和冬季可能是考慮到可以同時進行 HVAC 系統的季節性維護。

重點提示 Key Notes

備品策略: 儲存兩年份的備品——這對 SUS 設施尤其重要，因為一次性耗材的供應鏈中斷會直接影響生產。備品計畫必須涵蓋不僅是設備零件，還有拋棄式組件的安全庫存。

在 SUS 設施中，維護需求與傳統不鏽鋼設施有很大不同：不需要管路和容器的定期重新鈍化 (Re-passivation)、不需要墊片的定期更換、不需要焊接接頭的定期檢查——但需要確保搖擺裝置、蠕動泵驅動器等支撐設備的正常運作。

8.5 Documentation Requirements / 8.6 Validation and Testing

Original Text

8.5 Documentation Requirements

8.5.1 General

8.5.1.1 Version Handling

8.5.2 Risk Assessment

8.5.3 SOPs

8.6 Validation and Testing

(Note: Sections 8.5 and 8.6 are listed in the table of contents on p108 as part of the URS structure, with content on p120. These sections serve as placeholders indicating that the URS document must address documentation requirements, version control, risk assessment, SOPs, and validation/testing plans.)

Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

文件需求 (Documentation Requirements): URS 的最後幾節提醒我們，設施專案不僅僅是硬體和設備——文件體系同樣是 URS 的一部分。URS 應定義：

  • 版本管理 (Version Handling): 所有文件的版本控制規則
  • 風險評估 (Risk Assessment): 要求在設計階段進行哪些風險評估
  • SOPs: 需要在生產前完成哪些標準作業程序
  • 驗證與測試 (Validation & Testing): IQ/OQ/PQ 的基本策略和範圍

重點提示 Key Notes

這些「佔位符」式的章節提醒 URS 撰寫者：即使在初始版本中無法完全定義所有細節，也要在 URS 的結構中為這些主題保留位置。隨著專案推進，這些章節會被逐步充實。這體現了 URS 作為「活文件」的特性。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼驗證策略需要在 URS 階段就開始規劃，而不是等到設備安裝完成後？
  2. URS 中的風險評估要求與後續的 FMEA 或 HACCP 分析有何關係？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • URS 的定位: User Requirement Specification 是 SUS 設施專案的基礎文件，定義「需要什麼」而非「如何做到」，是後續所有設計和驗證活動的起點
  • 範例場景: 本 URS 範例描述的是一個用於基因治療腺病毒載體生產的 BSL2 級 SUS 設施，需同時符合 EU GMP 和 FDA cGMP
  • SUS 對設施設計的影響: 免去 CIP/SIP 系統，但仍需高壓滅菌釜、WFI 系統、潔淨蒸氣等基礎公用設施；同時增加了拋棄式耗材的儲存需求
  • BSL2 的設計挑戰: 需要全新風 HVAC 系統、排氣 HEPA H14 過濾、廢水/廢棄物滅活系統、以及 GMP 正壓與 BSL2 負壓之間的壓差平衡
  • 潔淨室分級: 從 Grade A (ISO 5) 到 Unclassified，每個功能區域都需要明確定義其潔淨等級，且需同時參照 ISO 14644 和 EU GMP 標準
  • 控制與監控: 獨立設備控制 + SCADA 整合能力 + FMS/BMS 環境監控，構成完整的自動化架構
  • HSE 與緊急系統: UPS + 柴油發電機的分層供電保障、廢棄物分類與滅活處理、氧氣偵測器等安全措施是 BSL2 SUS 設施的必備要素
  • 活文件概念: URS 是隨專案演進持續更新的文件，初版可以有佔位符式的章節，後續逐步充實

PDA Technical Report No. 66 (2014) - Single-Use Systems

Section 8.0: Appendix I - Overall User Requirement Specification Example | p108-p120

Educational Material for CDMO Professionals

A2

Section A2: Appendix: PEP Example

附錄：PEP範例 | p121-p134

PDA Technical Report No. 66 (2014): Single-Use Systems | p121 – p134

本章學習目標

  • 理解 Project Execution Plan (PEP) 的目的、結構與在一次性使用系統 (SUS) 專案中的角色
  • 掌握 PEP 中專案範圍 (Scope)、執行策略 (Execution Approach) 與品質策略 (Quality Strategy) 的核心要素
  • 學習如何規劃 Commissioning and Qualification (C&Q) 流程，包含 FAT、SAT、IQ、OQ 的執行方式
  • 瞭解 Supervising Engineering Contractor (SEC) 與業主之間的角色分工與責任劃分
  • 認識變更管理 (Change Management)、風險管理 (Risk Management) 與文件管控 (Document Control) 在專案中的實務應用

本節目錄 Table of Contents

9.1 Introduction 9.2 Project Overview 9.3 Contract Documents 9.4 Scope 9.5 Execution Approach 9.6 Organization 9.7 Quality 9.8 Risk Management 9.9 HSE 9.10 C&Q 9.11 Handover 9.12 Abbreviations 9.13 References

9.1 Introduction

9.1.1 Purpose

This appendix contains an example project execution plan (PEP). This material is referenced in Section 7.4.1, Project Execution Plan, and should be used as an example for how this type of document is structured. The complexity and size of the document will change according to the type of SUS and complexity of the project. These types of documents should be considered as living (i.e., they can be updated as appropriate should the project change). The document can be prepared by the end user or by a sponsor of the end user such as an engineering company or supplier.

The purpose of this PEP is to define and describe the project execution strategy as well as how the project will be managed and how quality control is applied in order to ensure that the project meets its goals regarding cost, time, and quality.

9.1.2 Context of this Document

This document provides a road map for the work to be completed. The PEP is a "fit-for-purpose" and living document that defines the supervising engineering contractor's (SEC's) scope of services and responsibilities for the project.

This plan describes and defines the project scope, the execution strategy, quality control systems, and management plan.

9.1.3 Revision of the PEP

All information included in this PEP is current as of the latest issue date of each document referred to. If changes are made that significantly affect the execution strategy, project management, and/or quality control activities as defined herein, a revision shall be made with rationale for the change explained in the new revision. The approval of the new revisions follows the same procedure as the approval of the original PEP. If there is a change to an appendix or a referred document to this PEP, only the document will be revised.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Project Execution Plan / PEP (專案執行計畫)：PEP 是整個 SUS 建廠或改造專案的「作戰計畫書」，涵蓋範圍定義、執行策略、品質管控與時程管理。它不是一份寫了就束之高閣的文件，而是一份「活的文件 (Living Document)」，隨專案進展持續更新。

Supervising Engineering Contractor / SEC (監督工程承包商)：在大型製藥工程專案中，業主通常委託 SEC 來統籌設計、採購、施工與確效等工作。SEC 扮演專案管理的核心角色。

比喻說明 Analogy

PEP 就像蓋房子時的「施工藍圖+工程管理計畫」。想像你要裝修一間新餐廳：你需要一份文件說明「要做什麼（範圍）」、「怎麼做（策略）」、「誰負責什麼（組織）」、「品質怎麼控管」、「時程怎麼安排」。PEP 就是把這些全部整合在一份主文件中，讓所有利害關係人有共同的依據。

重點提示 Key Notes

PEP 的「活文件」特性非常重要。在 SUS 專案中，由於一次性技術的供應商生態系仍在快速演進，專案執行過程中經常需要調整設計或供應商選擇。PEP 必須有明確的版本管控 (Revision Control) 機制，確保每次變更都經過正式審核與批准。

請注意：PEP 可以由最終使用者 (End User) 或其委託的工程公司/供應商來撰寫，但無論誰撰寫，業主都必須審核並批准。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 PEP 被定義為「活文件」？在 SUS 專案中，哪些因素最可能觸發 PEP 的修訂？
  2. 如果 PEP 附錄中的一份參考文件被修訂了，PEP 主文件是否也需要修訂？為什麼？

9.2 Project Overview

9.2.1 General

Company X wishes to design and equip a new production suite, GMPX, for manufacture of injectable products for viral particle gene therapy.

The products manufactured in the new production suite shall be based on modified live viral particle technologies (gene therapies). The manufacturing process shall cover production of biological bulk and final filled products for sterile, liquid drug applications. The viral developments are based on adenovirus. The production portfolio covers in the first place two bulk and two final products, which are known as Product 1 and Product 2.

9.2.2 Client

The client for the GMPX project is Company X.

9.2.3 Project History

A basic design was earlier developed for a traditional non-SUS approach.

The building for GMPX is already constructed alongside building T4, and all basic utility installations are available there.

9.2.4 Project Scope

The overall purpose of the project is:

  • To design and equip a new manufacturing suite, to be integrated into the T4 complex, for manufacture of injectable products for viral particle gene therapy with disposable technology
  • To finalize OQ for the manufacturing suite within 18 months from start of basic design within agreed project budget

9.2.5 Project Objectives, Success Criteria, and Focus Areas

(Refer to the original document for the detailed table of objectives, success criteria, and focus areas.)

9.2.6 Steering Committee

The SEC and Company X will implement a common steering committee for the project. The purpose and responsibilities of the steering committee are to:

  • Assure that the project goals are met
  • Create a common picture of questions, problems, and limitations within each organization
  • Create a common picture of roles and responsibilities between parties
  • Create a common picture of how project risks should be handled
  • Approve project execution plan, schedules, economy, and planning
  • Supervise project progress
  • Approve monthly project reporting

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Gene Therapy (基因治療) 與 SUS 的關聯：此範例非常典型地展示了為什麼 SUS 特別適合基因治療產品。病毒載體 (Viral Vector) 製造涉及活病毒操作，需要高生物安全等級 (BSL) 的環境。使用一次性系統可以大幅降低交叉污染風險，並簡化清潔驗證的複雜度。

Steering Committee (指導委員會)：由 SEC 與業主共同組成的最高決策機構，負責監督專案進度、審批計畫變更、管控預算與時程。

比喻說明 Analogy

把這個專案想像成「從傳統瓷器餐廳改造成使用免洗餐具的外送廚房」。Company X 原本規劃了傳統不鏽鋼 (non-SUS) 的產線，但後來決定改用一次性技術。建築已經蓋好了（就像廚房空間已經有了），現在要做的是把裡面的設備全部用一次性系統來重新設計和安裝。

重點提示 Key Notes

請特別注意專案時程目標：從 Basic Design 開始到 OQ 完成，僅有 18 個月。這在傳統不鏽鋼產線幾乎不可能達成，但 SUS 因為省去了大量管路安裝、焊接檢查與 CIP/SIP 驗證，大幅縮短了建廠時程。這正是 SUS 的核心商業優勢之一。

Steering Committee 的設置也值得學習：它確保了 SEC 與業主之間有結構化的溝通管道，避免因資訊不對稱而導致的專案延誤或品質問題。

實務應用 Practical Application

作為 CDMO，如果你要為客戶建置一條基因治療的 SUS 產線，這份 PEP 範例提供了非常好的結構參考。你可以直接套用其範圍定義、組織架構和品質策略的框架，再根據自身需求調整細節。特別是 Steering Committee 的設計，在 CDMO 與 Sponsor 之間的協作中尤為重要。

9.3 Contract Documents

9.3 Contract Documents

Basic Design:

  • Contract document
  • Project scope
  • Project organization
  • Reference group

Detailed Design and Execution:

  • Contract document
  • Project proposal
  • Project contents (basic design report)
  • Project UR
  • Project methodology
  • Process module diagram
  • Layouts for floors 0 and 2 with BSL and GMP classification
  • List of equipment and materials
  • Impact assessment GMP
  • Permits to be submitted
  • Main project time schedule
  • Definition of milestones
  • List of man-hours and travel time
  • Procurement strategy
  • Project organization
  • Manuals and training documents
  • Definitions of GMP and GEP

9.3.1 Customer X Deliverables

Customer X is responsible for providing:

  • Drawings of existing building
  • Information on available utilities and other information in existing building
  • Process know-how and product requirements and specifications
  • User Participation
  • Reviewer and approver of documents

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Contract Documents (合約文件)：這裡區分了 Basic Design（基本設計）和 Detailed Design and Execution（細部設計與執行）兩個階段的合約文件。這種分階段簽約的方式在大型製藥工程中很常見，可以降低業主的風險。

User Requirement / UR (使用者需求)：由業主提供的需求規格書，是整個設計的基礎。在 SUS 專案中，UR 需要特別涵蓋一次性組件的材質相容性、萃取物/浸出物規格等特殊要求。

比喻說明 Analogy

合約文件就像婚前協議書：在專案「結婚」之前，雙方必須清楚約定各自的責任、交付物和權利義務。Basic Design 階段的合約就像「訂婚」，先確認大方向；Detailed Design 階段的合約則是「正式結婚」，把所有細節都寫清楚。

重點提示 Key Notes

注意 Customer X 的交付責任中包括「Process know-how and product requirements」。這在 SUS 專案中特別重要，因為一次性組件的選擇（如袋材、管路材質）必須基於製程需求和產品特性。業主如果無法及時提供這些資訊，將直接影響 SEC 的設計工作。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼要將合約文件分成 Basic Design 和 Detailed Design 兩個階段？這對專案風險管理有什麼好處？
  2. 如果業主延遲提供製程知識 (Process Know-how)，對 SUS 專案會造成哪些連鎖影響？

9.4 Scope

9.4.1 Objectives of the Scope

The GMPX project activities such as value engineering and thorough schedule control of all design, construction, commissioning and qualification (C&Q), and changes will have a high importance throughout the project.

9.4.2 Scope Supervision

The scope and progress will be supervised by the steering committee. Changes in the scope will be handled by change orders as described in Section 4.6.

9.4.3 Scope of Engineering

All engineering required to supply and build the process building is within the scope of the SEC. The scope comprises design development of the technical documents prepared during basic design to a detailed design status (i.e., the status required for manufacturing, installation, commissioning, operation, and maintenance of the facility), with all the installed equipment.

The basic design documents have been reviewed and approved by Company X and constitute the project baseline, setting the specific requirements for the project. Any changes from this baseline are to be taken up through the change management procedure.

Reference documents (including client inputs) used during basic design become backup documents. In case of contradiction between requirements specified in the basic design documents and requirements specified in any of the reference documents, then the latter shall take precedence, unless such requirement is superseded by a subsequent change management.

During detailed design the information set by the basic design package is used to develop construction documentation.

9.4.3.1 Design Steps Overview

The SEC will provide a complete design of the new manufacturing suite in the following steps:

  • Front-end definition
  • Basic design
  • Detailed design

9.4.3.2 Basic Design

The SEC will prepare:

  • Project proposal with executive summary project contents
  • Project plan
  • Biosafety level impact assessment

9.4.3.3 Detailed Design

The SEC will provide engineering with:

  • Approved and signed piping and instrumentation diagrams
  • Approved building layout
  • Approved main documents such as UR, PEP, and QAP

9.4.4 Scope of Equipment and Systems

9.4.4.1 General

The scope includes all architectural considerations for cleanroom and mechanical spaces (with exception of the outer building walls) and finishes, building installations for HVAC, utility piping, safety, process piping, process equipment, electrical, and automation.

9.4.4.2 Spare Parts

The SEC will provide spare parts required for commissioning, testing, and qualification.

The SEC will also provide critical spare parts for two years from installation date.

9.4.4.3 Consumables

The SEC will supply the consumables, such as filters, gaskets, lubricant, lamps and lights, fluorescents, and bags, that are required until end of commissioning. Subsequent consumables shall be provided by Company X.

9.4.4.4 Disposables

Disposable bags for cell expansion will be supplied by the SEC based on the UR for the bags in a limited amount only if necessary for IQ and OQ purposes.

9.4.4.5 Utilities

The running cost for utilities during construction and commissioning and qualification (C&Q) will be accounted directly to Company X. All temporary utilities needed only during construction and C&Q will be supported by the project.

9.4.5 Change Management

Management of project change is essential to successful project execution. The project will implement a change management process that will provide for timely identification of deviations or changes in project scope.

All change orders shall be recorded in a change-order log.

See QAP for change control of documents and C&Q activities.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Value Engineering (價值工程)：在不降低功能和品質的前提下，尋找降低成本的替代方案。在 SUS 專案中，這可能包括評估不同供應商的一次性組件、優化管路配置以減少接頭數量等。

Project Baseline (專案基線)：經過批准的 Basic Design 文件構成專案基線。任何偏離基線的變更都必須走正式的變更管理程序。這是防止 Scope Creep（範圍蔓延）的關鍵機制。

Design Steps（設計步驟）：Front-end Definition → Basic Design → Detailed Design 是標準的三階段設計流程。每個階段的細緻程度逐步增加，也代表著投入的資源和承諾逐步加深。

比喻說明 Analogy

設計三階段就像畫一幅油畫：Front-end Definition 是構圖（確定要畫什麼）、Basic Design 是素描底稿（確定比例和結構）、Detailed Design 是上色完稿（所有細節都到位）。如果底稿畫錯了，上色階段再改就非常昂貴。這就是為什麼 Basic Design 階段的審核和批准如此重要。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 專案中 Disposables 的特殊考量：注意 9.4.4.4 提到一次性袋子「僅在 IQ 和 OQ 必要時提供有限數量」。這是因為一次性組件有保質期限制，如果太早大量採購，可能在 PQ 或正式生產前就過期了。SUS 專案的採購策略必須考慮組件的 shelf life。

文件優先順序原則：當 Basic Design 文件與參考文件產生矛盾時，參考文件優先（除非被後續變更管理所取代）。這個原則確保了業主的原始需求不會被設計過程中的解讀所稀釋。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在 SUS 專案中，Value Engineering 可能帶來哪些具體的成本節約？請舉三個例子。
  2. 為什麼一次性袋子僅在 IQ/OQ 階段才提供有限數量？如果提早大量採購會有什麼風險？
  3. Change Management 為什麼被單獨列為一個章節？在 SUS 專案中，最常見的變更觸發原因是什麼？

9.5 Project Execution Approach

9.5.1 General

As shown in the diagram below, many project activities will overlap. Detailed design, construction and installation, and C&Q will overlap. This figure is schematic and does not apply to the project time frame.

Project Phase Flow (schematic):

DD PHASE → Construction and Installation → Installation Commissioning (Static Part of SAT) → Walk Down → Documented Mechanical Completion → IQ → OQ → ATO, CCC Care Custody and Control → Operational Commissioning (Operational Part of SAT) → Handover Package (All Documents)

SAT — Site Acceptance Test
IQ — Installation Qualification
OQ — Operational Qualification
ATO — Approval to Operate
CCC — Care, Custody, and Control

9.5.2 Detailed Design (DD)

9.5.2.1 General

The SEC's operation department appoints and enrolls projects' design resources as are required by a project's scope and schedule. The request comes from the project manager or project leads by the project manager's approval.

9.5.2.2 Design Disciplines

The SEC splits engineering into the following disciplines for this project:

Architectural

  • Cleanroom

Process technology

  • Upstream (cell culture and virus infection)
  • Downstream (product purification)
  • Fill and finish
  • Packaging (inspection and packaging)
  • Labeling
  • Support (dishwasher, autoclave)

Utilities

  • Black piping
  • HVAC
  • Electrical
  • Clean utilities

Automation

QA is involved during the DD phase to review and watch over GMP requirements as an independent part of the project. See QAP, Doc. No. GMPX-QAP-07-001.

9.5.2.3 Engineering Organization

The project engineering manager leads and directs all engineering activities. The engineering manager is primarily responsible for providing backup to the leads in matters of coordination between the disciplines and/or for each discipline. There is a project design lead appointed for each discipline.

9.5.2.4 Design Execution

Detailed design and construction will be overlapping and partially concurrent activities.

During detailed design, detailed construction and installation drawings, specifications, schematics, test sheets, and other documents will be generated at a pace and content as is required by construction and installation.

The release of construction and installation documents is preceded by a series of reviews and approvals, internal to the SEC as well as together with the client's representatives.

See the QAP and C&Q plan for more details about the review and approval process.

9.5.2.5 Design Documents

Governing design documents will be sent to Company X for review and approval. Such documents are listed in the document progress table.

Detailed design documents that are required for construction and installation only will not be issued to Company X for review and approval unless such issuing is required to obtain building permits.

9.5.2.6 Permits and Authority Approvals

  • Building permit: QVIM June 2007
  • Authority review and approval before any construction activity starts
  • Occupancy permits (if applicable); need to be applied for by Company X

9.5.2.7 As-Built Drawings

Approved documents that need to be as-built have to be identified in a later stage.

These documents will be redlined at the site during construction and C&Q.

Redlined documents can be used as as-built documents for C&Q and handover of the systems. The work will be a joint effort of the SEC, vendors, and, if applicable, Company X.

These documents will thereafter be reissued (CAD) as revisions as-built by the SEC.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Concurrent Engineering (並行工程)：PEP 明確指出 DD、施工和 C&Q 將會重疊進行。這是「快速建廠 (Fast-Track Construction)」的核心策略，透過並行作業來壓縮整體時程。

As-Built Drawings (竣工圖)：施工過程中，實際安裝往往與原始設計有偏差。Redline（紅線標記）就是在現場直接在原圖上標記實際差異，最終由 SEC 正式重新出圖成為 As-Built 版本。

Design Disciplines（設計專業）：將工程拆分成建築、製程技術、公用設施和自動化四大領域，每個領域下再細分。這確保了每個專業都有對應的負責人 (Design Lead)。

比喻說明 Analogy

並行工程就像邊蓋房子邊裝潢：一樓還在砌牆的時候，二樓的設計圖已經在畫了。這種方式可以大幅縮短時程，但要求各團隊之間的溝通協調必須非常緊密，否則「一樓牆壁的管線預留孔」可能跟「二樓的管路設計」對不上。

重點提示 Key Notes

QA 獨立性：注意 9.5.2.2 特別強調 QA 在 DD 階段是以「獨立角色」參與審查 GMP 合規性。這符合 GMP 的基本原則——品質保證功能必須獨立於生產和工程，避免利益衝突。

文件分級審批：並非所有設計文件都需要業主審批。僅「Governing Design Documents」（主要設計文件）才送交業主。純施工用的詳細圖紙由 SEC 內部管控。這是務實的做法，避免業主被大量文件淹沒。

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis

專案階段流程圖清楚顯示了從 DD 到 Handover 的完整生命週期。關鍵里程碑包括：

  • Documented Mechanical Completion（文件化機械完工）：施工完成的正式確認點
  • ATO (Approval to Operate)：批准運轉的關鍵門檻，代表系統已通過 IQ/OQ
  • CCC (Care, Custody, and Control)：系統從 SEC 移交給業主管理的轉折點

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 QA 要在 DD 階段就以獨立角色介入？如果等到 C&Q 階段才介入，可能會發生什麼問題？
  2. Concurrent Engineering 在 SUS 專案中比傳統不鏽鋼專案更容易實施嗎？為什麼？
9.5.3 – 9.5.4 Subcontracting, Procurement & Commissioning

9.5.3 Supervising Engineering Contractor's Subcontracting and Procurement

9.5.3.1 General

The SEC will subcontract and procure material and equipment.

Subcontractors for design, support material, installations, and transports will be appointed by the SEC without prior information to Company X.

9.5.3.2 Subcontract Documents

Such subcontract documents that constitute technical specifications will be presented to Company X insofar as such documents relate to GMP equipment, systems, or components.

9.5.3.3 Equipment Log

Status of purchasing, design, fabrication, testing, and delivery of major equipment will be reported at project meetings.

9.5.3.4 Expediting

9.5.3.4.1 Equipment

During the complete delivery phase from contract to completed handover, the SEC supervises and checks the vendors' work and progress. This is made according to the contract with the specific vendor. A delivery of equipment or system is expedited in the following steps:

  • Follow up milestone achievements according to agreed schedule continuously during design, construction, and testing at the vendor's workshop. This is performed by visiting the vendor and/or following up progress reports from the vendor. If deemed to be required, such follow-up will encompass the vendor's major subcontractors also.
  • Review and approve the vendors' design documents.
  • Perform and report FAT.
  • Perform receiving check of equipment.
  • Supervise and check installation and start-up.
  • Supervise and attend qualification work, and review and approve qualification documentation (if applicable).
  • Check and approve final project documentation.

The monitoring, expediting, and reporting of progress of work is executed by the respective design leads.

9.5.3.5 Material

Purchasing and supply of material other than equipment will be monitored, expedited by the project's purchaser.

9.5.3.6 Subcontractors

All subcontractors for construction and installation activities will be contracted by the SEC on behalf of Company X.

9.5.3.7 Procurement

All purchase orders during detailed design and orders of equipment will be signed by the SEC's project manager and finally approved by Company X and placed in the name of Company X.

This will be described in more details in the procurement strategy and the purchase plan.

9.5.4 Commissioning and Qualification

Execution of C&Q is described in the commissioning and qualification plan GMPX-C&Q-07-001 and in the QAP Doc. no. GMPX-QAP-07-001. The execution can be summarized as follows.

9.5.4.1 Factory Acceptance Test (FAT) and Site Acceptance Test (SAT) for Systems Assessed as Indirect Impact and Direct Impact

Suppliers and contractors of indirect- and direct-impact systems must, if applicable according to SQP during FAT/SAT, demonstrate to the SEC that all requirements, including functions' "as-built" documentation, are fulfilled and available and that the deliverables operate as required. In situations where the supplier or contractor is not in a position to perform FAT/SAT as expected, the SEC, in cooperation with the supplier or contractor, must perform additional tests, possibly as commissioning.

FAT/SAT shall be prepared in a manner that ensures that all C&Q requirements are tested and documented and fulfill the acceptance criteria at the completion of SAT.

When the machine or product has been assembled at the site and adequately connected and run-in tested by the supplier or contractor, the SAT is carried out. This takes place in a way similar to the FAT, according to SEC-approved SAT protocols. For indirect-impact and direct-impact systems, SEC QA should review protocols and test plans in the planning of SAT to ensure that approval of the SAT report is obtainable. The SAT is finished with the SEC and SEC QA approval of the SAT report.

9.5.4.2 Commissioning Indirect-Impact Systems and Direct-Impact Systems

For systems assessed as direct or indirect impact, fulfillment of C-requirements shall be demonstrated through commissioning. The work package owner (WPO) has the responsibility to ensure that commissioning activities are well planned and adequately executed, documented, and reported. The Q-coordinator is responsible for overall coordination and follow-up.

Vendor SAT is part of the commissioning.

9.5.4.3 No-Impact Systems

For systems assessed as having no impact, fulfillment of requirements must be demonstrated and documented according to GEP based on the tradition in the discipline.

The WPO is responsible for planning and executing the commissioning activities for no-impact systems and to ensure that the activities are documented in a way that allows the SEC to illustrate that all requirements are met.

9.5.4.4 Qualification

For systems assessed as direct impact, fulfillment of Q-requirements in relation to installations and operations shall be demonstrated through installation qualification and operational qualification (IQ/OQ). Qualification and especially prerequisites before the qualification can start shall be described in the protocols. IQ and OQ must be carried out according to the approved protocols.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Impact Assessment（影響評估）：系統被分為三類——Direct Impact（直接影響）、Indirect Impact（間接影響）和 No Impact（無影響）。這個分類決定了 C&Q 的深度與嚴格程度：

  • Direct Impact：直接影響產品品質的系統（如生物反應器、充填設備），需要完整的 IQ/OQ
  • Indirect Impact：間接影響的系統（如 HVAC、純水系統），需要 FAT/SAT + Commissioning
  • No Impact：不影響產品品質的系統（如照明），僅需按 GEP 標準進行調試

C-requirements vs Q-requirements：C-requirements 是透過 Commissioning 驗證的工程需求，Q-requirements 是透過正式 Qualification (IQ/OQ) 驗證的 GMP 需求。這種區分是 ASTM E2500 和 ISPE 推薦的基於科學和風險的確效方法。

比喻說明 Analogy

Impact Assessment 就像醫院的感染風險分級：手術室（Direct Impact）需要最嚴格的消毒和監控、病房走廊（Indirect Impact）需要基本的清潔標準、停車場（No Impact）只需一般維護。每個區域的管控強度與其對患者安全的影響成正比。

重點提示 Key Notes

FAT/SAT 的 SUS 特殊性：在 SUS 專案中，FAT 通常在一次性組件供應商的工廠進行，重點驗證組件的品質管控系統和製造一致性；SAT 則在使用者現場驗證組件在實際製程條件下的表現。

採購以業主名義下單：雖然 SEC 負責採購，但訂單以 Company X 的名義下達。這確保了業主對供應商關係的最終控制權，也有利於保修和售後服務的銜接。

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 的 SUS 專案中，Impact Assessment 的結果直接決定了確效工作量和預算。一個常見的錯誤是將太多系統分類為 Direct Impact，導致確效成本膨脹。務實的做法是：嚴格按照系統對產品品質的實際影響來分類，並有科學依據支持分類決定。例如，SUS 的混合袋如果僅用於緩衝液配製，可以考慮分類為 Indirect Impact 而非 Direct Impact。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在一個 SUS 生物反應器系統中，哪些組件屬於 Direct Impact？哪些可能是 Indirect Impact？
  2. 如果供應商無法在工廠進行 FAT，SEC 應該如何處理？這對專案時程有什麼影響？
  3. C-requirements 和 Q-requirements 的區分對確效效率有什麼實際好處？

9.6 Organization

9.6.1 Supervising Engineering Contractor's Roles and Responsibilities

An overview of the SEC's roles and responsibilities is presented in the following table.

RoleDescription
Project Manager and Execution ManagerHas the overall responsibility for the project
Project QAIs responsible for setting up and maintaining quality assurance and quality control procedures and for aligning the supervising engineering contractor's quality routines with Company X and regulatory requirements
ProcurementIs responsible for setting up an overall procurement strategy and making sure that the strategy is implemented
Project Document ControllerIs responsible for setting up and implementing document control procedures within the project
Engineering ManagerIs responsible for ensuring that the overall design of the facility is done in a cost-effective sequence and for physical coordination (e.g., clash control procedures) and also to ensure that partners, suppliers, and the client are incorporated in the design process in an effective way
Construction ManagerHas the overall responsibility to establish and maintain the necessary organization and facilities for the construction taking part at Kuopio, Finland
C&Q ManagerHas the overall responsibility to plan and coordinate testing of the facility
Project leads (Engineering and installation leads)Are responsible for time and quality in their subparts of the project

9.6.2 Company X Organization

For details of the Company X organogram, refer to the Company X organogram in (4286) S9.13 References. Roles and responsibilities between the SEC and Company X are defined in Section 2.6 Steering Committee.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

RACI 式角色定義：雖然此表格沒有使用正式的 RACI 矩陣格式，但它清楚定義了每個角色的主要職責。在實際專案中，建議進一步將這些角色展開成 RACI 矩陣（Responsible 負責、Accountable 當責、Consulted 諮詢、Informed 知會），以避免責任模糊。

Clash Control（衝突檢查）：Engineering Manager 負責「Physical Coordination」和「Clash Control」，這是指確保不同工程專業的設計在空間上不會互相衝突（例如管路穿過結構樑）。在 SUS 設施中，雖然製程管路減少了，但仍需注意 HVAC 管道、電纜架和一次性組件支撐架之間的空間協調。

比喻說明 Analogy

SEC 的組織就像一支足球隊：Project Manager 是總教練（統籌全局）、Engineering Manager 是隊長（協調各位置）、各 Design Leads 是各位置的專項教練（負責前鋒、中場、後衛的訓練）、QA 是裁判（獨立監督規則遵守）、Document Controller 是紀錄員（確保每場比賽的數據都被準確記錄）。

重點提示 Key Notes

注意 C&Q Manager 的職責是「plan and coordinate testing」，而非「execute testing」。這意味著實際的測試執行可能由各 Design Lead 或分包商負責，C&Q Manager 負責的是整體計畫和協調。這種分工在大型專案中很常見，可以避免 C&Q Manager 成為瓶頸。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你是 CDMO 的專案負責人，你會在 SEC 的組織架構中額外增加什麼角色來確保 SUS 專案的特殊需求被滿足？
  2. 為什麼 Project QA 需要同時對齊 SEC 的品質標準和 Company X 的法規要求？這兩者可能有什麼差異？

9.7 Quality

9.7.1 Project Quality Strategy

A validation master plan (VMP) is produced by Company X for the project. This VMP will be used to provide the basis for all validation and quality activities during the lifecycle of the project.

The SEC is responsible for carrying out the commissioning and qualification activities (IQ and OQ) unless otherwise described in the VMP. The subsequent process qualification, cleaning validation, and process validation are carried out by Company X and are not included in this project.

The VMP is the overall document for validation in the project and will be master and basis for qualification of equipment facilities and utilities. A separate VMP will be written for process validation.

The qualifications sequence of CP, IQ, OQ, and PQ activities are described in details in the QAP.

9.7.1.5 Partner/Vendor/Supplier Qualifications

Partners and suppliers describe their "normal" test in the tender documents (for instance, via examples of test plans). If possible, the tests are performed on the GMP level when relevant.

  • Tests must address all requirements.
  • Scope of the test activity is determined in the contract (the partners and suppliers draft QAP).
  • After this, the SEC prepares a draft of IQ and OQ protocol in which test plans from the supplier may be entered, if relevant.
  • The suppliers test planning may be adjusted to achieve maximum synergy.
  • The SEC approves supplier's final QAP.

Time schedule and economy of the project includes a completed IQ and OQ with the SEC as the final step. The validation involves the active participation of the end user and Company X-QA. The scope of this is described in the basic design phase.

9.7.2 Quality Activity Plan (QAP)

The project's QAP manages all quality activities and quality documentation to be prepared. The QAP is made in compliance with the requirements in the VMP.

9.7.3 Document Control

Document control is handled in accordance with the QAP.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

VMP (Validation Master Plan / 驗證主計畫)：VMP 是整個驗證活動的最高層級文件，由業主 (Company X) 負責撰寫。它定義了驗證的範圍、策略、角色分工和接受標準。在此專案中，VMP 涵蓋設備確效 (IQ/OQ)，但製程驗證 (PV) 另立專屬 VMP。

QAP (Quality Activity Plan / 品質活動計畫)：QAP 是 VMP 的執行層級文件，詳細列出每項品質活動、負責人、時程和交付物。可以把 VMP 視為「品質的憲法」，QAP 則是「品質的執行辦法」。

Supplier Qualification Synergy（供應商確效整合）：PEP 提出了一個非常務實的做法：將供應商的標準測試計畫整合到 SEC 的 IQ/OQ 方案中，避免重複測試。這在 SUS 專案中尤其重要，因為一次性組件供應商通常已經有完善的出廠測試程序。

比喻說明 Analogy

VMP、QAP 和 IQ/OQ Protocol 的關係就像法律體系：VMP 是「憲法」（最高指導原則）、QAP 是「法律」（具體規範）、各個 IQ/OQ Protocol 是「作業標準程序」（具體執行步驟）。每一層都必須符合上一層的要求，不能互相矛盾。

重點提示 Key Notes

SUS 專案中清潔驗證的簡化：注意 PEP 提到「cleaning validation」由 Company X 負責且不在此專案範圍內。在 SUS 設施中，由於使用一次性接液面組件，傳統意義上的清潔驗證大幅減少，但仍可能需要針對可重複使用的設備外部和環境進行清潔確效。

確效分工的清晰界定：SEC 負責到 OQ，Company X 從 PQ 開始接手。這個交接點必須非常明確，因為 OQ 的完成品質直接影響 PQ 能否順利進行。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 VMP 由業主撰寫而非 SEC？這對確效策略的制定有什麼影響？
  2. 將供應商測試計畫整合到 IQ/OQ 方案中有什麼好處？可能有什麼風險？
  3. 在 SUS 專案中，清潔驗證的範圍與傳統不鏽鋼設施相比有何不同？

9.8 Risk Management

9.8 Risk Management

There will be a number of risk analyses performed during the project. Their main purpose is to identify risk early and create activities to reduce the risk.

The risk analyses are:

  • BD Project Risk Analysis 1
  • BD BSL and GMP Risk Analysis with Focus on the Layout
  • DD Project Risk Analysis 2
  • DD HSE Risk Analysis on the Execution Phase

9.8.1 Documentation

  • Language and templates — Project language is UK English with the exception of documents used for Finnish craftsmen. The SEC templates are used when adequate.
  • Organizing project data — Data storage must be planned for and organized at the start of the project in order to properly archive the information during project closeout. Proper setup at the start of the project will help make it possible to utilize data efficiently, minimize rework, and ensure complete electronic records retention.
  • Project documentation — In basic design the planned documents are described in the object breakdown structure. The quality managed documents are described in the QAP. The document delivery of the suppliers and partners are described in the tender documents or in the contract of the project.
  • Technical tools and standards — For each skill or profession (construction, architecture, bulk process, utility, etc.) it is necessary to determine and develop tools and standards to ensure continuous engineering of the project parts. The lead engineers manage these tools and standards. Specification tools and standards are being prepared in basic design.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

分階段風險分析：PEP 規劃了四次風險分析，分別在 Basic Design (BD) 和 Detailed Design (DD) 階段進行。這體現了「漸進式風險管理」的原則——隨著設計細節的增加，風險分析的焦點也從宏觀（專案風險、佈局風險）轉向微觀（執行風險、HSE 風險）。

BSL (Biosafety Level / 生物安全等級) Risk Analysis：由於本專案涉及活病毒操作，BSL 風險分析特別重要。它需要評估病毒逃逸風險、人員暴露風險以及環境釋放風險，並確保設施設計能夠有效控制這些風險。

比喻說明 Analogy

分階段風險分析就像飛行員的「檢查清單」：起飛前有一份（BD Risk Analysis）、巡航時有一份（DD Risk Analysis）、準備降落時還有一份（HSE on Execution）。每個階段面對的風險不同，需要不同的檢查重點。不是做一次就夠了，而是在每個關鍵節點重新評估。

重點提示 Key Notes

電子記錄管理的前瞻性：9.8.1 強調在專案開始時就要規劃資料存儲。這在現代 GMP 環境中尤其重要，因為法規要求（如 21 CFR Part 11 和 EU GMP Annex 11）對電子記錄的完整性、可追溯性和長期保存有嚴格要求。專案關閉時如果發現文件缺失或格式不兼容，補救成本將非常高昂。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在 SUS 專案中，哪些風險是傳統不鏽鋼專案不需要考慮的？（提示：供應鏈、組件相容性）
  2. 為什麼要在 Basic Design 階段就進行 BSL 和 GMP 風險分析？如果推遲到 Detailed Design 階段，可能會發生什麼？

9.9 Health, Safety, and Environment

9.9 Health, Safety, and Environment

An initial HSE evaluation has been started. The first version of this plan will be issued and approved before any construction activity starts. This plan will be updated during the construction with new items and activities.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

HSE (Health, Safety, and Environment / 健康、安全與環境)：HSE 計畫是法規強制要求的文件，在施工開始前必須批准。在涉及活病毒操作的 SUS 設施中，HSE 還需要特別考慮生物安全相關的風險，如病毒氣溶膠暴露、廢棄一次性組件的滅活處理等。

重點提示 Key Notes

HSE 計畫也是「活文件」，隨施工進展持續更新。這是因為施工現場的風險會隨著不同工序而變化——早期可能是結構施工風險，後期則可能涉及化學品和生物性物質的處理風險。

9.10 Commissioning and Qualification

9.10 Commissioning and Qualification

When the SEC finds it beneficial, an all-day meeting will be called in order to approve documents and/or carry out reviews. This will be scheduled no less than one week in advance and with duration from one day to several days.

When the SEC finds it beneficial, an all-day commissioning day will be called in order to correct errors and carry through cleanroom documents. This will be arranged no less than one week ahead and with duration from one day to several days.

The SEC is responsible for carrying out or supervising and reporting all qualification activities up to and including OQ.

Company X will participate in the test activities.

Company X provides QA resources during the OQ test period.

Company X is responsible for the calibration and maintenance after OQ.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

C&Q 交接點：此節清楚劃定了 SEC 與 Company X 在確效活動中的分工界線。SEC 的責任止於 OQ 完成；OQ 之後的校正、維護和 PQ 全部由 Company X 接手。這是業界標準的交接模式。

比喻說明 Analogy

這就像買新車的交車流程：經銷商（SEC）負責到把車開到你面前、完成所有檢查（IQ/OQ）；交車之後的保養、加油和日常維護（PQ、校正、維護）就是車主（Company X）的責任了。但交車時雙方都要在場確認車況（Company X 的 QA 資源參與 OQ）。

重點提示 Key Notes

OQ 後的校正與維護責任轉移：這個細節很容易被忽略。Company X 必須在 OQ 完成前就建立起內部的校正和維護能力（包括 SOP、人員培訓和備件庫存），否則在 SEC 撤出後可能出現管理真空期。

9.11 Handover and Operation Support

9.11 Handover and Operation Support

The project is handed over to the customer in three steps: 1) ready to run, 2) handover, and 3) final handover. Final handover is the last part of the project.

The project is handed over to the customer with the participation of the SEC project manager, relevant SEC and/or contract project engineers, and representatives from the customer of his or her own choosing.

If the customer wishes to put the area into use before the handover has taken place, the SEC project manager shall ensure that a physical examination of the area takes place together with the customer or the user and that an agreement on operation and maintenance responsibilities is made.

Prior to final handover, deviation lists will be resolved by a cleanup team.

Warranties from third-party vendors, suppliers, and subcontractors are handed over to Company X.

PQ and PV activities are not part of this project. The SEC recommends the client to plan on a PQ support team. SEC will supply resources for support in PQ/PV phase if Company X so wishes. The SEC resources will work under Company X supervision and management during PQ/PV.

Company X has full responsibility for running and maintaining equipment after handover. This must be carried out without invoking any delays to the project.

Documentation will be handed over in binders and/or electronic copy as specified by Company X at final handover, and direct to Company X document control. Where the SEC has produced or obtained from a supplier an electronic copy, this will be provided with the final documentation.

Optimizing program and parameters is not within the scope of this project. Education and training are to be defined. (See C&Q plan.)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

三階段移交 (Three-Step Handover)：

  • Ready to Run（就緒運轉）：設備已安裝完成、通過 OQ，可以開始運轉
  • Handover（移交）：正式將系統的操作與維護責任從 SEC 轉移給 Company X
  • Final Handover（最終移交）：所有偏差處理完畢、文件齊全、保固轉移，專案正式結束

Deviation Lists / Punch Lists（偏差清單/缺陷清單）：在移交前，會有一份列出所有待解決問題的清單。Cleanup Team 負責在最終移交前逐一解決這些問題。

比喻說明 Analogy

三階段移交就像新房交屋：第一階段「預驗收」（Ready to Run），確認硬體完工；第二階段「交鑰匙」（Handover），你可以開始搬進去住了；第三階段「尾款結清」（Final Handover），所有瑕疵修繕完畢、保固書交接、裝修公司撤場。每一階段都需要雙方簽字確認。

重點提示 Key Notes

PQ/PV 的銜接規劃：PEP 明確指出 PQ/PV 不在此專案範圍內，但 SEC 建議業主提前組建 PQ 支援團隊。這是非常務實的建議——許多專案在 OQ 完成後才發現沒有足夠的內部能力執行 PQ，導致產品上市時間延遲。CDMO 在承接 SUS 專案時，應在 PEP 階段就將 PQ/PV 的人力和資源需求納入規劃。

提前使用的風險管控：如果業主在正式移交前就需要使用設施，PEP 要求進行現場檢查並簽訂操作和維護責任協議。這是為了釐清責任界線，避免在出現問題時產生歸責爭議。

實務應用 Practical Application

對 CDMO 而言，Handover 階段是專案成功與否的關鍵時刻。建議在 PEP 中加入「知識轉移計畫 (Knowledge Transfer Plan)」，確保 SEC 的技術團隊在撤出前將所有操作知識和維護經驗傳授給 CDMO 的運營團隊。尤其是 SUS 專案中一次性組件的安裝技巧、無菌連接操作和故障排除經驗，這些「隱性知識」往往比書面文件更有價值。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼要設計三階段移交而非一次移交？每個階段的關鍵交付物是什麼？
  2. 如果 Final Handover 時仍有未解決的偏差，應該如何處理？能否帶偏差移交？
  3. SEC 在 PQ/PV 階段提供支援時，為什麼要「在 Company X 的監督和管理下」工作？

9.12 Abbreviations

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

此縮寫表是 PEP 的標準組成部分。在實際專案中，建議將縮寫表放在 PEP 的開頭（而非附錄），因為讀者在閱讀過程中需要頻繁查閱。

特別注意以下縮寫在 SUS 專案中的特殊意義：

  • GEP (Good Engineering Practice / 良好工程實務)：適用於 No-Impact 系統的驗證標準
  • BSL (Biosafety Level / 生物安全等級)：在基因治療產品製造中是關鍵設計參數
  • SEC (Supervising Engineering Contractor / 監督工程承包商)：此範例中的核心執行角色

重點提示 Key Notes

GEP 和 GMP 的區分是理解 C&Q 策略的關鍵：GEP 適用於不直接影響產品品質的系統，要求較低但仍需文件化；GMP 適用於直接影響產品品質的系統，要求正式的確效文件和審批流程。在 SUS 專案中，正確區分兩者可以顯著降低確效工作量和成本。

9.13 References

9.13 References

The following reference documents should be read in association with this project execution plan:

  • Level A Time Schedule
  • Project Quality Activity Plan (QAP)
  • Project Validation Master Plan (VMP)
  • Object Breakdown Structure
  • Procurement Strategy
  • Purchase Plan
  • Travel and Costs Principles

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PEP 的配套文件體系：PEP 不是一份孤立的文件，它與多份配套文件共同構成完整的專案管理框架：

  • Level A Time Schedule（主時程表）：專案的最高層級時程，標示關鍵里程碑
  • QAP：品質活動的詳細計畫
  • VMP：驗證策略的最高指導文件
  • Object Breakdown Structure（設備分解結構）：將設施拆解為可管理的單元
  • Procurement Strategy（採購策略）：定義供應商選擇和採購流程

重點提示 Key Notes

在 SUS 專案中，Procurement Strategy 特別重要，因為一次性組件的供應商選擇直接影響製程設計和產品品質。採購策略需要考慮：供應商的法規合規狀態、組件的 E&L (Extractables & Leachables) 數據可用性、供應鏈穩定性（單一供應商風險）以及交貨前置時間。

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • PEP 是 SUS 專案的核心管理文件：它定義了專案範圍、執行策略、組織架構、品質管控和時程規劃，是所有利害關係人的共同依據
  • 活文件特性：PEP 隨專案進展持續更新，每次重大變更需經正式審核與批准程序
  • Impact Assessment 決定 C&Q 深度：Direct Impact 系統需完整 IQ/OQ，Indirect Impact 需 FAT/SAT + Commissioning，No Impact 僅需 GEP 級調試
  • SEC 與業主的分工界線：SEC 負責設計、施工、採購和確效（至 OQ），業主負責 VMP 制定、PQ/PV 執行和後續運維
  • 三階段移交機制：Ready to Run → Handover → Final Handover，確保責任有序轉移、文件完整交接
  • SUS 專案的特殊考量：一次性組件的 shelf life 管理、E&L 數據需求、供應商單一來源風險，以及清潔驗證範圍的簡化
  • 品質文件層級：VMP（憲法）→ QAP（法律）→ IQ/OQ Protocols（SOP），逐級承接且不得矛盾
  • 風險管理貫穿全程：從 BD 到 DD 分階段進行風險分析，涵蓋專案風險、GMP/BSL 風險和 HSE 風險

本章學習目標

  • 理解 Single-Use Systems (一次性使用系統, SUS) 導入時的 Training Plan (培訓計畫) 設計邏輯與範例表格結構
  • 掌握培訓計畫中 跨部門人員配置、內/外部訓練師、時程規劃與簽核流程的要素

  • 辨識各參考文獻的類別（ICH 指引、USP 通則、ISO 標準、ASTM 方法、PDA 技術報告、期刊論文等）及其在 SUS 實務中的應用場景
10.0 Appendix III: Training Requirements Example

Original Text

SUS Implementation Training Plan

The following table presents an example SUS Implementation Training Plan showing the organization and planning elements required when introducing single-use systems into a manufacturing facility.

The training plan matrix captures the following key elements:

  • Training Organization: The name of each training module
  • Provisional Date / Realization Date: Planned vs. actual delivery timeline
  • Department assignments: Personnel across departments (Names 1–20) with check marks indicating who attends which training
  • Training Module details: Module name, INT/EXT (internal vs. external trainer), duration/frequency, and trainer's name

The example training modules include:

Training Module INT/EXT Duration Trainer Target Date Department Key Personnel
Bioreactor Bags: Reception & Storage INT 2 hours John Q1 2015 Warehousing / Production Support Names 2, 7–12
Bioreactor Bags: Preparation & Integration EXT 4 hours Brian Q1 2015 Production Support Names 7–12
Calibration & Qualification EXT 4 hours Dave Q2/Q3 2015 Production Names 13–19
SUS Bioreactor Utilization 1 EXT 4 hours Susan Q1 2015 Production Names 14–19
SUS Bioreactor Utilization 2 EXT 4 hours Alan Q3 2015 Production Support Names 7–12, 14–15
SUS Disposal INT 2 hours Lucy Q2/Q3 2015 Production Support Names 7–15
SUS Integrity & Leak Testing EXT 4 hours James Q1 2015 — —

Approvals (Date/Signature)

  • Manufacturing
  • Quality
  • Qualified Person
  • Human Resources
  • Finance

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

SUS Implementation Training Plan (SUS 導入培訓計畫)：這是一次性使用系統導入時不可或缺的人員準備文件。它不只是「排課表」，而是一份系統性的 能力建構藍圖 (Competency Building Blueprint)，確保所有接觸 SUS 的人員在操作前已具備足夠的知識與技能。

INT vs. EXT (內部 vs. 外部培訓)：

  • INT (Internal)：由公司內部具備資格的培訓師執行，通常用於倉儲接收、廢棄物處理等公司特定流程
  • EXT (External)：由 SUS 供應商或外部專家執行，通常用於設備操作、校驗、完整性測試等需要原廠知識的技術模組

比喻說明 Analogy

想像你的工廠要從傳統不鏽鋼設備轉換到一次性系統，就像一家餐廳從使用瓷碗盤改成使用免洗餐具。雖然看似「更簡單」，但每個環節的操作方式都不同：倉庫人員要學會如何正確儲存塑膠袋（溫濕度管控）、生產人員要學會如何安裝與拆卸、品管人員要學會新的完整性測試方法。如果不經過系統性培訓就直接上線，就像讓沒學過微波爐操作的廚師去使用微波爐一樣危險。

重點提示 Key Notes

培訓計畫的幾個關鍵設計原則：

  • 跨部門覆蓋：從倉儲、生產支援、生產操作到品管，所有接觸 SUS 的人員都需要對應的培訓模組
  • 分階段實施：Q1 先完成基礎操作（接收、安裝、基本使用），Q2/Q3 再進行進階項目（校驗、廢棄物處理）
  • 五方簽核：Manufacturing、Quality、QP、HR、Finance 五個部門簽核，確保培訓計畫獲得跨職能認可
  • Realization Date（實際完成日期）：對比 Provisional Date 可追蹤培訓進度，這在 GMP 稽核時是重要的合規證據

實務應用 Practical Application

在 CDMO 環境中，SUS 培訓計畫的挑戰更大，因為：

  • 不同客戶可能使用不同供應商的 SUS 組件，人員需要多品牌操作能力
  • 人員流動率較高，需要建立可持續的培訓體系而非一次性活動
  • 客戶稽核時經常要求查看培訓記錄，因此文件管理必須嚴謹

建議建立「SUS 培訓矩陣資料庫」，將培訓模組標準化，新人到職時可快速配對所需的培訓課程。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼「Bioreactor Bags: Reception & Storage」使用內部培訓師（INT），而「Preparation & Integration」使用外部培訓師（EXT）？請從知識專業性的角度分析。
  2. Finance 部門為什麼也需要簽核培訓計畫？這與 SUS 的成本管理有什麼關係？
  3. 如果你是 CDMO 的培訓經理，如何設計一個能同時服務多個客戶專案的 SUS 培訓架構？

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

參考文獻架構 (Reference Framework)：TR66 的 122 條參考文獻構成了一次性使用系統的完整知識體系。理解這些文獻的分類與層級，就等於掌握了 SUS 領域的「知識地圖」。

這些文獻可以分為以下幾個層級：

  • 第一層 — 法規框架：ICH 指引（Q6A–Q11）、21 CFR、EMA 指引 → 定義「必須做什麼」
  • 第二層 — 標準與方法：USP 通則、ISO 標準、ASTM 方法 → 定義「如何測試與驗證」
  • 第三層 — 行業指引：PDA TR、BPSA 建議、ISPE 指南 → 定義「最佳實務做法」
  • 第四層 — 技術文獻：期刊論文、會議報告 → 提供「科學依據與案例」

比喻說明 Analogy

想像你在蓋一棟建築物。ICH 指引就像建築法規（告訴你最低安全標準）；USP/ISO/ASTM 就像工程標準與材料規範（告訴你如何測試混凝土強度）；PDA Technical Reports 就像建築師手冊（告訴你最佳設計實務）；而期刊論文就像工程案例研究（告訴你別人蓋過的樓有什麼經驗教訓）。你不會只看其中一層就動工，而是需要全面理解後才能做出正確的設計決策。

重點提示 Key Notes — 各類別參考文獻的關鍵應用

ICH Q8–Q11 系列：這是 SUS 導入的品質管理哲學基礎。Q8 的 Quality by Design (QbD) 概念指導你如何系統性地評估 SUS 對產品品質的影響；Q9 的 Quality Risk Management (QRM) 框架是 SUS 風險評估的方法論基礎；Q10 的 Pharmaceutical Quality System (PQS) 確保 SUS 變更管理有完整的品質系統支撐。

USP <87>/<88> 生物反應性測試：這是評估 SUS 材料生物相容性 (Biocompatibility) 的關鍵藥典方法。<87> 為體外試驗（細胞毒性），<88> 為體內試驗（動物植入）。在 SUS 材料選擇階段，這些測試是判斷材料是否適合與藥品接觸的第一道關卡。

Extractables & Leachables (E&L) 文獻群：TR66 引用了大量 E&L 相關文獻（Refs 27–31, 36, 38–46, 96–102），反映出 E&L 是 SUS 導入中最具技術挑戰性的領域。這些文獻涵蓋了從分析方法、安全閾值到風險評估策略的完整知識鏈。

重點提示 Key Notes — 經濟與環境評估文獻

TR66 專門引用了多篇 SUS 經濟性分析文獻（Refs 53, 58–63），這在技術報告中相當少見，反映出 PDA 認知到 SUS 的導入決策不純粹是技術問題，而是需要 Total Cost of Ownership (TCO, 總擁有成本) 的全面評估。

同時，環境影響文獻（Refs 64–70, 82）也被大量引用，顯示 SUS 的「一次性」本質所帶來的廢棄物管理挑戰已成為行業關注焦點。CDMO 在向客戶提案時，需要能夠同時回答經濟效益與環境責任兩個面向的問題。

文獻統計分析 Reference Statistics

將 122 條參考文獻依類別統計：

類別數量佔比
ICH 指引75.7%
PDA 技術報告64.9%
ISO 標準54.1%
USP 通則75.7%
其他藥典 (EP/JP/WHO)32.5%
ASTM 標準54.1%
美國聯邦法規 (CFR)32.5%
FDA/EMA 指引64.9%
E&L 專題文獻1915.6%
SUS 導入/經濟/環境2419.7%
品質/供應鏈/驗證2520.5%
廢棄物/生物安全54.1%
其他/工具75.7%

可以看出，SUS 導入實務與經濟評估（19.7%）以及品質/供應鏈/驗證（20.5%）佔比最高，反映 TR66 的核心關注在於「如何實際落地 SUS」而非純粹的技術規格討論。

實務應用 Practical Application

如何在 CDMO 中活用這份參考文獻清單：

  • 供應商評估時：要求供應商提供符合 USP <87>/<88>、ISO 10993 的生物相容性測試報告，以及符合 BPSA 建議的 E&L 數據包
  • 變更管理時：使用 ICH Q9 的 QRM 框架進行風險評估，參考 PDA TR54 的實務案例
  • 客戶提案時：引用 Refs 59–63 的經濟分析方法進行 TCO 比較，引用 Refs 64、68、82 回應環境影響問題
  • 法規申報時：確保 SUS 相關的 CMC 文件引用了正確的 ICH、USP、ISO 標準

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 TR66 的參考文獻中，Extractables & Leachables 相關文獻佔比如此高（15.6%）？這反映了 SUS 領域的什麼技術挑戰？
  2. ICH Q8 (QbD)、Q9 (QRM)、Q10 (PQS) 三者如何在 SUS 導入的不同階段發揮作用？請舉例說明。
  3. 如果你要建立一個 SUS 知識庫，你會如何將這 122 條文獻按優先順序分級？哪些是「必讀」、哪些是「參考」？
  4. 比較 USP <87>（體外）和 <88>（體內）生物反應性測試，在 SUS 材料評估中各自扮演什麼角色？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 培訓計畫（Appendix III）：SUS 導入需要系統性的培訓計畫，涵蓋倉儲、生產支援、生產操作等跨部門人員。培訓模組應區分內部（INT）與外部（EXT）訓練師，並按時程分階段實施（基礎操作 → 進階校驗 → 專項技能）。五方簽核（Manufacturing、Quality、QP、HR、Finance）確保計畫獲得全面認可。
  • 參考文獻體系：TR66 的 122 條參考文獻構成四個層級的知識體系：法規框架（ICH）→ 標準與方法（USP/ISO/ASTM）→ 行業指引（PDA/BPSA/ISPE）→ 技術文獻（期刊/會議）。每個層級回答不同的問題：「必須做什麼」→「如何測試驗證」→「最佳實務」→「科學依據」。
  • E&L 是核心挑戰：Extractables & Leachables 相關文獻在整體參考文獻中佔比高達 15.6%，反映出 SUS 材料與產品接觸時的化學相互作用是最具技術深度的議題，需要從分析方法、安全閾值到風險評估進行全面管理。
  • 經濟與環境並重：TR66 大量引用 SUS 經濟性分析與環境影響評估文獻，強調 SUS 導入決策必須同時考量 Total Cost of Ownership 與廢棄物管理兩個維度，而非僅看初始採購成本。
  • CDMO 實務價值：這份參考文獻清單是 CDMO 建立 SUS 知識庫的最佳起點。善用分類索引，可快速找到供應商評估、變更管理、客戶提案、法規申報等不同場景所需的權威依據。
